OBJECT Table 39 Purchase Line
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=03/07/25;
    Time=12:46:42 AM;
    Modified=Yes;
    Version List=NAVW1.x,N.7.2.1, WBL-006,WBL009,AP001856;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    OnInsert=VAR
               PresentRecRefL@1109400001 : RecordRef;
               PreviousRecRefL@1109400000 : RecordRef;
               TypeL@1109400002 : ',Insert,Modify,Rename';
             BEGIN
               // Start PA032225
               IF ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnInsert,ExitPointSetupG.Type::Pre,'') THEN
                 EXIT;
               // Stop PA032225
               // Start PA036842
               StatusCheckFunction(FALSE);
               // Stop PA036842

               // Start PA033019
               CheckUserRights(ModificationTypeG::Insert);
               // Stop PA033019
               LOCKTABLE;
               PurchHeader.GET("Document Type","Document No.");
               PurchHeader.CheckChangePermision();
               // Start WBL-009
               PurchHeader.TESTFIELD("Purchaser Code");
               // Stop WBL-009
               PurchHeader."No." := '';
               // Start INC
               PurchLine2.RESET;
               PurchLine2.SETCURRENTKEY("Document Type","Document No.","Line No.");
               PurchLine2.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
               PurchLine2.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
               PurchLine2.SETFILTER("Line No.",'<>%1',"Line No.");
               PurchLine2.SETFILTER("Order Type",'<>%1',PurchHeader."Order Type");
               IF PurchLine2.FINDFIRST THEN
                 PurchLine2.DELETEALL;
               "Order Type" := PurchHeader."Order Type";
               IF ("Order Type" = "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases") AND (Type <> Type::"Charge (Item)") THEN
               // Stop INC
                 "Vehicle Direct Unit Cost Date" := PurchHeader."Vehicle Direct Unit Cost Date";

               "Vendor Order No." := PurchHeader."Vendor Order No.";
               CheckExclusiveDiffTax();
               IF ("Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle) AND ("No." <> '') THEN BEGIN
                 VALIDATE(Quantity,1);
                 VehicleUnitG.MakePurchOptionLines(Rec);
                 VehicleUnitG.MakePurchVehicleLines(Rec);
                 IF VIN <> '' THEN
                   GetOptionPrice();
               END;

               CheckBelongingLines();
               // Start PA036296.29245
               // Stop PA036296.29245

               IF "Item Type" = "Item Type"::"Veh. Transfer" THEN BEGIN
                 VehicleStatusInvPostGrpG.SETRANGE(Code,"Posting Group");
                 VehicleStatusInvPostGrpG.SETRANGE("Vehicle Status","Vehicle Status"-1);
                 VehicleStatusInvPostGrpG.SETRANGE("Location Code","Location Code");
                 IF VehicleStatusInvPostGrpG.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                   VehicleStatusInvPostGrpG.TESTFIELD("Inventory Posting Group");
                   "Posting Group" := VehicleStatusInvPostGrpG."Inventory Posting Group";
                 END;
               END;

               IF "Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle THEN BEGIN
                 PresentRecRefL.GETTABLE(Rec);
                 PreviousRecRefL.GETTABLE(xRec);
                 TypeL := TypeL::Insert;
                 VINFunctionsG.CheckDuplicates(PreviousRecRefL,PresentRecRefL,Rec."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code",TypeL);
                 PresentRecRefL.SETTABLE(Rec);
               END;
               // Start PA032473
               // Start PA035597
               InsertAssociatedSalesLine();
               // Stop PA035597
               // Start PA032473
               IF ("Item Type" = "Item Type"::Item) AND ("No." <> '') THEN
                 FillDocCampLines;
               // Stop INC
               // Start PA034482
               IF "Item Type" = "Item Type"::"Charge (Item)" THEN BEGIN
               // Start EU.0005642
                 UpdatePurchaseLineGlobalDim(Rec, FALSE);
               // Stop EU.0005642
               // Start PA035597
                 UpdateDimSetID();
               // Stop PA035597
               END;
               // Stop PA034482
               // Start PA033985.19040
               // Stop PA033985.19040

               // Start PA042846
               IF PurchHeader."Document Type" IN [PurchHeader."Document Type"::Order, PurchHeader."Document Type"::Invoice] THEN
                 IF PurchHeader."Trade-In for Order No."<>'' THEN BEGIN
                   IF "From Sales Document No." <> PurchHeader."Trade-In for Order No." THEN
                     ERROR(C_INC_TradeInVehicle);
                 END;
               // Stop PA042846

               // Start PA032225
               ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnInsert,ExitPointSetupG.Type::Post,'');
               // Stop PA032225
             END;

    OnModify=VAR
               PresentRecRefL@1109400002 : RecordRef;
               PreviousRecRefL@1109400001 : RecordRef;
               TypeL@1109400000 : ',Insert,Modify,Rename';
             BEGIN
               // Start PA032225
               IF ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnModify,ExitPointSetupG.Type::Pre,'') THEN
                 EXIT;
               // Stop PA032225
               // Start PA036842
               StatusCheckFunction(FALSE);
               // Stop PA036842

               // Start PA033019
               CheckUserRights(ModificationTypeG::Modify);
               // Stop PA033019
               // Start INC
               TableTriggerG := TableTriggerG::Modify;
               IF ("Cockpit Entry No." <> 0) AND NOT ImportCostUpdateG THEN BEGIN
               // Stop INC
                 IF CockpitHdrG.GET("Cockpit Entry No.") THEN
               // Start PA041662.73195
               // Start PA043935
                   IF ((CockpitHdrG."Document Type" >= CockpitHdrG."Orig. Document Type") OR (CockpitHdrG."Orig. Document Type" = CockpitHdrG."Orig. Document Type"::"Purch. Return Order")) AND
               // Stop PA043935
                      (PurchHeader."Transfer Method" > PurchHeader."Transfer Method"::" ") AND
               // Stop PA041662.73195
                      (CockpitHdrG."Processing Status" < CockpitHdrG."Processing Status"::Closed) AND
               // Start PA043935.99714
                      (CurrFieldNo <> 0) AND
               // Stop PA043935.99714
                      ("Order Type" <> "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases")
                   THEN
                     ERROR(C_INC066);
               END;
               IF ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Blanket Order") AND ((Type <> xRec.Type) OR ("No." <> xRec."No.")) THEN BEGIN
                 PurchLine2.RESET;
                 PurchLine2.SETCURRENTKEY("Document Type","Blanket Order No.","Blanket Order Line No.");
                 PurchLine2.SETRANGE("Blanket Order No.","Document No.");
                 PurchLine2.SETRANGE("Blanket Order Line No.","Line No.");
                 IF PurchLine2.FINDSET THEN
                   REPEAT
                     PurchLine2.TESTFIELD(Type,Type);
                     PurchLine2.TESTFIELD("No.","No.");
                   UNTIL PurchLine2.NEXT = 0;
               END;
               // Start INC
               IF "Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle THEN
                 IF ("VAT %" <> xRec."VAT %") OR ("VAT Calculation Type" <> xRec."VAT Calculation Type") THEN BEGIN
                   OptionVariantG.RESET;
                   OptionVariantG.SETRANGE(Area,OptionVariantG.Area::Purchase);
                   OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
                   OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
                   OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document Line No.","Line No.");
                   OptionVariantG.SetVat(OptionVariantG, "VAT %", "VAT Calculation Type");
                 END;
               // Start PA044975
               IF "Process Type" = "Process Type"::Manually THEN
                 ReservEngineMgt.PurchLineVerifyChange(Rec);
               // Stop PA044975
               // Start EU.0114873.115555
               FindStatus(FALSE);
               // Stop EU.0114873.115555
               CheckBelongingLines();
               InsertAssociatedSalesLine();
               // Start PA036296.29245
               // Stop PA036296.29245
               IF "Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle THEN BEGIN
                 PresentRecRefL.GETTABLE(Rec);
                 PreviousRecRefL.GETTABLE(xRec);
                 TypeL := TypeL::Modify;
                 VINFunctionsG.CheckDuplicates(PreviousRecRefL,PresentRecRefL,Rec."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code",TypeL);
                 PresentRecRefL.SETTABLE(Rec);
               // Start PA033985.18827
                 SalesIncentiveMgmtG.UpdateSalIncLineWithVIN(Rec);
               // Stop PA033985.18827
               END;
               CheckImportCostUpdate();
               // Start PA033985.19040
               // Stop PA033985.19040
               // Stop INC

               // Start PA032225
               ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnModify,ExitPointSetupG.Type::Post,'');
               // Stop PA032225
             END;

    OnDelete=VAR
               PurchCommentLine@1001 : Record 43;
               SourceOfDemandL@1119432000 : Record 5028739;
               SalesTradeInL@1109400000 : Record 5025442;
               PostedSalesTradeInL@1109400001 : Record 5025443;
               PurchHdrL@1109400002 : Record 38;
               PurchLineL@1109400003 : Record 39;
               TechDataValueL@1109400004 : Record 5205856;
               PurchInvoiceLineL@11161000 : Record 123;
             BEGIN
               // Start PA032225
               IF ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnDelete,ExitPointSetupG.Type::Pre,'') THEN
                 EXIT;
               // Stop PA032225
               // Start PA036842
               StatusCheckFunction(FALSE);
               // Stop PA036842

               // Start PA033019
               CheckUserRights(ModificationTypeG::Delete);
               // Stop PA033019
               // Start INC
               IF "Receipt No." = '' THEN
                 TESTFIELD("Qty. Rcd. Not Invoiced",0);
               IF "Return Shipment No." = '' THEN
                 TESTFIELD("Return Qty. Shipped Not Invd.",0);
               // Stop INC

               TESTFIELD("Reserved Qty. (Base)",0);
               // Start PA033011
               IF "Trade-In for VIN" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                 SalesTradeInL.RESET;
                 SalesTradeInL.SETRANGE("Document Type",SalesTradeInL."Document Type"::Order);
                 // Start PA041187.89536
                 SalesTradeInL.SETRANGE("Purch. Invoice No.","Document No.");
                 SalesTradeInL.SETRANGE(VIN,VIN);
                 SalesTradeInL.SETRANGE("Purch. Invoice Line No.","Line No.");
                 // Stop PA041187.87656
                 IF SalesTradeInL.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
               // Start PA038476
                   SalesTradeInL.VALIDATE("Purch. Invoice No.",'');
                   SalesTradeInL.VALIDATE("Purch. Invoice Line No.",0);
               // Stop PA038476
                   SalesTradeInL.VALIDATE(Assigned,FALSE);
                   SalesTradeInL.MODIFY;
                 END;
               // Start PA038476
                 PostedSalesTradeInL.RESET;
                 // Start PA041187.89536
                 PostedSalesTradeInL.SETRANGE("Purch. Invoice No.","Document No.");
                 PostedSalesTradeInL.SETRANGE(VIN,VIN);
                 PostedSalesTradeInL.SETRANGE("Purch. Invoice Line No.","Line No.");
                 // Stop PA041187.87656
                 IF PostedSalesTradeInL.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                   PostedSalesTradeInL.VALIDATE("Purch. Invoice No.",'');
                   PostedSalesTradeInL.VALIDATE("Purch. Invoice Line No.",0);
                   PostedSalesTradeInL.MODIFY;
                 END;
               // Stop PA038476
               END;
               // Stop PA033011
               // Start INC
               CheckDealerVehicleReqStatus;
               IF IsImporter THEN BEGIN
                 CheckImportCostDelete;
                 CheckVehicleStocklistDelete;
               END;
               // Stop INC
               CheckChangePermision();
               // Start PA032071
               // Stop PA032071
               IF "Sales Order Line No." <> 0 THEN BEGIN
                 LOCKTABLE;
                 SalesOrderLine.LOCKTABLE;
                 SalesOrderLine.GET(SalesOrderLine."Document Type"::Order,"Sales Order No.","Sales Order Line No.");
                 SalesOrderLine."Purchase Order No." := '';
                 SalesOrderLine."Purch. Order Line No." := 0;
                 SalesOrderLine.MODIFY;
               END;
               CheckAttachedToServiceOrder('');
               LinkedSalLineG.SETCURRENTKEY("From Purch. Document Type","From Purch. Document No.");
               LinkedSalLineG.SETRANGE("From Purch. Document Type","Document Type");
               LinkedSalLineG.SETRANGE("From Purch. Document No.","Document No.");
               LinkedSalLineG.SETRANGE("From Purch. Line No.","Line No.");
               IF LinkedSalLineG.COUNT = 1 THEN BEGIN
                 LinkedSalLineG.FINDFIRST;
               // Start PA033984
                 IF DeleteQuietFlagG OR CONFIRM(C_INC031,FALSE, "Item Type", LinkedSalLineG."Document Type",
                    LinkedSalLineG."Document No.", LinkedSalLineG."Line No.")
               // Stop PA033984
                 THEN BEGIN
               // Start EU.0101759.101909
                   LinkedSalLineG.SetSkipPurchLineUpdate(TRUE);
               // Stop EU.0101759.101909
                   LinkedSalLineG.DissolvePurchRelation();
               // Start INC
               // Start PA043942
                   LinkedSalLineG.GET(LinkedSalLineG."Document Type", LinkedSalLineG."Document No.", LinkedSalLineG."Line No.");
               // Stop PA043942
                   LinkedSalLineG.MODIFY(TRUE);
                 END ELSE
                   ERROR(C_INC032);
               END ELSE
                 IF LinkedSalLineG.COUNT > 1 THEN BEGIN
                   IF DeleteQuietFlagG OR CONFIRM(C_INC033,FALSE) THEN BEGIN
                     IF LinkedSalLineG.FINDSET THEN
                       REPEAT
                         LinkedSalLine2G := LinkedSalLineG;
                         LinkedSalLine2G."From Purch. Document Type" := 0;
                         LinkedSalLine2G."From Purch. Document No." := '';
                         LinkedSalLine2G."From Purch. Line No." := 0;
                         LinkedSalLine2G.MODIFY;
                       UNTIL LinkedSalLineG.NEXT = 0;
                   END ELSE
                     ERROR(C_INC032);
                 END;
               AssociatedServHdrG.RESET;
               AssociatedServHdrG.SETCURRENTKEY("Purch. Document Type", "Purch. Document No.", "Purch. Document Line No.");
               AssociatedServHdrG.SETRANGE("Purch. Document Type","Document Type");
               AssociatedServHdrG.SETRANGE("Purch. Document No.","Document No.");
               AssociatedServHdrG.SETRANGE("Purch. Document Line No.","Line No.");
               IF AssociatedServHdrG.FINDSET THEN
                 REPEAT
                   IF CONFIRM(C_INC067,FALSE,"Document Type", "Document No.", "Line No.",
                      AssociatedServHdrG."Purch. Document Type", AssociatedServHdrG."Purch. Document No.",
                      AssociatedServHdrG."Purch. Document Line No.")
                   THEN
                     AssociatedServHdrG.DELETE(TRUE)
                   ELSE BEGIN
                     AssociatedServHdrG."Purch. Document No." := '';
                     AssociatedServHdrG."Purch. Document Line No." := 0;
                     AssociatedServHdrG.MODIFY;
                   END;
                 UNTIL AssociatedServHdrG.NEXT = 0;

               IF "Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Blanket Order" THEN BEGIN
                 PurchLine2.RESET;
                 PurchLine2.SETCURRENTKEY("Document Type","Blanket Order No.","Blanket Order Line No.");
                 PurchLine2.SETRANGE("Blanket Order No.","Document No.");
                 PurchLine2.SETRANGE("Blanket Order Line No.","Line No.");
                 IF PurchLine2.FINDFIRST THEN
                   PurchLine2.TESTFIELD("Blanket Order Line No.",0);
               END;
               PurchLine2.RESET;
               PurchLine2.SETCURRENTKEY("Document Type","Document No.","Line No.");
               PurchLine2.SETRANGE("Document Type",PurchLine2."Document Type"::"Credit Memo");
               PurchLine2.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
               IF PurchLine2.FINDFIRST THEN
                 IF (PurchLine2."No." = '') AND (PurchLine2.VIN = '') AND (PurchLine2.Description <> '') THEN
                   PurchLine2.DELETE;
               IF Type = Type::Item THEN
                 DeleteItemChargeAssgnt("Document Type","Document No.","Line No.");

               IF Type = Type::"Charge (Item)" THEN
                 DeleteChargeChargeAssgnt("Document Type","Document No.","Line No.");
               // Start PA044975
               // Start EU.0010595.12463
               DeleteRelatedLines(NOT DeleteQuietFlagG);
               // Stop EU.0010595.12463
               // Stop PA044975
               OnDeleteDeleteSubTables();
               // Delete related Document Campaign Lines
               DeleteDocCampLines;
               // Stop INC
               // Start PA032450
               IF SourceOfDemandL.SourceOfDemandFind
                  (DATABASE::"Purchase Line",'',0,"Document No.","Line No.",'','',0)
               THEN
                 SourceOfDemandL.DELETEALL(TRUE);
               // Stop PA032450
               PurchCommentLine.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
               PurchCommentLine.SETRANGE("No.","Document No.");
               PurchCommentLine.SETRANGE("Document Line No.","Line No.");
               IF NOT PurchCommentLine.ISEMPTY THEN
                 PurchCommentLine.DELETEALL;
               // Start EU.0111610.113294
               PurchInvoiceLineL.SETRANGE("No.", "No.");
               PurchInvoiceLineL.SETRANGE("Order No.", "Document No.");
               IF PurchInvoiceLineL.ISEMPTY THEN
               // Stop EU.0111610.113294
               // Start PA040667
               // Start PA040070.63485
               CodedPartValG.DeleteCodedValues("Serial No.", "No.");
               // Stop PA040070.63485
               // Stop PA040667

               // Start PA038476
               // If all the lines are deleted, the Trade-in fields should be revalidated
               // Start PA042846
               IF NOT DeletedFromHdrG THEN BEGIN
               // Stop PA042846
                 PurchHdrL.GET("Document Type","Document No.");
                 IF PurchHdrL."Trade-In for Order No." > '' THEN BEGIN
                   PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
                   PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
                   IF PurchLineL.COUNT = 1 THEN BEGIN
                     PurchHdrL.VALIDATE("Trade-In for Order No.",'');
                     PurchHdrL.CheckTradeInInformation();
                     PurchHdrL.MODIFY;
                   END;
                 END;
               END;
               // Stop PA038476
               // Start EU.0114873.115555
               FindStatus(TRUE);
               // Stop EU.0114873.115555
               // Start EU.0020651
               TechDataValueL.DeleteTechnicalData(Rec);
               // Stop EU.0020651

               // Start PA032225
               ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnDelete,ExitPointSetupG.Type::Post,'');
               // Stop PA032225
             END;

    OnRename=BEGIN
               // Start PA033019
               ERROR(Text000,TABLECAPTION);
               // Stop PA033019
             END;

    CaptionML=ENU=Purchase Line;
    PasteIsValid=Yes;

    { 3   ;   ;Document No.        ;Code20        ;TableRelation="Purchase Header".No. WHERE (Document Type=FIELD(Document Type));

    { 4   ;   ;Line No.            ;Integer       ;OnValidate=BEGIN

                                                              END;

                                                   CaptionML=ENU=Line No.;
                                                   Description=PA032795;
                                                   Editable=No }
    { 5   ;   ;Type                ;Option        ;OnValidate=BEGIN
                                                                // Start PA032225
                                                                IF ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnValidate,ExitPointSetupG.Type::Pre,FIELDNAME(Type)) THEN
                                                                  EXIT;
                                                                // Stop PA032225

                                                                // Start PA037059
                                                                CheckChangePermision();
                                                                // Stop PA037059
                                                                StatusCheckFunction(TRUE);
                                                                // Start INC
                                                                // Start PA040667
                                                                CheckCodedPart();
                                                                // Stop PA040667
                                                                CheckImportCostUpdate();
                                                                TESTFIELD("Qty. Rcd. Not Invoiced",0);
                                                                TESTFIELD("Quantity Received",0);
                                                                TESTFIELD("Reserved Qty. (Base)",0);
                                                                TESTFIELD("Receipt No.",'');

                                                                TESTFIELD("Return Qty. Shipped Not Invd.",0);
                                                                TESTFIELD("Return Qty. Shipped",0);
                                                                TESTFIELD("Return Shipment No.",'');
                                                                // Stop INC
                                                                // Start PA033019
                                                                IF PurchLine2.GET("Document Type", "Document No.", "Line No.") THEN
                                                                  CheckUserRights(ModificationTypeG::Modify)
                                                                ELSE
                                                                  CheckUserRights(ModificationTypeG::Insert);
                                                                // Stop PA033019
                                                                CheckAssignedSalLine(FIELDCAPTION(Type));
                                                                IF "Drop Shipment" THEN
                                                                  ERROR(
                                                                    Text001,
                                                                    FIELDCAPTION(Type),"Sales Order No.");

                                                                CheckAttachedToServiceOrder(FIELDCAPTION(Type));
                                                                // Start INC
                                                                IF xRec.Type = xRec.Type::Item THEN
                                                                  DeleteDocCampLines;

                                                                IF Type <> xRec.Type THEN BEGIN
                                                                  IF xRec.Type IN [Type::Item,Type::"Fixed Asset"] THEN
                                                                    DeleteItemChargeAssgnt("Document Type","Document No.","Line No.");
                                                                  IF xRec.Type = Type::"Charge (Item)" THEN
                                                                    DeleteChargeChargeAssgnt("Document Type","Document No.","Line No.");
                                                                END;
                                                                // Stop INC
                                                                TempPurchLine := Rec;
                                                                INIT;
                                                                Type := TempPurchLine.Type;
                                                                // Start INC
                                                                // Start EU.0005642
                                                                UpdatePurchaseLineGlobalDim(TempPurchLine, FALSE);
                                                                // Stop EU.0005642
                                                                "Order Type" := TempPurchLine."Order Type";
                                                                "Location Code" := TempPurchLine."Location Code";
                                                                "Allow Invoice Disc." := TempPurchLine."Allow Invoice Disc.";
                                                                IF ("Order Type" IN ["Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases","Order Type"::Service]) AND (Type = Type::Item) THEN
                                                                  "Item Type" := "Item Type"::Item;
                                                                IF ("Order Type" IN ["Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases","Order Type"::Service]) AND
                                                                   (Type = Type::"Account (G/L)")
                                                                THEN
                                                                  "Item Type" := "Item Type"::"G/L Account";
                                                                IF ("Line No." <> 0) THEN BEGIN
                                                                  OptionVariantG.SETRANGE(Area,OptionVariantG.Area::Purchase);
                                                                  OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
                                                                  OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
                                                                  OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document Line No.","Line No.");
                                                                  IF OptionVariantG.FINDFIRST THEN
                                                                    OptionVariantG.DELETEALL;
                                                                END;
                                                                // Start EU.0005642
                                                                UpdatePurchaseLineGlobalDim(Rec, FALSE);
                                                                // Stop EU.0005642
                                                                // Stop INC
                                                                "System-Created Entry" := TempPurchLine."System-Created Entry";
                                                                VALIDATE("FA Posting Type");

                                                                IF Type = Type::Item THEN
                                                                  "Allow Item Charge Assignment" := TRUE
                                                                ELSE
                                                                  "Allow Item Charge Assignment" := FALSE;
                                                                // Start PA035597
                                                                UpdateDimSetID();
                                                                // Stop PA035597
                                                                // Start PA032225
                                                                ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnValidate,ExitPointSetupG.Type::Post,FIELDNAME(Type));
                                                                // Stop PA032225
                                                              END;

    { 6   ;   ;No.                 ;Code20        ;TableRelation=IF (Type=CONST(" ")) "Standard Text"

                                                                CampMngtL@1109400004 : Codeunit 5045777;

                                                              BEGIN
                                                                // Start PA032225
                                                                IF ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnValidate,ExitPointSetupG.Type::Pre,FIELDNAME("No.")) THEN
                                                                  EXIT;
                                                                // Stop PA032225

                                                                // Start PA033019
                                                                CheckUserRights(ModificationTypeG::Modify);
                                                                // Stop PA033019
                                                                // Start PA040667
                                                                CheckCodedPart();
                                                                // Stop PA040667
                                                                CheckMaster();
                                                                TESTFIELD("Qty. Rcd. Not Invoiced",0);

                                                                TESTFIELD("Reserved Qty. (Base)",0);
                                                                TESTFIELD("Receipt No.",'');
                                                                // Start INC
                                                                TESTFIELD("Return Qty. Shipped Not Invd.",0);
                                                                TESTFIELD("Return Qty. Shipped",0);
                                                                TESTFIELD("Return Shipment No.",'');

                                                                IF "Drop Shipment" THEN
                                                                  ERROR(
                                                                    Text001,
                                                                    FIELDCAPTION("No."),"Sales Order No.");

                                                                CheckChangePermision();
                                                                StatusCheckFunction(TRUE);
                                                                CheckAttachedToServiceOrder(FIELDCAPTION("No."));
                                                                // Start INC
                                                                CheckImportCostUpdate;
                                                                CheckDealerVehicleReqStatus;

    { 15  ;   ;Quantity            ;Decimal       ;OnValidate=VAR
                                                                CodedPartValueL@1109400000 : Record 5205352;

                                                              BEGIN
                                                                // Start PA036544
                                                                IF ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnValidate,ExitPointSetupG.Type::Pre,FIELDNAME(Quantity)) THEN
                                                                  EXIT;
                                                                // Stop PA036544

                                                                  CheckUserRights(ModificationTypeG::Modify);

                                                                END;

                                                                // Start INC
                                                                StatusCheckFunction(TRUE);

                                                                  ERROR(C_INC001);

                                                                // Start EU.0061953
                                                                // Stop EU.0061953

                                                                  ERROR(
                                                                    Text001,
                                                                    FIELDCAPTION(Quantity),"Sales Order No.");
                                                                "Quantity (Base)" := CalcBaseQty(Quantity);

                                                                  IF (Quantity * "Return Qty. Shipped" < 0) OR
                                                                     ((ABS(Quantity) < ABS("Return Qty. Shipped")) AND ("Return Shipment No." = ''))
                                                                  THEN
                                                                    FIELDERROR(Quantity,STRSUBSTNO(Text004,FIELDCAPTION("Return Qty. Shipped")));
                                                                  IF ("Quantity (Base)" * "Return Qty. Shipped (Base)" < 0) OR
                                                                     ((ABS("Quantity (Base)") < ABS("Return Qty. Shipped (Base)")) AND ("Return Shipment No." = ''))
                                                                  THEN
                                                                    FIELDERROR("Quantity (Base)",STRSUBSTNO(Text004,FIELDCAPTION("Return Qty. Shipped (Base)")));
                                                                END ELSE BEGIN
                                                                  IF (Quantity * "Quantity Received" < 0) OR
                                                                     ((ABS(Quantity) < ABS("Quantity Received")) AND ("Receipt No." = ''))
                                                                  THEN
                                                                    FIELDERROR(Quantity,STRSUBSTNO(Text004,FIELDCAPTION("Quantity Received")));
                                                                  IF ("Quantity (Base)" * "Qty. Received (Base)" < 0) OR
                                                                     ((ABS("Quantity (Base)") < ABS("Qty. Received (Base)")) AND ("Receipt No." = ''))
                                                                  THEN
                                                                    FIELDERROR("Quantity (Base)",STRSUBSTNO(Text004,FIELDCAPTION("Qty. Received (Base)")));
                                                                END;
                                                                IF (Type = Type::"Charge (Item)") AND (CurrFieldNo <> 0) THEN BEGIN
                                                                  IF (Quantity * "Qty. Assigned" < 0) OR (ABS(Quantity) < ABS("Qty. Assigned")) THEN
                                                                    FIELDERROR(Quantity,STRSUBSTNO(Text004,FIELDCAPTION("Qty. Assigned")));
                                                                  UpdateItemChargeAssgnt;
                                                                END;

                                                                IF "Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Return Order","Document Type"::"Credit Memo"] THEN
                                                                  InitQtyToShip
                                                                ELSE
                                                                // Stop INC
                                                                  InitQtyToReceive;
                                                                // Start EU.0005636
                                                                // Stop EU.0005636

                                                                "Quantity Disc. %" := 0;
                                                                IF Type = Type::Item THEN BEGIN
                                                                  ItemPurchQtyDisc.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
                                                                  ItemPurchQtyDisc.SETRANGE("Vendor No.","Buy-from Vendor No.");
                                                                  ItemPurchQtyDisc.SETRANGE("Minimum Quantity",0,ABS("Quantity (Base)"));

                                                                      CodedPartValueL.GetCodedPartSetup(RecRefL, FIELDNO("No."), FIELDNO("Coded Part Type"), FIELDNO("Serial No."), CurrFieldNo, VIN)
                                                                    ELSE

                                                                    RecRefL.SETTABLE(Rec);
                                                                // Stop PA040070.63485
                                                                  END;

                                                                    UNTIL DocCampLineG.NEXT = 0;
                                                                END;
                                                                // Stop INC
                                                                // Start PA044975
                                                                UpdateFieldInAttachedLines(FIELDNO(Quantity));
                                                                // Stop PA044975

                                                                      ("Direct Unit Cost" - "Line Discount Amount" / Quantity) * 100,0.00001)

                                                                UpdateServCost;

    { 29  ;   ;Amount              ;Decimal       ;OnValidate=BEGIN

                                                                  ERROR(C_INC058);

                                                                // Start PA036544
                                                                IF NOT ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnValidate,ExitPointSetupG.Type::"Condition 1",FIELDNAME(Amount)) THEN
                                                                // Stop PA036544
                                                                  CASE "VAT Calculation Type" OF
                                                                    "VAT Calculation Type"::"Normal VAT",
                                                                    "VAT Calculation Type"::"Reverse Charge VAT",
                                                                    "VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax":
                                                                      BEGIN
                                                                        "VAT Base Amount" := ROUND(Amount * (1 - PurchHeader."VAT Base Discount %" / 100),0.00001);
                                                                        "Amount Including VAT" := ROUND(Amount + "VAT Base Amount" * "VAT %" / 100,0.00001);
                                                                      END;
                                                                    "VAT Calculation Type"::"Full VAT":
                                                                      IF Amount <> 0 THEN
                                                                        FIELDERROR(Amount,
                                                                          STRSUBSTNO(

                                                                            "VAT Calculation Type"));
                                                                    "VAT Calculation Type"::"Exch. Parts Tax":
                                                                      BEGIN
                                                                        "VAT Base Amount" := ROUND(Amount * (1 - PurchHeader."VAT Base Discount %" / 100),0.00001);
                                                                        "Exch. Parts Tax Base" := "List Price (LCY)" * Quantity;
                                                                        IF PurchHeader."Currency Code" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                                                          PurchHeader.TESTFIELD("Currency Factor");
                                                                          "Exch. Parts Tax Base" := ROUND(CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(
                                                                            GetDate(), "Currency Code", "Exch. Parts Tax Base", PurchHeader."Currency Factor"), 0.00001);
                                                                        END;
                                                                        "Exch. Parts Tax Base" := ROUND("Exch. Parts Tax Base" * "Exch. Parts Tax %" / 100, 0.00001);
                                                                        "Exch. Parts Tax Amount" := ROUND("Exch. Parts Tax Base" * "Exch. Parts VAT %" / 100,0.00001);
                                                                        "Amount Including VAT" := ROUND(Amount + "VAT Base Amount" * "VAT %" /100 +
                                                                          "Exch. Parts Tax Amount",0.00001);
                                                                      END;
                                                                    "VAT Calculation Type"::"Sales Tax":
                                                                      BEGIN
                                                                        PurchHeader.TESTFIELD("VAT Base Discount %",0);
                                                                        "VAT Base Amount" := ROUND(Amount,0.00001);
                                                                        IF "Use Tax" THEN
                                                                          "Amount Including VAT" := ROUND("VAT Base Amount",0.00001)
                                                                        ELSE BEGIN
                                                                // Start PA036544
                                                                          ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnValidate,ExitPointSetupG.Type::"Inside 1",FIELDNAME(Amount));
                                                                // Stop PA036544
                                                                          "Amount Including VAT" :=
                                                                            Amount +
                                                                            SalesTaxCalculate.CalculateTax(
                                                                              "Tax Area Code","Tax Group Code","Tax Liable",PurchHeader."Posting Date",
                                                                              "VAT Base Amount",Quantity,PurchHeader."Currency Factor");
                                                                          IF "VAT Base Amount" <> 0 THEN
                                                                            "VAT %" :=
                                                                              ROUND(100 * ("Amount Including VAT" - "VAT Base Amount") / "VAT Base Amount",0.00001)
                                                                          ELSE BEGIN
                                                                            "VAT %" := 0;
                                                                          END;
                                                                        END;
                                                                      END;
                                                                  END;

                                                                "Inv. Discount Amount" := 0;
                                                                "Line Discount Amount" := ROUND(
                                                                  ROUND(Quantity * "Direct Unit Cost",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision") - Amount,
                                                                  Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
                                                                IF ("Direct Unit Cost" <> 0) AND (Quantity <> 0) THEN
                                                                  "Line Discount %" := ROUND(("Line Discount Amount" / Quantity) / "Direct Unit Cost" * 100,0.00001)
                                                                ELSE
                                                                  "Line Discount %" := 0;

                                                                // Start PA040256.58388
                                                                IF "Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle THEN
                                                                  DiscountOnOptionTable;
                                                                // Stop PA040256.58388

                                                                InitOutstandingAmount;
                                                                UpdateUnitCost;
                                                                // Start INC
                                                                IF (Amount <> xRec.Amount) AND (CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO(Amount)) AND ("Item Type" = "Item Type"::Item) THEN BEGIN
                                                                  "Campaign Discount %" := 0;
                                                                  UpdateDocCampLine;
                                                                END;
                                                                // Stop INC

                                                                // Start PA036544
                                                                ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnValidate,ExitPointSetupG.Type::Post,FIELDNAME(Amount));
                                                                // Stop PA036544
                                                              END;

                                                   CaptionML=ENU=Amount;
                                                   AutoFormatType=1;
                                                   AutoFormatExpr="Currency Code" }
    { 30  ;   ;Amount Including VAT;Decimal       ;OnValidate=BEGIN
                                                                // Start PA036544
                                                                IF ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnValidate,ExitPointSetupG.Type::Pre,FIELDNAME("Amount Including VAT")) THEN
                                                                  EXIT;
                                                                // Stop PA036544
                                                                // Start PA036842
                                                                StatusCheckFunction(TRUE);
                                                                // Stop PA036842

                                                                // Start INC
                                                                IF (CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO("Amount Including VAT")) AND ("Line No." = 0) AND ("Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle) THEN
                                                                  ERROR(C_INC058);
                                                                // Stop INC
                                                                TESTFIELD(Type);
                                                                TESTFIELD(Quantity);
                                                                TESTFIELD("Direct Unit Cost");
                                                                GetPurchHeader;
                                                                "Amount Including VAT" := ROUND("Amount Including VAT",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");

                                                                // Start PA036544
                                                                IF NOT ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnValidate,ExitPointSetupG.Type::"Condition 1",FIELDNAME("Amount Including VAT")) THEN
                                                                // Stop PA036544
                                                                  CASE "VAT Calculation Type" OF
                                                                    "VAT Calculation Type"::"Normal VAT",
                                                                    "VAT Calculation Type"::"Reverse Charge VAT",
                                                                    "VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax":
                                                                      BEGIN
                                                                        Amount :=
                                                                          ROUND(
                                                                            "Amount Including VAT" /
                                                                            (1 + (1 - PurchHeader."VAT Base Discount %" / 100) * "VAT %" / 100),
                                                                            0.00001);
                                                                        "VAT Base Amount" :=
                                                                          ROUND(Amount * (1 - PurchHeader."VAT Base Discount %" / 100),0.00001);
                                                                      END;
                                                                    "VAT Calculation Type"::"Full VAT":
                                                                      BEGIN
                                                                        Amount := 0;
                                                                        "VAT Base Amount" := 0;
                                                                      END;

                                                                    "VAT Calculation Type"::"Exch. Parts Tax":
                                                                      BEGIN
                                                                        Amount :=
                                                                          ROUND(
                                                                            ("Amount Including VAT"-"Exch. Parts Tax Amount") /
                                                                            (1 + (1 - PurchHeader."VAT Base Discount %" / 100) * "VAT %" / 100),0.00001);
                                                                        "VAT Base Amount" := ROUND(Amount * (1 - PurchHeader."VAT Base Discount %" / 100),0.00001);
                                                                      END;

                                                                    "VAT Calculation Type"::"Sales Tax":
                                                                      BEGIN
                                                                        PurchHeader.TESTFIELD("VAT Base Discount %",0);
                                                                        IF "Use Tax" THEN BEGIN
                                                                          Amount := ROUND("Amount Including VAT",0.00001);
                                                                          "VAT Base Amount" := ROUND(Amount,0.00001);
                                                                        END ELSE BEGIN
                                                                          Amount :=
                                                                            ROUND(
                                                                              SalesTaxCalculate.ReverseCalculateTax(
                                                                                "Tax Area Code","Tax Group Code","Tax Liable",PurchHeader."Posting Date",
                                                                                "Amount Including VAT",Quantity,PurchHeader."Currency Factor"),
                                                                              0.00001);
                                                                          "VAT Base Amount" := Amount;
                                                                          IF "VAT Base Amount" <> 0 THEN
                                                                            "VAT %" :=
                                                                              ROUND(100 * ("Amount Including VAT" - "VAT Base Amount") / "VAT Base Amount",0.00001)
                                                                // Start PA036544
                                                                          ELSE BEGIN
                                                                            "VAT %" := 0;
                                                                          END;
                                                                        END;
                                                                      END;
                                                                // Stop PA036544
                                                                  END;

                                                                "Inv. Discount Amount" := 0;
                                                                "Line Discount Amount" :=
                                                                  ROUND(
                                                                    ROUND(Quantity * "Direct Unit Cost",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision") - Amount,
                                                                    Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
                                                                IF ("Direct Unit Cost" <> 0) AND (Quantity <> 0) THEN
                                                                  "Line Discount %" := ROUND(("Line Discount Amount" / Quantity) / "Direct Unit Cost" * 100,0.00001)
                                                                ELSE
                                                                  "Line Discount %" := 0;
                                                                // Start PA040256.58388
                                                                IF "Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle THEN
                                                                  DiscountOnOptionTable;
                                                                // Stop PA040256.58388
                                                                InitOutstandingAmount;
                                                                UpdateUnitCost;
                                                                // Start INC
                                                                IF ("Amount Including VAT" <> xRec."Amount Including VAT") AND (CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO("Amount Including VAT")) AND
                                                                   ("Item Type" = "Item Type"::Item)
                                                                THEN BEGIN
                                                                  "Campaign Discount %" := 0;
                                                                  UpdateDocCampLine;
                                                                END;
                                                                // Stop INC

                                                                // Start PA036544
                                                                ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnValidate,ExitPointSetupG.Type::Post,FIELDNAME("Amount Including VAT"));
                                                                // Stop PA036544
                                                              END;

                                                   CaptionML=ENU=Amount Including VAT;
                                                   AutoFormatType=1;
                                                   AutoFormatExpr="Currency Code" }
    { 31  ;   ;Unit Price (LCY)    ;Decimal       ;OnValidate=BEGIN
                                                                StatusCheckFunction(TRUE);
                                                                IF (CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO("Unit Price (LCY)")) AND ("Line No." = 0) AND ("Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle) THEN
                                                                  ERROR(C_INC058);
                                                                IF "VAT Calculation Type" = "VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax" THEN BEGIN
                                                                  SalPriceVATCalcBaseG := "Unit Price (LCY)" - "Unit Cost (LCY)";
                                                                  IF (SalPriceVATCalcBaseG <= 0) THEN
                                                                    "Unit Price Incl. VAT (LCY)" := "Unit Price (LCY)"
                                                                  ELSE BEGIN
                                                                    IF NOT VATPostingSetup.GET("VAT Bus. Posting Group","VAT Prod. Posting Group") THEN
                                                                      VATPostingSetup.INIT;
                                                                    SalPriceVATPctG := VATPostingSetup."VAT %";
                                                                    "Unit Price Incl. VAT (LCY)" := ROUND("Unit Price (LCY)" + SalPriceVATCalcBaseG * SalPriceVATPctG / 100,0.00001)
                                                                  END;
                                                                END ELSE
                                                                  "Unit Price Incl. VAT (LCY)" := ROUND("Unit Price (LCY)" + "Unit Price (LCY)" * "VAT %" / 100,0.00001);
                                                                SalPriceToOptionTable;
                                                              END;

                                                   CaptionML=ENU=Unit Price (LCY);
                                                   AutoFormatType=2 }
    { 32  ;   ;Allow Invoice Disc. ;Boolean       ;InitValue=Yes;

    { 38  ;   ;Appl.-to Item Entry ;Integer       ;OnValidate=VAR

                                                                // Start EU.0055250

                                                                  IF (("Receipt No." <> '') OR ("Return Shipment No." <> '')) OR

                                                                  THEN

                                                                // Stop EU.0055250

                                                                // Stop PA041662.73195
                                                                // Start EU.0055250
                                                                  IF ItemLedgEntry."Location Code" <> "Location Code"  THEN BEGIN
                                                                // Stop EU.0055250
                                                                    "Location Code" := ItemLedgEntry."Location Code";
                                                                // Start PA036118
                                                                // Start EU.0055250
                                                                // Stop EU.0055250
                                                                // Start PA036549.34230
                                                                    LocationG.PurchaseCrossLocationCheck(FORMAT(Type), PurchHeader."Location Code", "Location Code", "Order Type");
                                                                // Stop PA036549.34230
                                                                    LocationG.PurchaseCrossBranchCheck(PurchHeader, Rec);
                                                                // Start EU.0055250
                                                                  END;
                                                                // Stop EU.0055250
                                                                // Stop PA036118
                                                                END;
                                                                IF VIN <> '' THEN
                                                                  TESTFIELD("Serial No.",VIN);
                                                                // Stop INC
                                                              END;

                                                   OnLookup=BEGIN
                                                              SelectItemEntry(FIELDNO("Appl.-to Item Entry"));
                                                              // Start PA039250
                                                              StatusCheckFunction(FALSE);
                                                              // Stop PA039250
                                                            END;

    { 90  ;   ;VAT Prod. Posting Group;Code10     ;TableRelation="VAT Product Posting Group";
                                                   OnValidate=BEGIN
                                                                // Start PA036544
                                                                IF ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnValidate,ExitPointSetupG.Type::Pre,FIELDNAME("VAT Prod. Posting Group")) THEN
                                                                  EXIT;
                                                                // Stop PA036544
                                                                // Start PA036842
                                                                StatusCheckFunction(TRUE);
                                                                // Stop PA036842

                                                                IF NOT VATPostingSetup.GET("VAT Bus. Posting Group","VAT Prod. Posting Group") THEN
                                                                  VATPostingSetup.INIT;
                                                                "VAT %" := VATPostingSetup."VAT %";
                                                                "VAT Calculation Type" := VATPostingSetup."VAT Calculation Type";
                                                                // Start PA032441
                                                                // Stop PA032441
                                                                "Exch. Parts VAT %" := VATPostingSetup."VAT %";
                                                                // Start PA033042
                                                                "VAT Identifier" := VATPostingSetup."VAT Identifier";
                                                                // Stop PA033042
                                                                CASE "VAT Calculation Type" OF
                                                                  "VAT Calculation Type"::"Reverse Charge VAT",
                                                                    "VAT Calculation Type"::"Sales Tax",
                                                                  "VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax":
                                                                    "VAT %" := 0;
                                                                  "VAT Calculation Type"::"Full VAT":
                                                                    BEGIN
                                                                      TESTFIELD(Type,Type::"Account (G/L)");
                                                                      VATPostingSetup.TESTFIELD("Purchase VAT Account");
                                                                      TESTFIELD("No.",VATPostingSetup."Purchase VAT Account");
                                                                    END;
                                                                END;

                                                                IF Type <> Type::" " THEN
                                                                  UpdateAmounts;
                                                                VALIDATE("Unit Price (LCY)");
                                                                IF ("VAT Calculation Type" <> xRec."VAT Calculation Type") AND ("Line No." <> 0) THEN
                                                                  CheckExclusiveDiffTax;
                                                                IF "VAT Calculation Type" <> xRec."VAT Calculation Type" THEN
                                                                // Start PA040256.58388
                                                                  IF "Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle THEN
                                                                    DiscountOnOptionTable;
                                                                // Stop PA040256.58388
                                                                IF ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::Invoice) AND ("Trade-In for VIN" <> '') THEN BEGIN
                                                                  SalTradeInsG.SETCURRENTKEY("Purch. Invoice No.","Purch. Invoice Line No.");
                                                                  SalTradeInsG.SETRANGE("Purch. Invoice No.","Document No.");
                                                                  SalTradeInsG.SETRANGE("Purch. Invoice Line No.","Line No.");
                                                                  IF SalTradeInsG.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                                                    SalTradeInsG."VAT Prod. Posting Group" := "VAT Prod. Posting Group";
                                                                    IF "VAT Calculation Type" = "VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax" THEN
                                                                      SalTradeInsG."Differential Taxation" := TRUE
                                                                    ELSE
                                                                      SalTradeInsG."Differential Taxation" := FALSE;
                                                                    SalTradeInsG.VALIDATE("VAT %", "VAT %");
                                                                    SalTradeInsG.MODIFY;
                                                                  END;
                                                                END;
                                                                IF ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Credit Memo") AND ("Trade-In for VIN" <> '') THEN BEGIN
                                                                  SalTradeInsG.SETCURRENTKEY("Purch. Cr. Memo No.","Purch. Cr. Memo Line No.");
                                                                  SalTradeInsG.SETRANGE("Purch. Cr. Memo No.","Document No.");
                                                                  SalTradeInsG.SETRANGE("Purch. Cr. Memo Line No.","Line No.");
                                                                  IF SalTradeInsG.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                                                    SalTradeInsG."VAT Prod. Posting Group" := "VAT Prod. Posting Group";
                                                                    IF "VAT Calculation Type" = "VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax" THEN
                                                                      SalTradeInsG."Differential Taxation" := TRUE
                                                                    ELSE
                                                                      SalTradeInsG."Differential Taxation" := FALSE;
                                                                    SalTradeInsG.VALIDATE("VAT %", "VAT %");
                                                                    SalTradeInsG.MODIFY;
                                                                  END;
                                                                END;

                                                                // Start PA036544
                                                                ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnValidate,ExitPointSetupG.Type::Post,FIELDNAME("VAT Prod. Posting Group"));
                                                                // Stop PA036544
                                                              END;

                                                                    ERROR(C_INC019,FIELDCAPTION("Unit of Measure Code"));

                                                                ELSE BEGIN
                                                                  UnitOfMeasure.GET("Unit of Measure Code");
                                                                  "Unit of Measure" := UnitOfMeasure.Description;
                                                                  GetPurchHeader;
                                                                  IF PurchHeader."Language Code" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                                                    UnitOfMeasureTranslation.SETRANGE(Code,"Unit of Measure Code");
                                                                    UnitOfMeasureTranslation.SETRANGE("Language Code",PurchHeader."Language Code");
                                                                    IF UnitOfMeasureTranslation.FINDFIRST THEN
                                                                      "Unit of Measure" := UnitOfMeasureTranslation.Description;
                                                                  END;
                                                                END;
                                                                IF (Type = Type::Item) AND ("No." <> '') THEN BEGIN
                                                                  GetItem;
                                                                  "Qty. per Unit of Measure" := UOMMgt.GetQtyPerUnitOfMeasure(Item,"Unit of Measure Code");
                                                                  "Gross Weight" := Item."Gross Weight" * "Qty. per Unit of Measure";
                                                                  "Net Weight" := Item."Net Weight" * "Qty. per Unit of Measure";
                                                                  "Unit Volume" := Item."Unit Volume" * "Qty. per Unit of Measure";
                                                                  UpdateUOMQtyPerStockQty;
                                                                  FillDocCampLines;
                                                                END ELSE
                                                                  "Qty. per Unit of Measure" := 1;
                                                                VALIDATE(Quantity);
                                                                VALIDATE("Reserved Qty. (Base)");
                                                              END;

                                                   CaptionML=ENU=Unit of Measure Code }

                                                                    IF PurchLineL.FINDSET THEN

                                                                           (PurchLineL."Document No." <> "Document No.") OR
                                                                           (PurchLineL."Line No." <> "Line No.")

                                                                // Start PA043248

                                                                      VehicleG."Vehicle Status"::"Used Vehicle":
                                                                        "Vehicle Status" := "Vehicle Status"::"Used Vehicle";
                                                                      VehicleG."Vehicle Status"::"Demo Vehicle":
                                                                        "Vehicle Status" := "Vehicle Status"::"Demo Vehicle";
                                                                    END;
                                                                    IF NOT (VehicleG."Vehicle Status" IN [
                                                                       VehicleG."Vehicle Status"::"New Vehicle",
                                                                       VehicleG."Vehicle Status"::"Demo Vehicle",
                                                                       VehicleG."Vehicle Status"::"Used Vehicle"])
                                                                    THEN

                                                                    UpdatePurchaseLineGlobalDim(Rec, FALSE);
                                                                // Stop EU.0005642

                                                                      "Posting Group" := VehicleStatusInvPostGrpG."Inventory Posting Group";
                                                                    END ELSE
                                                                      "Posting Group" := Item."Inventory Posting Group";
                                                                    IF "Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Return Order","Document Type"::"Credit Memo"] THEN BEGIN

                                                                      "Gen. Prod. Posting Group" := VehicleG."Gen. Prod. Posting Group";

                                                                    PurchaseLineExitPoint(Rec, ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnValidate,ExitPointSetupG.Type::"Inside 1",FIELDNAME(VIN));

                                                                      Description := VehicleG.Model;
                                                                // Stop EU.0066797
                                                                  END ELSE BEGIN

                                                                // Start EU.0005642
                                                                    UpdatePurchaseLineGlobalDim(Rec, FALSE);
                                                                // Stop EU.0005642
                                                                  END;
                                                                END ELSE BEGIN

                                                                      END;

                                                                          ELSE

                                                                              "Vehicle Status" := "Vehicle Status"::"Demo Vehicle"
                                                                            ELSE
                                                                              "Vehicle Status" := "Vehicle Status"::"Used Vehicle";
                                                                        END;

                                                                          "Item Type"::"Veh. Transfer":

                                                                                  END;

                                                                                "Gen. Prod. Posting Group");
                                                                // Stop PA032776
                                                                              VALIDATE("Gen. Prod. Posting Group");
                                                                            END;
                                                                        END;
                                                                      END;
                                                                // Start PA043248
                                                                  END;
                                                                // Stop PA043248
                                                                  IF TableTriggerG <> TableTriggerG::Modify THEN
                                                                // Start EU.0005642

                                                                // Stop EU.0005642

    { 5025362;;Trade-In for VIN    ;Code20        ;TableRelation=IF (Document Type=FILTER(<>Credit Memo)) Vehicle.VIN WHERE (Vehicle Status=FILTER(New Vehicle|Used Vehicle|Demo Vehicle))
