    PROCEDURE InitOutstanding@16();
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF "Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Return Order","Document Type"::"Credit Memo"] THEN BEGIN
        "Outstanding Quantity" := Quantity - "Return Qty. Shipped";
        "Outstanding Qty. (Base)" := "Quantity (Base)" - "Return Qty. Shipped (Base)";
        "Return Qty. Shipped Not Invd." := "Return Qty. Shipped" - "Quantity Invoiced";
        "Ret. Qty. Shpd Not Invd.(Base)" := "Return Qty. Shipped (Base)" - "Qty. Invoiced (Base)";
      END ELSE BEGIN
        "Outstanding Quantity" := Quantity - "Quantity Received";
        "Outstanding Qty. (Base)" := "Quantity (Base)" - "Qty. Received (Base)";
        "Qty. Rcd. Not Invoiced" := "Quantity Received" - "Quantity Invoiced";
        "Qty. Rcd. Not Invoiced (Base)" := "Qty. Received (Base)" - "Qty. Invoiced (Base)";
      END;
      // Stop INC
      InitOutstandingAmount;
      IF CurrFieldNo = 0 THEN
      // Start EU.0114873.115555
        FindStatus(FALSE);
      // Stop EU.0114873.115555
    END;

    PROCEDURE InitOutstandingAmount@19();
    BEGIN
      // Start PA036544
      IF ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function",ExitPointSetupG.Type::Pre,'InitOutstandingAmount') THEN
        EXIT;
      // Stop PA036544

      IF Quantity = 0 THEN BEGIN
        "Outstanding Amount" := 0;
        "Outstanding Amount (LCY)" := 0;
        "Amt. Rcd. Not Invoiced" := 0;
        "Amt. Rcd. Not Invoiced (LCY)" := 0;
      // Start INC
        "Return Shpd. Not Invd." := 0;
        "Return Shpd. Not Invd. (LCY)" := 0;
      // Stop INC
      END ELSE BEGIN
        GetPurchHeader;

      // Start PA036544
        ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function",ExitPointSetupG.Type::"Inside 1",'InitOutstandingAmount');
      // Stop PA036544

        VALIDATE(
          "Outstanding Amount",
          ROUND(
            "Amount Including VAT" * "Outstanding Quantity" / Quantity,
            Currency."Amount Rounding Precision"));
      // Start INC
        IF "Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Return Order","Document Type"::"Credit Memo"] THEN
          VALIDATE(
            "Return Shpd. Not Invd.",
            ROUND(
              "Amount Including VAT" * "Return Qty. Shipped Not Invd." / Quantity,
              Currency."Amount Rounding Precision"))
        ELSE
      // Stop INC
          VALIDATE(
            "Amt. Rcd. Not Invoiced",
            ROUND(
              "Amount Including VAT" * "Qty. Rcd. Not Invoiced" / Quantity,
              Currency."Amount Rounding Precision"));
      END;

      // Start PA036544
      ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function",ExitPointSetupG.Type::Post,'InitOutstandingAmount');
      // Stop PA036544
    END;

    PROCEDURE InitQtyToReceive@15();
    BEGIN
      "Qty. to Receive" := "Outstanding Quantity";
      "Qty. to Receive (Base)" := "Outstanding Qty. (Base)";

      InitQtyToInvoice;
    END;

    PROCEDURE InitQtyToShip@5803();
    BEGIN
      "Return Qty. to Ship" := "Outstanding Quantity";
      "Return Qty. to Ship (Base)" := "Outstanding Qty. (Base)";

      InitQtyToInvoice;
    END;

    PROCEDURE InitQtyToInvoice@13();
    BEGIN
      "Qty. to Invoice" := MaxQtyToInvoice;
      "Qty. to Invoice (Base)" := MaxQtyToInvoiceBase;

      IF CurrFieldNo = 0 THEN
      // Start EU.0114873.115555
        FindStatus(FALSE);
      // Stop EU.0114873.115555
    END;

    PROCEDURE MaxQtyToInvoice@18() : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF "Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Return Order","Document Type"::"Credit Memo"] THEN
        EXIT("Return Qty. Shipped" + "Return Qty. to Ship" - "Quantity Invoiced");
      // Stop INC
      EXIT("Quantity Received" + "Qty. to Receive" - "Quantity Invoiced");
    END;

    PROCEDURE MaxQtyToInvoiceBase@17() : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF "Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Return Order","Document Type"::"Credit Memo"] THEN
        EXIT("Return Qty. Shipped (Base)" + "Return Qty. to Ship (Base)" - "Qty. Invoiced (Base)");
      // Stop INC
      EXIT("Qty. Received (Base)" + "Qty. to Receive (Base)" - "Qty. Invoiced (Base)");
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CalcBaseQty@14(Qty@1000 : Decimal) : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      TESTFIELD("Qty. per Unit of Measure");
      EXIT(ROUND(Qty * "Qty. per Unit of Measure",0.00001));
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE SelectItemEntry@7(CurrentFieldNoP@1109400000 : Integer);
    VAR
      ReturnShpmtLineL@1109400003 : Record 6651;
      RecordsFromRetShipFoundL@1109400001 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      TESTFIELD(Type,Type::Item);
      ItemLedgEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Item No.","Variant Code",Open);
      ItemLedgEntry.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
      ItemLedgEntry.SETRANGE(Open,TRUE);
      IF Quantity <> 0 THEN

        IF "Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Return Order","Document Type"::"Credit Memo"] THEN
          ItemLedgEntry.SETRANGE(Positive,Quantity > 0)
        ELSE
          ItemLedgEntry.SETRANGE(Positive,Quantity < 0);

      IF CurrentFieldNoP = FIELDNO("Appl.-to Item Entry") THEN
        IF ItemLedgEntry.GET("Appl.-to Item Entry") THEN
          ;

      // Start EU.0055250
      IF (("Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Credit Memo")  AND ("Return Shipment No." <> '')) OR
         (("Document Type" = "Document Type"::Invoice)  AND ("Receipt No." <> ''))
      THEN
        ItemLedgEntry.SETRANGE("Location Code","Location Code");
      // Stop EU.0055250
      // Start PA041662.73195
      // Find also ILE records for Parts Purchase Orders that has Return Qty Shipped and Not Invoiced
      IF "Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Credit Memo" THEN BEGIN
        RecordsFromRetShipFoundL := MarkRecordsFromRetShipment(ItemLedgEntry);
        IF RecordsFromRetShipFoundL THEN BEGIN
          ItemLedgEntry.SETRANGE(Open);
          ItemLedgEntry.SETRANGE(Positive);
      // Start PA041187.95052
          ItemLedgEntry.MARKEDONLY(TRUE);
      // Stop PA041187.95052
        END;
      END;
      // Stop PA041662.73195

      IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Item Ledger Entries",ItemLedgEntry) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
        IF CurrentFieldNoP = FIELDNO("Appl.-to Item Entry") THEN BEGIN
          "Appl.-to Item Entry" := ItemLedgEntry."Entry No.";

          IF "Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Return Order","Document Type"::"Credit Memo"] THEN
      // Stop INC
            "Unit Cost (LCY)" := CalculateUnitCost(ItemLedgEntry);
          VALIDATE("Unit Cost (LCY)");
      // Start PA041662.73195
          IF "Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Credit Memo" THEN
            GetReturnShipmentLineForCR();
      // Stop PA041662.73195
        END;
      // Start EU.0055250
        GetPurchHeader();
        IF (("Return Shipment No." <> '') OR ("Receipt No." <> '')) OR
           ((PurchHeader."Applies-to Doc. No." <> '') AND
            (PurchHeader."Applies-to Doc. Type" <> PurchHeader."Applies-to Doc. Type"::" " ))
        THEN
          ItemLedgEntry.TESTFIELD("Location Code","Location Code");
        IF ItemLedgEntry."Location Code" <> "Location Code" THEN BEGIN
      // Stop EU.0055250
          "Location Code" := ItemLedgEntry."Location Code";
      // Start PA036118
      // Start EU.0055250
      // Stop EU.0055250
      // Start PA036549.34230
          LocationG.PurchaseCrossLocationCheck(FORMAT(Type), PurchHeader."Location Code", "Location Code", "Order Type");
      // Start PA036549.34230
          LocationG.PurchaseCrossBranchCheck(PurchHeader, Rec);
      // Stop PA036118
      // Start EU.0055250
        END;
      // Stop EU.0055250
        "Serial No." := ItemLedgEntry."Serial No.";

        IF VIN <> '' THEN
          TESTFIELD("Serial No.",VIN);
        "Bin Code" := ItemLedgEntry."Bin Code";
        "Book No." := ItemLedgEntry."Book No.";
      END;
      // Start EU.0055250
      ItemLedgEntry.MARKEDONLY(FALSE);
      // Stop EU.0055250
    END;

    PROCEDURE SetPurchHeader@12(NewPurchHeader@1000 : Record 38);
    BEGIN
      PurchHeader := NewPurchHeader;

      IF PurchHeader."Currency Code" = '' THEN
        Currency.InitRoundingPrecision
      ELSE BEGIN
        PurchHeader.TESTFIELD("Currency Factor");
        Currency.GET(PurchHeader."Currency Code");
        Currency.TESTFIELD("Amount Rounding Precision");
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetPurchHeader@1();
    BEGIN
      TESTFIELD("Document No.");
      // Start INC
      IF ("Document Type" <> PurchHeader."Document Type") OR
         ("Document No." <> PurchHeader."No.") OR
         ("Buy-from Vendor No." <> PurchHeader."Buy-from Vendor No.") OR
         ("Pay-to Vendor No." <> PurchHeader."Pay-to Vendor No.")
      THEN BEGIN
        PurchHeader.GET("Document Type","Document No.");
        IF PurchHeader."Currency Code" = '' THEN
          Currency.InitRoundingPrecision
        ELSE BEGIN
          PurchHeader.TESTFIELD("Currency Factor");
          Currency.GET(PurchHeader."Currency Code");
          Currency.TESTFIELD("Amount Rounding Precision");
        END;
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetItem@4();
    BEGIN
      TESTFIELD("No.");
      IF Item."No." <> "No." THEN
        Item.GET("No.");
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE UpdateDirectUnitCost@2();
    BEGIN
      IF ("Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle) AND (VIN <> '') AND VehicleG.GET(VIN) THEN BEGIN
        //Purch. Price will be retrieved from option table
      END ELSE BEGIN
        GetPurchHeader();
        GetItem();
        ItemVend."Vendor No." := "Buy-from Vendor No.";
        ItemVend."Unit of Measure Code" := "Unit of Measure Code";
        IF "Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::Inquiry,"Document Type"::Order] THEN
          ItemVend."Starting Date" := PurchHeader."Order Date"
        ELSE
          ItemVend."Starting Date" := PurchHeader."Posting Date";

        IF "Order Type" = "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases" THEN
          ItemVend."Starting Date" := "Vehicle Direct Unit Cost Date";
        ItemVend."Purch. Order Type" := PurchHeader."Purch. Order Type";
        ItemVend."Ending Date" := ItemVend."Starting Date";

        IF "Order Type" = "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases" THEN
          ItemVend."Ending Date" := "Vehicle Direct Unit Cost Date";
        Item.FindItemVend(ItemVend,"Location Code",TRUE);
        "Direct Unit Cost" := ItemVend."Direct Unit Cost";
        IF ItemVend."Currency Code" <> PurchHeader."Currency Code" THEN BEGIN
          IF ItemVend."Currency Code" <> '' THEN
            "Direct Unit Cost" :=
              CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtFCYToLCY(
                GetDate,ItemVend."Currency Code",
                "Direct Unit Cost",
                CurrExchRate.ExchangeRate(GetDate,ItemVend."Currency Code"));
          IF PurchHeader."Currency Code" <> '' THEN BEGIN
            "Direct Unit Cost" :=
              CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(
                GetDate,"Currency Code",
                "Direct Unit Cost",
                PurchHeader."Currency Factor");
            Currency.TESTFIELD("Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");
          END;
          "Direct Unit Cost" := ROUND("Direct Unit Cost",Currency."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");
        END;
        "Vendor Item No." := ItemVend."Vendor Item No.";
        // Start AP001856
        IF "Vendor Item No." = '' THEN
          "Vendor Item No." := Item."Vendor Item No.";
        // Stop AP001856
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdateUnitCost@5();
    BEGIN
      IF Quantity <> 0 THEN
        "Unit Cost" :=
          ("Direct Unit Cost" - (("Line Discount Amount" + "Inv. Discount Amount") / Quantity)) *
          (1 + "Indirect Cost %" / 100)
      ELSE
        "Unit Cost" := "Direct Unit Cost" * (1 + "Indirect Cost %" / 100);

      GetPurchHeader;
      IF PurchHeader."Currency Code" <> '' THEN BEGIN
        PurchHeader.TESTFIELD("Currency Factor");
        "Unit Cost (LCY)" :=
          CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtFCYToLCY(
            GetDate,"Currency Code",
            "Unit Cost",PurchHeader."Currency Factor");
      END ELSE
        "Unit Cost (LCY)" := "Unit Cost";

      IF Type = Type::Item THEN BEGIN
        GetItem;
        IF Item."Costing Method" = Item."Costing Method"::Standard THEN BEGIN
      // Start INC
          IF SKU.GET("No.","Location Code") THEN
            "Unit Cost (LCY)" := SKU."Unit Cost" * "Qty. per Unit of Measure"
          ELSE
      // Stop INC
            "Unit Cost (LCY)" := Item."Unit Cost" * "Qty. per Unit of Measure";
          "Indirect Cost %" := 0;
        END;
      END;

      "Unit Cost (LCY)" := ROUND("Unit Cost (LCY)",0.00001);
      IF PurchHeader."Currency Code" <> '' THEN
        Currency.TESTFIELD("Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");
      "Unit Cost" := ROUND("Unit Cost",Currency."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");

      UpdateSalesCost;
      // Start INC
      UpdateServCost();
      IF "VAT Calculation Type" = "VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax" THEN
        VALIDATE("Unit Price (LCY)");
      IF Type = Type::"Charge (Item)" THEN
        UpdateItemChargeAssgnt();
      // Stop INC
      IF ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::Invoice) AND ("Trade-In for VIN" <> '') THEN BEGIN
        SalTradeInsG.SETCURRENTKEY("Purch. Invoice No.","Purch. Invoice Line No.");
        SalTradeInsG.SETRANGE("Purch. Invoice No.","Document No.");
        SalTradeInsG.SETRANGE("Purch. Invoice Line No.","Line No.");
        IF (SalTradeInsG.FINDFIRST) AND (SalTradeInsG."Unit Cost (LCY)" <> "Unit Cost (LCY)") THEN BEGIN
          SalTradeInsG.VALIDATE("Unit Cost (LCY)", "Unit Cost (LCY)");
          SalTradeInsG.MODIFY;
        END;
      END;
      IF ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Credit Memo") AND ("Trade-In for VIN" <> '') THEN BEGIN
        SalTradeInsG.SETCURRENTKEY("Purch. Cr. Memo No.","Purch. Cr. Memo Line No.");
        SalTradeInsG.SETRANGE("Purch. Cr. Memo No.","Document No.");
        SalTradeInsG.SETRANGE("Purch. Cr. Memo Line No.","Line No.");
        IF (SalTradeInsG.FINDFIRST) AND (SalTradeInsG."Unit Cost (LCY)" <> "Unit Cost (LCY)") THEN BEGIN
          SalTradeInsG.VALIDATE("Unit Cost (LCY)", "Unit Cost (LCY)");
          SalTradeInsG.MODIFY;
        END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdateAmounts@3();
    BEGIN
      // Start PA036544
      IF ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function",ExitPointSetupG.Type::Pre,'UpdateAmounts') THEN
        EXIT;
      // Stop PA036544

      // Start INC
      IF CurrFieldNo <> 0 THEN
        CheckImportCostUpdate;
      // Stop INC

      GetPurchHeader;
      TESTFIELD(Type);

      // Start PA036544
      IF NOT ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function",ExitPointSetupG.Type::"Condition 1",'UpdateAmounts') THEN
      // Stop PA036544
        CASE "VAT Calculation Type" OF
          "VAT Calculation Type"::"Normal VAT",
          "VAT Calculation Type"::"Reverse Charge VAT",
          "VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax":
            BEGIN
              Amount :=
                ROUND(Quantity * "Direct Unit Cost",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision") -
                "Line Discount Amount" - "Inv. Discount Amount";
              "VAT Base Amount" := ROUND(Amount * (1 - PurchHeader."VAT Base Discount %" / 100),0.00001);
              "Amount Including VAT" := ROUND(Amount + "VAT Base Amount" * "VAT %" / 100,0.00001);
            END;

          "VAT Calculation Type"::"Exch. Parts Tax":
            BEGIN
              Amount :=
                ROUND(Quantity * "Direct Unit Cost",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision") -
                "Line Discount Amount" - "Inv. Discount Amount";
              "VAT Base Amount" := ROUND(Amount * (1 - PurchHeader."VAT Base Discount %" / 100),0.00001);
              "Exch. Parts Tax Base" := "List Price (LCY)" * Quantity;
              IF PurchHeader."Currency Code" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                PurchHeader.TESTFIELD("Currency Factor");
                "Exch. Parts Tax Base" := ROUND(CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(
                  GetDate(), "Currency Code", "Exch. Parts Tax Base", PurchHeader."Currency Factor"), 0.00001);
              END;
              "Exch. Parts Tax Base" := ROUND("Exch. Parts Tax Base" * "Exch. Parts Tax %" / 100, 0.00001);

              "Exch. Parts Tax Amount" := ROUND("Exch. Parts Tax Base" * "Exch. Parts VAT %" / 100,0.00001);
              "Amount Including VAT" := ROUND(Amount + "VAT Base Amount" * "VAT %" /100 +
                "Exch. Parts Tax Amount",0.00001);
            END;

          "VAT Calculation Type"::"Full VAT":
            BEGIN
              Amount := 0;
              "VAT Base Amount" := 0;
              "Amount Including VAT" :=
                ROUND(Quantity * "Direct Unit Cost",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
            END;
          "VAT Calculation Type"::"Sales Tax":
            BEGIN
              PurchHeader.TESTFIELD("VAT Base Discount %",0);
              Amount :=
                ROUND(Quantity * "Direct Unit Cost",Currency."Amount Rounding Precision") -
                "Line Discount Amount" - "Inv. Discount Amount";
              "VAT Base Amount" := ROUND(Amount,0.00001);
              IF "Use Tax" THEN
                "Amount Including VAT" := ROUND("VAT Base Amount",0.00001)
              ELSE BEGIN
      // Start PA036544
                ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function",ExitPointSetupG.Type::"Inside 1",'UpdateAmounts');
      // Stop PA036544
                "Amount Including VAT" :=
                  Amount +
                  SalesTaxCalculate.CalculateTax(
                    "Tax Area Code","Tax Group Code","Tax Liable",PurchHeader."Posting Date",
                    "VAT Base Amount",Quantity,PurchHeader."Currency Factor");
                IF "VAT Base Amount" <> 0 THEN
                  "VAT %" :=
                    ROUND(100 * ("Amount Including VAT" - "VAT Base Amount") / "VAT Base Amount",0.00001)
                ELSE BEGIN
                  "VAT %" := 0;
                END;
              END;
            END;
        END;
      InitOutstandingAmount;

      // Start PA036544
      ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function",ExitPointSetupG.Type::Post,'UpdateAmounts');
      // Stop PA036544
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE UpdateSalesCost@6();
    BEGIN
      IF "Sales Order Line No." <> 0 THEN BEGIN // Drop Shipment
        SalesOrderLine.GET(SalesOrderLine."Document Type"::Order,"Sales Order No.","Sales Order Line No.");
        SalesOrderLine."Unit Cost (LCY)" := "Unit Cost (LCY)";
        SalesOrderLine."Unit Cost" := "Unit Cost";
        SalesOrderLine.VALIDATE("Unit Cost (LCY)"); // xOrderLine = OrderLine
      // Start PA035597
      // Stop PA035597
        SalesOrderLine.MODIFY;
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetFAPostingGroup@10();
    VAR
      LocalGLAcc@1000 : Record 15;
      FAPostingGr@1001 : Record 5606;
    BEGIN
      IF (Type <> Type::"Fixed Asset") OR ("No." = '') THEN
        EXIT;
      IF "Depreciation Book Code" = '' THEN BEGIN
        FASetup.GET;
        "Depreciation Book Code" := FASetup."Default Depr. Book";
        IF NOT FADeprBook.GET("No.","Depreciation Book Code") THEN
          "Depreciation Book Code" := '';
        IF "Depreciation Book Code" = '' THEN
          EXIT;
      END;
      IF "FA Posting Type" = "FA Posting Type"::" " THEN
        "FA Posting Type" := "FA Posting Type"::"Acquisition Cost";
      FADeprBook.GET("No.","Depreciation Book Code");
      FADeprBook.TESTFIELD("FA Posting Group");
      FAPostingGr.GET(FADeprBook."FA Posting Group");
      IF "FA Posting Type" = "FA Posting Type"::"Acquisition Cost" THEN BEGIN
        FAPostingGr.TESTFIELD("Acquisition Cost Account");
        LocalGLAcc.GET(FAPostingGr."Acquisition Cost Account");
      END ELSE BEGIN
        FAPostingGr.TESTFIELD("Maintenance Expense Account");
        LocalGLAcc.GET(FAPostingGr."Maintenance Expense Account");
      END;
      LocalGLAcc.TESTFIELD(Blocked,FALSE);
      LocalGLAcc.TESTFIELD("Account Type",GLAcc."Account Type"::Posting);
      LocalGLAcc.TESTFIELD("Gen. Prod. Posting Group");

      "Posting Group" := FADeprBook."FA Posting Group";
      VALIDATE("Gen. Prod. Posting Group",LocalGLAcc."Gen. Prod. Posting Group");
      VALIDATE("VAT Prod. Posting Group",LocalGLAcc."VAT Prod. Posting Group");
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdateUOMQtyPerStockQty@9();
    BEGIN
      GetItem;
      "Unit Cost (LCY)" := Item."Unit Cost" * "Qty. per Unit of Measure";
      GetPurchHeader;
      IF PurchHeader."Currency Code" <> '' THEN
        "Unit Cost" :=
          CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(
            GetDate,PurchHeader."Currency Code",
            "Unit Cost (LCY)",PurchHeader."Currency Factor")
      ELSE
        "Unit Cost" := "Unit Cost (LCY)";
      UpdateDirectUnitCost;
    END;

    PROCEDURE ShowReservation@8();
    VAR
      ReservVeh@1109400000 : Page 5025512;

      TESTFIELD(Reserve);
      IF "Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle THEN BEGIN

      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE ShowReservationEntries@21(Modal@1000 : Boolean);
    BEGIN
      TESTFIELD(Type,Type::Item);
      TESTFIELD("No.");
      IF Signed("Quantity (Base)") < 0 THEN BEGIN
        ReservEngineMgt.InitFilterAndSortingLookupFor(ReservEntry,TRUE);
        ReservEngineMgt.PurchLineFilterReservFor(ReservEntry,Rec);
      END ELSE BEGIN
        ReservEngineMgt.InitFilterAndSortingLookupFrom(ReservEntry,TRUE);
        ReservEngineMgt.PurchLineFilterReservFrom(ReservEntry,Rec);
      END;
      IF Modal THEN
        PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Reservation Entries",ReservEntry)
      ELSE
        PAGE.RUN(PAGE::"Reservation Entries",ReservEntry);
    END;

    PROCEDURE AutoReserve@11(ShowReservationForm@1109400000 : Boolean);
    BEGIN
      TESTFIELD(Type,Type::Item);
      TESTFIELD("No.");
      ReservSetupG.GET;
      IF ((("Document Type" = "Document Type"::Inquiry) AND ReservSetupG."Auto Purchase Inquiry") OR
         (("Document Type" = "Document Type"::Order) AND ReservSetupG."Auto Purchase Order") OR
         (("Document Type" = "Document Type"::Invoice) AND ReservSetupG."Auto Purchase Invoice") OR
      // Start INC
         (("Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Return Order") AND (ReservSetupG."Auto Purchase Return Order")) OR
      // Stop INC
         (("Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Credit Memo") AND ReservSetupG."Auto Purchase Credit Memo") OR
         (("Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Blanket Order") AND ReservSetupG."Auto Blanket Purchase Order")) AND
         (ReservEngineMgt.PurchLineReservQuantity(Rec,FALSE) > 0)
      THEN BEGIN
        ReservEngineMgt.PurchLineSetReservFor(Rec);
        TESTFIELD("Expected Receipt Date");
        ReservEngineMgt.AutoReserve(
          FullAutoReservation,CALCDATE(ReservSetupG."Valid-to Formula","Expected Receipt Date"),'',
          "Expected Receipt Date");
        FIND;
        IF NOT FullAutoReservation AND ShowReservationForm THEN BEGIN
          COMMIT;
          IF CONFIRM(Text025,TRUE) THEN BEGIN
            ShowReservation;
            FIND;
          END;
        END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetDate@28() : Date;
    BEGIN
      IF PurchHeader."Document Type" = PurchHeader."Document Type"::Inquiry THEN
        EXIT(WORKDATE);
      // Start INC
      IF PurchHeader."Posting Date" <> 0D THEN
        EXIT(PurchHeader."Posting Date");
      EXIT(WORKDATE);
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE Signed@20(Value@1000 : Decimal) : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      CASE "Document Type" OF
        "Document Type"::Inquiry,
          "Document Type"::Order,
          "Document Type"::Invoice,
        "Document Type"::"Blanket Order":
          EXIT(Value);
      // Start INC
        "Document Type"::"Return Order",
      // Stop INC
        "Document Type"::"Credit Memo":
          EXIT(-Value);
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE ItemAvailability@22(AvailabilityType@1000 : 'Date,Variant,Location,Bin');
    BEGIN
      TESTFIELD(Type,Type::Item);
      TESTFIELD("No.");
      Item.RESET;
      Item.GET("No.");
      Item.SETRANGE("No.","No.");
      Item.SETRANGE("Date Filter",0D,"Expected Receipt Date");

      CASE AvailabilityType OF
        AvailabilityType::Date:
          BEGIN
            Item.SETRANGE("Variant Filter","Variant Code");
            Item.SETRANGE("Location Filter","Location Code");
            Item.SETRANGE("Bin Filter","Bin Code");
            CLEAR(ItemAvailByDate);
            ItemAvailByDate.LOOKUPMODE(TRUE);
            ItemAvailByDate.SETRECORD(Item);
            ItemAvailByDate.SETTABLEVIEW(Item);
            IF ItemAvailByDate.RUNMODAL = ACTION::LookupOK THEN
              IF "Expected Receipt Date" <> ItemAvailByDate.GetLastDate THEN
                IF CONFIRM(
                     Text014,TRUE,FIELDCAPTION("Expected Receipt Date"),
                     "Expected Receipt Date",ItemAvailByDate.GetLastDate)
                THEN
                  VALIDATE("Expected Receipt Date",ItemAvailByDate.GetLastDate);
          END;
        AvailabilityType::Variant:
          BEGIN
            Item.SETRANGE("Location Filter","Location Code");
            Item.SETRANGE("Bin Filter","Bin Code");
            CLEAR(ItemAvailByVar);
            ItemAvailByVar.LOOKUPMODE(TRUE);
            ItemAvailByVar.SETRECORD(Item);
            ItemAvailByVar.SETTABLEVIEW(Item);
            IF ItemAvailByVar.RUNMODAL = ACTION::LookupOK THEN
              IF "Variant Code" <> ItemAvailByVar.GetLastVariant THEN
                IF CONFIRM(
                     Text014,TRUE,FIELDCAPTION("Variant Code"),"Variant Code",
                     ItemAvailByVar.GetLastVariant)
                THEN
                  VALIDATE("Variant Code",ItemAvailByVar.GetLastVariant);
          END;
        AvailabilityType::Location:
          BEGIN
            Item.SETRANGE("Variant Filter","Variant Code");
            Item.SETRANGE("Bin Filter","Bin Code");
            CLEAR(ItemAvailByLoc);
            ItemAvailByLoc.LOOKUPMODE(TRUE);
            ItemAvailByLoc.SETRECORD(Item);
            ItemAvailByLoc.SETTABLEVIEW(Item);
            IF ItemAvailByLoc.RUNMODAL = ACTION::LookupOK THEN
      // Start INC
              IF ("Location Code" <> ItemAvailByLoc.GetLastLocation) AND (ItemAvailByLoc.GetLastLocation <> '') THEN
      // Stop INC
                IF CONFIRM(
                   Text014,TRUE,FIELDCAPTION("Location Code"),"Location Code",
                   ItemAvailByLoc.GetLastLocation)
                THEN
                  VALIDATE("Location Code",ItemAvailByLoc.GetLastLocation);
          END;
        AvailabilityType::Bin:
          BEGIN
            Item.SETRANGE("Variant Filter","Variant Code");
            Item.SETRANGE("Location Filter","Location Code");
            CLEAR(ItemAvailByBinG);
            ItemAvailByBinG.LOOKUPMODE(TRUE);
            ItemAvailByBinG.SETRECORD(Item);
            ItemAvailByBinG.SETTABLEVIEW(Item);
            IF ItemAvailByBinG.RUNMODAL = ACTION::LookupOK THEN
      // Start INC
              IF NOT (ItemAvailByBinG.GetLastBin IN ['',"Bin Code"]) THEN
      // Stop INC
                IF CONFIRM(
                   Text014,TRUE,FIELDCAPTION("Bin Code"),"Bin Code",
                   ItemAvailByBinG.GetLastBin)
                THEN
                  VALIDATE("Bin Code",ItemAvailByBinG.GetLastBin);
          END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE BlanketOrderLookup@36();
    BEGIN

        PurchLine2.TESTFIELD("Document Type","Document Type"::"Blanket Order");
        "Blanket Order No." := PurchLine2."Document No.";
        VALIDATE("Blanket Order Line No.",PurchLine2."Line No.");
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE VerifyItemLineDim@73();
    BEGIN
      IF ("Dimension Set ID" <> xRec."Dimension Set ID") AND (Type = Type::Item) THEN
        IF ("Qty. Rcd. Not Invoiced" <> 0) OR ("Return Qty. Shipped Not Invd." <> 0) THEN
          IF NOT CONFIRM(Text049,TRUE,TABLECAPTION) THEN
            ERROR(Text050);
    END;

    PROCEDURE CreateDim@26(Type1@1000 : Integer;No1@1001 : Code[20];Type2@1002 : Integer;No2@1003 : Code[20]);
    VAR
      SourceCodeSetup@1008 : Record 242;
      TableID@1009 : ARRAY [10] OF Integer;

      "Dimension Set ID" := DimMgt.GetDefaultDimID(TableID,No,MakeCodeL,SourceCodeSetup.Purchases,"Shortcut Dimension 1 Code","Shortcut Dimension 2 Code",PurchHeader."Dimension Set ID",DATABASE::Vendor);
      // Stop PA036002.27153

    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetSKU@5806() : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      TESTFIELD("No.");
      IF (SKU."Location Code" = "Location Code") AND (SKU."Item No." = "No.") THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);
      IF SKU.GET("No.","Location Code") THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);
      EXIT(FALSE);
      // Stop INC
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CalculateUnitCost@5809(ItemLedgEntry@1000 : Record 32) : Decimal;
    VAR
      ValueEntry@1001 : Record 5802;
      CalculatedAdjustedCost@1002 : Decimal;
      ExpectedAdjustedCost@1003 : Decimal;
      UnitCost@1004 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      ValueEntry.RESET;
      ValueEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Item Ledger Entry No.",Inventoriable,"Expected Cost");
      ValueEntry.SETRANGE("Item Ledger Entry No.",ItemLedgEntry."Entry No.");
      ValueEntry.SETRANGE(Inventoriable,TRUE);
      IF ItemLedgEntry."Completely Invoiced" THEN
        ValueEntry.SETRANGE("Expected Cost",FALSE);
      IF ValueEntry.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          IF ValueEntry."Expected Cost" THEN
            ExpectedAdjustedCost := ExpectedAdjustedCost + ValueEntry."Adjusted Cost"
          ELSE
            CalculatedAdjustedCost := CalculatedAdjustedCost + ValueEntry."Adjusted Cost";
        UNTIL ValueEntry.NEXT = 0;
      UnitCost :=
        ((ExpectedAdjustedCost / ItemLedgEntry.Quantity *
        (ItemLedgEntry.Quantity - ItemLedgEntry."Invoiced Quantity")) +
        CalculatedAdjustedCost) / ItemLedgEntry.Quantity;
      EXIT(ABS(ROUND(UnitCost * "Qty. per Unit of Measure",0.00001)));
    END;

    PROCEDURE ShowItemChargeAssgnt@5801();
    VAR
      ItemChargeAssgnts@1000 : Page 5805;
      AssignItemChargePurch@1001 : Codeunit 5805;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      GET("Document Type","Document No.","Line No.");
      TESTFIELD(Type,Type::"Charge (Item)");
      TESTFIELD("No.");
      TESTFIELD(Quantity);

      ItemChargeAssgntPurch.RESET;
      ItemChargeAssgntPurch.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
      ItemChargeAssgntPurch.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
      ItemChargeAssgntPurch.SETRANGE("Document Line No.","Line No.");
      ItemChargeAssgntPurch.SETRANGE("Item Charge No.","No.");
      IF NOT ItemChargeAssgntPurch.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
        ItemChargeAssgntPurch."Document Type" := "Document Type";
        ItemChargeAssgntPurch."Document No." := "Document No.";
        ItemChargeAssgntPurch."Document Line No." := "Line No.";
        ItemChargeAssgntPurch."Item Charge No." := "No.";
        GetPurchHeader;
        IF "Inv. Discount Amount" = 0 THEN
          ItemChargeAssgntPurch."Unit Cost" := "Unit Cost"
        ELSE
          ItemChargeAssgntPurch."Unit Cost" :=
            ROUND(
              (Amount - "Inv. Discount Amount") / Quantity,
              Currency."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");
      END;

      IF "Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Return Order","Document Type"::"Credit Memo"] THEN
        AssignItemChargePurch.CreateDocChargeAssgnt(ItemChargeAssgntPurch,"Return Shipment No.")
      ELSE
        AssignItemChargePurch.CreateDocChargeAssgnt(ItemChargeAssgntPurch,"Receipt No.");
      CLEAR(AssignItemChargePurch);
      COMMIT;

      ItemChargeAssgnts.Initialize(Rec,ItemChargeAssgntPurch."Unit Cost");
      ItemChargeAssgnts.RUNMODAL;
      // Start EU.0005642
      UpdatePurchaseLineGlobalDim(Rec, TRUE);
      // Stop EU.0005642
      CALCFIELDS("Qty. to Assign");
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdateItemChargeAssgnt@5807();
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      CALCFIELDS("Qty. Assigned");
      TESTFIELD("Quantity Invoiced","Qty. Assigned");
      ItemChargeAssgntPurch.RESET;
      ItemChargeAssgntPurch.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
      ItemChargeAssgntPurch.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
      ItemChargeAssgntPurch.SETRANGE("Document Line No.","Line No.");
      IF (CurrFieldNo <> 0) AND ("Unit Cost" <> xRec."Unit Cost") THEN BEGIN
        ItemChargeAssgntPurch.SETFILTER("Qty. Assigned",'<>0');
        IF ItemChargeAssgntPurch.FINDFIRST THEN
          ERROR(Text022,
            FIELDCAPTION("Unit Cost"));
        ItemChargeAssgntPurch.SETRANGE("Qty. Assigned");
      END;

      IF ItemChargeAssgntPurch.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        GetPurchHeader;
        REPEAT
          IF "Inv. Discount Amount" = 0 THEN BEGIN
            IF ItemChargeAssgntPurch."Unit Cost" <> "Unit Cost" THEN BEGIN
              ItemChargeAssgntPurch."Unit Cost" := "Unit Cost";
              ItemChargeAssgntPurch.VALIDATE("Qty. to Assign");
              ItemChargeAssgntPurch.MODIFY;
            END;
          END ELSE
            IF ItemChargeAssgntPurch."Unit Cost" <> ROUND(
               (Amount - "Inv. Discount Amount") / Quantity,
               Currency."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision")
            THEN BEGIN
              ItemChargeAssgntPurch."Unit Cost" :=
                ROUND(
                  (Amount - "Inv. Discount Amount") / Quantity,
                  Currency."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");
              ItemChargeAssgntPurch.VALIDATE("Qty. to Assign");
              ItemChargeAssgntPurch.MODIFY;
            END;
        UNTIL ItemChargeAssgntPurch.NEXT = 0;
        CALCFIELDS("Qty. to Assign");
      // Start EU.0005642
        UpdatePurchaseLineGlobalDim(Rec, TRUE);
      // Stop EU.0005642
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE DeleteItemChargeAssgnt@5802(DocType@1000 : Option;DocNo@1001 : Code[20];DocLineNo@1002 : Integer);
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      ItemChargeAssgntPurch.SETCURRENTKEY(
        "Applies-to Doc. Type","Applies-to Doc. No.","Applies-to Doc. Line No.");
      ItemChargeAssgntPurch.SETRANGE("Applies-to Doc. Type",DocType);
      ItemChargeAssgntPurch.SETRANGE("Applies-to Doc. No.",DocNo);
      ItemChargeAssgntPurch.SETRANGE("Applies-to Doc. Line No.",DocLineNo);
      IF NOT ItemChargeAssgntPurch.ISEMPTY THEN
        ItemChargeAssgntPurch.DELETEALL(TRUE);
      // Stop INC
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE DeleteChargeChargeAssgnt@5804(DocType@1000 : Option;DocNo@1001 : Code[20];DocLineNo@1002 : Integer);
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF "Quantity Invoiced" <> 0 THEN BEGIN
        CALCFIELDS("Qty. Assigned");

      END;
      ItemChargeAssgntPurch.RESET;
      ItemChargeAssgntPurch.SETRANGE("Document Type",DocType);
      ItemChargeAssgntPurch.SETRANGE("Document No.",DocNo);
      ItemChargeAssgntPurch.SETRANGE("Document Line No.",DocLineNo);
      IF NOT ItemChargeAssgntPurch.ISEMPTY THEN
        ItemChargeAssgntPurch.DELETEALL;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    VAR
      ItemChargeAssgntPurch@1000 : Record 5805;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      ItemChargeAssgntPurch.SETCURRENTKEY(
        "Applies-to Doc. Type","Applies-to Doc. No.","Applies-to Doc. Line No.");
      ItemChargeAssgntPurch.SETRANGE("Applies-to Doc. Type","Document Type");
      ItemChargeAssgntPurch.SETRANGE("Applies-to Doc. No.","Document No.");

      ItemChargeAssgntPurch.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");

        TESTFIELD("Allow Item Charge Assignment");
        REPEAT
          ItemChargeAssgntPurch.TESTFIELD("Qty. to Assign",0);
        UNTIL ItemChargeAssgntPurch.NEXT = 0;
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE ExitPointCall@1109400005(MakeCoddeP@1109400003 : Code[20];TriggerP@1109400002 : Integer;TypeP@1109400001 : Integer;ExitPointIDP@1109400000 : Text[50];VAR EPRecRefP@1109400005 : RecordRef) : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(ExitPointUnitG.RunExitPoint(
        ExitPointSetupG."Object Type"::Table,
        DATABASE::"Purchase Line",
        MakeCoddeP, TriggerP, TypeP, ExitPointIDP, EPRecRefP, EPRecRef2G, ExitPointParamG));
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE ExitPoint@5025450(TriggerP@1119452001 : Integer;TypeP@1119432000 : Integer;ExitPointIDP@1119432001 : Text[50]) ReturnR : Boolean;
    VAR
      EPRecRefL@1109400004 : RecordRef;
    BEGIN
      // @ This local function works as ExitPoint wrapper function. It will control the ExitPointCheck function call.
      // @ It passes thru all the handshake parameter values.
      // @ It takes care to provide the processing records as RecordReference to the ExitPointCheck function.
      // @ When possible a Make Code is also identified and passed to the called ExitPointCheck function.

      // Start PA036544
      EPRecRefL.GETTABLE(Rec);
      EPRecRef2G.GETTABLE(xRec);
      ExitPointParamG."Called CurrFieldNo" := CurrFieldNo;
      ReturnR := ExitPointCall("Shortcut Dimension 2 Code", TriggerP, TypeP, ExitPointIDP, EPRecRefL);
      EPRecRefL.SETTABLE(Rec);
      CLEAR(EPRecRef2G);
      // Stop PA036544
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE PurchaseLineExitPoint@1101342651(VAR PurchLineP@1101342643 : Record 39;TriggerP@1109400002 : Integer;TypeP@1109400001 : Integer;ExitPointIDP@1109400000 : Text[50]) ReturnR : Boolean;
    VAR
      EPRecRefL@1109400004 : RecordRef;
    BEGIN
      // @ This local function works as ExitPoint wrapper function. It will control the ExitPointCheck function call.
      // @ It passes thru all the handshake parameter values.
      // @ It takes care to provide the processing records as RecordReference to the ExitPointCheck function.
      // @ When possible a Make Code is also identified and passed to the called ExitPointCheck function.

      EPRecRefL.GETTABLE(PurchLineP);
      ReturnR := ExitPointCall(PurchLineP."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code", TriggerP, TypeP, ExitPointIDP, EPRecRefL);
      EPRecRefL.SETTABLE(PurchLineP);
      CLEAR(EPRecRef2G);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE __STOP_EXITPOINT__@5025451();
    BEGIN
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckUserRights@1109400003(ActionTypeP@1109400001 : Integer);
    VAR
      ShowErrorL@1109400000 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      // Stop INC
      // Start PA033019
      IF "Order Type" <> "Order Type"::Service THEN
        EXIT;
      UserSetupGet();
      CASE Type OF
        Type::" ":
          ShowErrorL := UserSetupG."Service Change Text" = UserSetupG."Service Change Text"::" ";
        Type::"Account (G/L)":
          ShowErrorL := UserSetupG."Service G/L Account Line" = UserSetupG."Service G/L Account Line"::" ";
        Type::Item:
          ShowErrorL := UserSetupG."Service Item Line" = UserSetupG."Service Item Line"::" ";
        Type::"Charge (Item)":
          ShowErrorL := UserSetupG."Service Item Line" = UserSetupG."Service Item Line"::" ";
      END;
      IF ShowErrorL THEN
        ERROR(C_INC_YouHaveNoRightsToDoThat,
          SELECTSTR(ActionTypeP + 1, C_INC_InsertModifyDeleteRename),
          TABLECAPTION,
          FIELDCAPTION(Type),
          Type);
      IF (xRec.Type <> Type) AND (ActionTypeP <> ModificationTypeG::Insert) THEN
        CASE xRec.Type OF
          Type::" ":
            ShowErrorL := UserSetupG."Service Change Text" = UserSetupG."Service Change Text"::" ";
          Type::"Account (G/L)":
            ShowErrorL := UserSetupG."Service G/L Account Line" = UserSetupG."Service G/L Account Line"::" ";
          Type::Item:
            ShowErrorL := UserSetupG."Service Item Line" = UserSetupG."Service Item Line"::" ";
          Type::"Charge (Item)":
            ShowErrorL := UserSetupG."Service Item Line" = UserSetupG."Service Item Line"::" ";
        END;
      IF ShowErrorL THEN
        ERROR(C_INC_YouHaveNoRightsToDoThat,
          SELECTSTR(ActionTypeP + 1, C_INC_InsertModifyDeleteRename),
          TABLECAPTION,
          FIELDCAPTION(Type),
          xRec.Type);
      // Stop PA033019
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE UserSetupGet@1109400004();
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      // Start PA033019
      IF UserSetupG."User ID" = USERID THEN
        EXIT;
      UserSetupG.GET(USERID);
      // Stop PA033019
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE ShowDocument@90026();
    VAR
      PurchHdrL@1109400000 : Record 38;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      PurchHdrL.GET("Document Type","Document No.");
      // Start PA036549.33628
      IF "Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Blanket Order" THEN
        PAGE.RUN(PAGE::"Blanket Purchase Order",PurchHdrL)
      ELSE
        CASE "Order Type" OF
          "Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases":
            BEGIN
              CASE "Document Type" OF
                "Document Type"::Inquiry:
                  PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Parts Purchase Inquiry",PurchHdrL);
                "Document Type"::Order:
                  PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Parts Purchase Order",PurchHdrL);
                "Document Type"::Invoice:
                  PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Parts Purchase Invoice",PurchHdrL);
                "Document Type"::"Return Order":
                  PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Purchase Return Order",PurchHdrL);
                "Document Type"::"Credit Memo":
                  PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Parts Purchase Credit Memo",PurchHdrL);
              END;
            END;
          "Order Type"::Service:
            BEGIN
              CASE "Document Type" OF
                "Document Type"::Inquiry:
                  PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Vehicle Purch. Inquiry",PurchHdrL);
                "Document Type"::Order:
                  PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Serv. Purchase Order",PurchHdrL);
                "Document Type"::Invoice:
                  PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Vehicle Purchase Invoice",PurchHdrL);
                "Document Type"::"Credit Memo":
                  PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Serv. Purch. Credit Memo",PurchHdrL);
              END;
            END;
          ELSE
            CASE "Document Type" OF
              "Document Type"::Inquiry:
                PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Vehicle Purch. Inquiry",PurchHdrL);
              "Document Type"::Order:
                PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Vehicle Purchase Order",PurchHdrL);
              "Document Type"::Invoice:
                PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Vehicle Purchase Invoice",PurchHdrL);
              "Document Type"::"Return Order":
                PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Vehicle Purchase Return Order",PurchHdrL);
              "Document Type"::"Credit Memo":
                PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Vehicle Purchase Credit Memo",PurchHdrL);
            END;
        END;
      // Stop PA036549.33628
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetOptionPrice@5025351();
    VAR
      OptionVariantL@1109400000 : Record 5025424;
      PurchPriceNewL@1109400001 : Decimal;
      PurchAmountNewL@1109400002 : Decimal;
      SalPriceNewL@1109400003 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      OptionVariantL.SETRANGE(Area,OptionVariantL.Area::Purchase);
      OptionVariantL.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type");
      OptionVariantL.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
      OptionVariantL.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", "Line No.");
      PurchPriceNewL := 0;
      PurchAmountNewL := 0;
      SalPriceNewL := 0;
      IF OptionVariantL.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          PurchPriceNewL := PurchPriceNewL + OptionVariantL."Direct Unit Cost";
          PurchAmountNewL := PurchAmountNewL + OptionVariantL.Amount;
          SalPriceNewL := SalPriceNewL + (OptionVariantL."Unit Price (LCY)");
        UNTIL OptionVariantL.NEXT = 0;

        "Direct Unit Cost" := PurchPriceNewL;
        Amount := PurchAmountNewL;

        NotToOptionTableG := TRUE;
        VALIDATE("Unit Price (LCY)",SalPriceNewL);
        IF Amount <> 0 THEN
          VALIDATE(Amount);
        NotToOptionTableG := FALSE;
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE DiscountOnOptionTable@5025352();
    VAR
      OptionVariantL@1109400000 : Record 5025424;
      TotalPruchAmountL@1109400001 : Decimal;
      PurchAmountInLineL@1109400002 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF NOT NotToOptionTableG THEN BEGIN
        OptionVariantL.SETRANGE(Area,OptionVariantL.Area::Purchase);
        OptionVariantL.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type");
        OptionVariantL.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
        OptionVariantL.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", "Line No.");
        OptionVariantL.SETRANGE(Type,OptionVariantL.Type::Vehicle,OptionVariantL.Type::"Manuf. Option");
        OptionVariantL.SETFILTER("Direct Unit Cost (LCY)",'>0');
        TotalPruchAmountL := 0;
        IF OptionVariantL.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
          REPEAT
            //in case the chaning of the VAT Prod. Posting Group changes the handling of tax
            OptionVariantL."VAT %" := "VAT %";
            IF "VAT Calculation Type" = "VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax" THEN
              OptionVariantL."Differential Taxation" := TRUE
            ELSE
              OptionVariantL."Differential Taxation" := FALSE;
            OptionVariantL.VALIDATE("Line Discount %", "Line Discount %");
            CheckOptionVATBaseAmount(OptionVariantL,CurrFieldNo);
            TotalPruchAmountL := TotalPruchAmountL + OptionVariantL.Amount;
            OptionVariantL.MODIFY;
          UNTIL OptionVariantL.NEXT = 0;
          PurchAmountInLineL := Amount;
          IF (PurchAmountInLineL <> TotalPruchAmountL) AND OptionVariantL.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
            OptionVariantL.VALIDATE(Amount, OptionVariantL.Amount - (PurchAmountInLineL - TotalPruchAmountL));
            OptionVariantL.MODIFY;
          END;
        END ELSE BEGIN
          OptionVariantL.SETRANGE(Type,OptionVariantL.Type::Vehicle);
          OptionVariantL.SETRANGE("Direct Unit Cost (LCY)");
          IF OptionVariantL.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
            OptionVariantL."VAT %" := "VAT %";
            OptionVariantL."Line Discount %" := "Line Discount %";
            IF "Currency Code" = '' THEN BEGIN
              OptionVariantL."Direct Unit Cost (LCY)" := "Direct Unit Cost";
              OptionVariantL."Line Discount Amount (LCY)" := "Line Discount Amount";
              OptionVariantL."Amount (LCY)" := Amount;
              OptionVariantL."Amount Incl. VAT (LCY)" := "Amount Including VAT";
              OptionVariantL."VAT Amount (LCY)" := "Amount Including VAT" - Amount;
              OptionVariantL."Direct Unit Cost" := "Direct Unit Cost";
              OptionVariantL."Line Discount Amount" := "Line Discount Amount";
              OptionVariantL.Amount := Amount;
              OptionVariantL."Amount Including VAT" := "Amount Including VAT";
              OptionVariantL."VAT Amount" := "Amount Including VAT" - Amount;
            END ELSE BEGIN
              GetPurchHeader();
              OptionVariantL."Direct Unit Cost (LCY)" := CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtFCYToLCY(
                PurchHeader."Posting Date",
                "Currency Code",
                "Direct Unit Cost",
                PurchHeader."Currency Factor");
              OptionVariantL."Line Discount Amount (LCY)" := CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtFCYToLCY(
                PurchHeader."Posting Date",
                "Currency Code",
                "Line Discount Amount",
                PurchHeader."Currency Factor");
              OptionVariantL."Amount (LCY)" := CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtFCYToLCY(
                PurchHeader."Posting Date",
                "Currency Code",
                Amount,
                PurchHeader."Currency Factor");
              OptionVariantL."Amount Incl. VAT (LCY)" := CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtFCYToLCY(
                PurchHeader."Posting Date",
                "Currency Code",
                "Amount Including VAT",
                PurchHeader."Currency Factor");
              OptionVariantL."VAT Amount (LCY)" := CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtFCYToLCY(
                PurchHeader."Posting Date",
                "Currency Code",
                ("Amount Including VAT" - Amount),
                PurchHeader."Currency Factor");
              OptionVariantL."Direct Unit Cost" := "Direct Unit Cost";
              OptionVariantL."Line Discount Amount" := "Line Discount Amount";
              OptionVariantL.Amount := Amount;
              OptionVariantL."Amount Including VAT" := "Amount Including VAT";
              OptionVariantL."VAT Amount" := "Amount Including VAT" - Amount;
            END;
            OptionVariantL.CalcAmounts;
            OptionVariantL.MODIFY;
          END;
        END;

        // Start  - Forces updates of correct Foreign Exchange amounts if changed. INC
        IF "Currency Code" <> '' THEN BEGIN
          OptionVariantL.RESET;
          OptionVariantL.SETRANGE(Area,OptionVariantL.Area::Purchase);
          OptionVariantL.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type");
          OptionVariantL.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
          OptionVariantL.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", "Line No.");
          OptionVariantL.SETRANGE(Type,OptionVariantL.Type::Vehicle,OptionVariantL.Type::"Manuf. Option");
          // Start PA043248
          //IF OptionVariantL.FINDSET(TRUE) THEN // FINDSET error if records is modified in the meantime elsewhere (Invoice rounding)
          IF OptionVariantL.FINDFIRST THEN // Minimize the time between read and modify
          // Stop PA043248
            REPEAT
              OptionVariantL.CalcAmounts;
              OptionVariantL.MODIFY;
            UNTIL OptionVariantL.NEXT = 0;
        END;
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetBookNo@5025353();
    VAR
      NoSeriesMgtL@1109400000 : Codeunit 396;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      //can be deleted because the book no. should be first pulled during posting.
      VehicleSetupG.GET;
      IF VehicleSetupG."Automatic Posting Nos." THEN BEGIN
        VehicleSetupG.TESTFIELD("Book Nos.");
        NoSeriesMgtL.InitSeries(VehicleSetupG."Book Nos.",xRec."Book No. Series",0D,"Book No.","Book No. Series");
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckBookNo@5025354();
    VAR
      PurchLineL@1109400000 : Record 39;
      VehicleL@1109400001 : Record 5025400;
      VehicleLedgEntryL@1109400002 : Record 5025405;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type"::Order, "Document Type"::Invoice);
      PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Item Type","Item Type"::Vehicle);
      PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Book No.", "Book No.");
      IF NOT PurchLineL.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
        VehicleL.SETCURRENTKEY(VIN);
        IF VIN = '' THEN BEGIN
          VehicleG.SETCURRENTKEY("Current Book No.");
          VehicleG.SETRANGE("Current Book No.", "Book No.");
          IF VehicleG.FINDFIRST THEN
            VIN := VehicleG.VIN
          ELSE
            ERROR(C_INC015);
        END ELSE
          IF NOT VehicleL.GET(VIN) THEN
            ERROR(C_INC008);
        PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type"::Order, "Document Type"::Invoice);  //Vehicle is currently being bought
        PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Item Type","Item Type"::Vehicle);
        PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Book No.");
        PurchLineL.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
        IF PurchLineL.FINDFIRST THEN
          "Book No." := PurchLineL."Book No.";
        VehicleLedgEntryL.SETCURRENTKEY(VIN);
        VehicleLedgEntryL.SETRANGE(VIN,VIN);
        VehicleLedgEntryL.SETRANGE("Book No.","Book No.");
        VehicleLedgEntryL.SETRANGE("Entry Type", VehicleLedgEntryL."Entry Type"::Sale);
        IF NOT VehicleLedgEntryL.ISEMPTY THEN
          ERROR(C_INC010);
      END ELSE
        IF VIN = '' THEN
          VIN := PurchLineL.VIN
        ELSE
          IF PurchLineL.VIN <> VIN THEN
            ERROR(C_INC009);
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE NoOnLookUp@5025355(VAR TextP@1109400000 : Text[260];VAR ItemP@1101286982 : Record 27) Change : Boolean;
    VAR
      DataL@1109400002 : Record 5600;
      StandardTextsL@1109400004 : Record 7;
      GLAccL@1109400005 : Record 15;
      VendMakeL@1109400006 : Record 5028684;
      ItemCharge@5045500 : Record 5800;
      GLAccountsListL@1109400007 : Page 18;
    BEGIN
      // @ Performs a lookup and fills TextP and buffer records that are passed as parameters by VAR
      // @ TextP - Text[250]
      // @ ItemP - Buffer Record Item
      // @ retval ChangeR - boolean

      // Start INC
      GetPurchHeader();
      CASE Type OF
      // Start PA034531.I001184
        Type::Item:
          BEGIN
            ItemP.SETCURRENTKEY("Item Type","Make Code","No.");
            VendMakeL.GetVendorMakeFilter(PurchHeader."Buy-from Vendor No.");
            VendMakeL.COPYFILTER("Make Code", ItemP."Make Code");
      // Start PA041023
            IF PurchHeader."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code" <> '' THEN
              ItemP.SETFILTER("Make Code",'%1|%2',PurchHeader."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code",'');
      // Stop PA041023
            IF NOT ItemP.GET(TextP) THEN
              IF NOT ItemP.FINDFIRST() THEN
                ItemP.INIT;
            CASE "Item Type" OF
              "Item Type"::Vehicle:
                BEGIN
                  IF NOT ItemP.GET(TextP) THEN
                    IF NOT ItemP.FINDFIRST() THEN
                      ItemP.INIT;
                  IF ItemP.VehModelLookupWithMaster() THEN BEGIN
                    TextP := ItemP."No.";
                    Change := TRUE;
                  END;
                END;

              "Item Type"::"Veh. Transfer":
                BEGIN
                  IF NOT ItemP.GET(TextP) THEN
                    IF NOT ItemP.FINDFIRST() THEN
                      ItemP.INIT;
                  IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Transfer Fees List",ItemP) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
                    TextP := ItemP."No.";
                    Change := TRUE;
                  END;
                END;

              "Item Type":: Item:
                BEGIN
      // Start EU.0114065
                  IF PurchHeader."General Document" THEN BEGIN
                    ItemP.FILTERGROUP(2);
                    ItemP.SETRANGE("No Inventory Tracking",TRUE);
                    ItemP.FILTERGROUP(0);
                  END;
      // Stop EU.0114065
                  IF NOT ItemP.GET(TextP) THEN
                    IF NOT ItemP.FINDFIRST() THEN
                      ItemP.INIT;
                  IF PurchHeader."Campaign No." <> '' THEN BEGIN
                    IF ItemP.CampaignLookup(PurchHeader."Campaign No.",PurchHeader."Location Code") THEN BEGIN
                      TextP := ItemP."No.";
                      Change := TRUE;
                    END;
                  END ELSE
                    IF ItemP.LookupWithMaster() THEN BEGIN
                      TextP := ItemP."No.";
                      Change := TRUE;
                    END;
                END;
            END;
          END;
      // Stop PA034531.I001184
        Type::"Account (G/L)":
          BEGIN
            IF CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO("No.") THEN
              CheckAttachedToServiceOrder(FIELDCAPTION("No."));
            IF GLAccL.GET(TextP) THEN
      // Start PA035942
              GLAccountsListL.SETRECORD(GLAccL);
            CASE "Order Type" OF
              "Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases":
                GLAccountsListL.Def(UserGLAccG.Area::"Parts Purchases");
              "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases":
                GLAccountsListL.Def(UserGLAccG.Area::"Vehicle Purchases");
              "Order Type"::Service:
                GLAccountsListL.Def(UserGLAccG.Area::"Service Purchases");
      // Stop PA035942
            END;
            GLAccountsListL.LOOKUPMODE(TRUE);
            IF GLAccountsListL.RUNMODAL = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
              GLAccountsListL.GETRECORD(GLAccL);
      // Start PA034531.I001184
      // Stop PA034531.I001184
              TextP := GLAccL."No.";
              Change := TRUE;
            END;
          END;
        Type::" ":
          BEGIN
            IF StandardTextsL.GET(TextP) THEN
              ;
            IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(0, StandardTextsL) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
              TextP := StandardTextsL.Code;
              Change := TRUE;
            END;
          END;

        Type::"Fixed Asset":
          BEGIN
            IF DataL.GET(TextP) THEN
              ;
            IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(0, DataL) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
              TextP := DataL."No.";
              Change := TRUE;
            END;
          END;

        Type::"Charge (Item)":
          BEGIN
            IF ItemCharge.GET(TextP) THEN
              ;
            IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(0, ItemCharge) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
              TextP := ItemCharge."No.";
              Change := TRUE;
            END;
          END;
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE SalPriceToOptionTable@5025356();
    VAR
      TotalamountL@1109400000 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF NOT NotToOptionTableG THEN BEGIN
        OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type");
        OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document No.", "Document No.");
        OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", "Line No.");
        OptionVariantG.SETRANGE(Type, OptionVariantG.Type::Vehicle, OptionVariantG.Type::"Manuf. Option");
        OptionVariantG.SETRANGE(Area, OptionVariantG.Area::Purchase);
        OptionVariantG.SETFILTER("Unit Price (LCY)",'>0');
        IF OptionVariantG.COUNT > 1 THEN BEGIN
          IF OptionVariantG.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
            REPEAT
              TotalamountL += OptionVariantG."Direct Unit Cost";
            UNTIL OptionVariantG.NEXT = 0;
            IF TotalamountL <> "Direct Unit Cost" THEN
              ERROR(C_INC023);
          END;
        END;
        IF OptionVariantG.COUNT = 0 THEN BEGIN
          OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Unit Price (LCY)");
          IF OptionVariantG.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
            OptionVariantG."Unit Price Incl. VAT (LCY)" := "Unit Price Incl. VAT (LCY)";
            OptionVariantG."Unit Price (LCY)" := "Unit Price (LCY)";
            OptionVariantG."Unit Price" := OptionVariantG.CalcAmountInFCY("Unit Price (LCY)");
            OptionVariantG."Unit Price Incl. VAT" := OptionVariantG.CalcAmountInFCY("Unit Price Incl. VAT (LCY)");
            OptionVariantG.MODIFY;
          END;
        END;
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckExclusiveDiffTax@5025357();
    VAR
      PurchLineL@1109400000 : Record 39;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
      PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
      IF "Line No." <> 0 THEN
        PurchLineL.SETFILTER("Line No.", '<>%1', "Line No.");
      PurchLineL.SETFILTER("Item Type",'<>%1',"Item Type"::" ");
      IF "Item Type" <> "Item Type"::" " THEN
        IF "VAT Calculation Type" = "VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax" THEN BEGIN
          IF ("Item Type" <> "Item Type"::Vehicle) AND ("Item Type" <> "Item Type"::"Charge (Item)") THEN
            ERROR(C_INC027);
          PurchLineL.SETFILTER("VAT Calculation Type", '<>%1', PurchLineL."VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax");
          IF PurchLineL.FINDFIRST THEN
            ERROR(C_INC028);
        END ELSE BEGIN
          PurchLineL.SETFILTER("VAT Calculation Type", '=%1', PurchLineL."VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax");
          IF PurchLineL.FINDFIRST THEN
            ERROR(C_INC028);
        END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CheckAttachedToServiceOrder@5025358(FieldCaptionP@1109400000 : Text[50]);
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF CurrFieldNo <> 0 THEN
        IF ("Service Order No." <> '') OR ("Service Order Line No." <> 0) THEN
          IF FieldCaptionP = '' THEN
            ERROR(C_INC030, "Document Type","Service Order No.")
          ELSE
            ERROR(C_INC029, FieldCaptionP,"Document Type","Service Order No.");
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckAssignedSalLine@5025359(FieldCaptionP@1109400000 : Text[50]);
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      LinkedSalLineG.SETCURRENTKEY("From Purch. Document Type","From Purch. Document No.");
      LinkedSalLineG.SETRANGE("From Purch. Document Type","Document Type");
      LinkedSalLineG.SETRANGE("From Purch. Document No.","Document No.");
      LinkedSalLineG.SETRANGE("From Purch. Line No.","Line No.");
      IF LinkedSalLineG.COUNT = 1 THEN BEGIN
        LinkedSalLineG.FINDFIRST;
        ERROR(C_INC035,FieldCaptionP,LinkedSalLineG."Document Type",LinkedSalLineG."Document No.",LinkedSalLineG."Line No.");
      END ELSE
        IF LinkedSalLineG.COUNT > 1 THEN
          ERROR(C_INC036);
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE NewPriceDeterm@5025361();
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      // If item line, then get the standard purchase price
      IF Type = Type::Item THEN BEGIN
        GetItem();
        UpdateDirectUnitCost();
        VALIDATE("Direct Unit Cost");
        "List Price (LCY)" := Item."List Price (LCY)";
        // Recalculate Document Campaign Lines
        FillDocCampLines();
        // Redetermine Quantity Disc.
        "Quantity Disc. %" := 0;
        ItemPurchQtyDisc.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
        ItemPurchQtyDisc.SETRANGE("Vendor No.","Buy-from Vendor No.");
        ItemPurchQtyDisc.SETRANGE("Minimum Quantity",0,ABS("Quantity (Base)"));
        GetPurchHeader();
        ItemPurchQtyDisc.SETRANGE("Purch. Order Type",PurchHeader."Purch. Order Type");
        ItemPurchQtyDisc.SETRANGE("Valid-From Date",0D,PurchHeader."Order Date");
        ItemPurchQtyDisc.SETFILTER("Valid-To Date",'=%1|>=%2',0D,PurchHeader."Order Date");
        IF ItemPurchQtyDisc.FINDLAST THEN
          "Quantity Disc. %" := ItemPurchQtyDisc."Discount %"
        ELSE
          IF PurchHeader."Purch. Order Type" <> '' THEN BEGIN
            ItemPurchQtyDisc.SETRANGE("Purch. Order Type",'');
            IF ItemPurchQtyDisc.FINDLAST THEN
              "Quantity Disc. %" := ItemPurchQtyDisc."Discount %";
          END;
        VALIDATE("Quantity Disc. %");
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetDepartment@5025362();
    VAR
      LocationL@1109400000 : Record 14;
      PartsDeptL@1109400001 : Record 5028666;
      VehSalesDeptL@1109400002 : Record 5028667;
      GLAccL@1109400003 : Record 15;
      ServDeptL@1055600 : Record 5028668;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      // Start PA036002.26254
      "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := '';
      // Stop PA036002.26254
      GetPurchHeader();
      IF (Type <> Type::" ") AND ("Location Code" <> '') THEN BEGIN
        LocationL.GET("Location Code");
      // Start PA041187.85979
        IF "Order Type" = "Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases" THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA041187.85979
          PartsDeptL.SETRANGE("Location Code","Location Code");
          CASE Type OF
            Type::Item:
              PartsDeptL.SETRANGE("Line Type",PartsDeptL."Line Type"::Item);
            Type::"Account (G/L)":
      // Start PA036002.26254
              BEGIN
                IF GLAccL.GET("No.") THEN BEGIN
                  IF GLAccL."Global Dimension 1 Code" <> '' THEN
                    "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := GLAccL."Global Dimension 1 Code";
                 END;
      // Stop PA036002.26254
                PartsDeptL.SETRANGE("Line Type",PartsDeptL."Line Type"::"G/L Account");
      // Start PA036002.26254
              END;
      // Stop PA036002.26254
            Type::"Charge (Item)":
              PartsDeptL.SETRANGE("Line Type",PartsDeptL."Line Type"::"Charge (Item)");
          END;
      // Start PA036002.26254
          IF "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" = '' THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA036002.26254
            IF PartsDeptL.FINDFIRST AND (PartsDeptL."Department Code" <> '') THEN
              "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := PartsDeptL."Department Code"
            ELSE
              IF LocationL."Department Code" <> '' THEN
                "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := LocationL."Department Code"
              ELSE
                "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := PurchHeader."Shortcut Dimension 1 Code";
      // Start PA036002.26254
          END;
      // Stop PA036002.26254
        END ELSE
          IF "Order Type" = "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases" THEN BEGIN
            VehSalesDeptL.SETRANGE("Location Code","Location Code");
            CASE "Item Type" OF
              "Item Type"::Item:
                VehSalesDeptL.SETRANGE("Line Type",VehSalesDeptL."Line Type"::Item);
              "Item Type"::"G/L Account":
      // Start PA036002.26254
                BEGIN
                  IF GLAccL.GET("No.") THEN BEGIN
                    IF GLAccL."Global Dimension 1 Code" <> '' THEN
                      "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := GLAccL."Global Dimension 1 Code";
                   END;
      // Stop PA036002.26254
                  VehSalesDeptL.SETRANGE("Line Type",VehSalesDeptL."Line Type"::"G/L Account");
      // Start PA036002.26254
                END;
      // Stop PA036002.26254
              "Item Type"::Vehicle:
                VehSalesDeptL.SETRANGE("Line Type",VehSalesDeptL."Line Type"::Vehicle);
              "Item Type"::"Veh. Transfer":
                VehSalesDeptL.SETRANGE("Line Type",VehSalesDeptL."Line Type"::"Veh. Transfer");
              "Item Type"::"Charge (Item)":
      // Start PA034482
                BEGIN
                  VehSalesDeptL.SETRANGE("Line Type",VehSalesDeptL."Line Type"::"Charge (Item)");
                  VehSalesDeptL.SETRANGE("Vehicle Status", VehStatusG - 1);
                END;
            END;
            IF "Item Type" <> "Item Type"::"Charge (Item)" THEN
      // Start PA040070.62779
              CASE "Vehicle Status" OF
                "Vehicle Status"::"New Vehicle":
                  VehSalesDeptL.SETRANGE("Vehicle Status", VehSalesDeptL."Vehicle Status"::"New Vehicle");
                "Vehicle Status"::"Used Vehicle":
                  VehSalesDeptL.SETRANGE("Vehicle Status", VehSalesDeptL."Vehicle Status"::"Used Vehicle");
                "Vehicle Status"::"Demo Vehicle":
                  VehSalesDeptL.SETRANGE("Vehicle Status", VehSalesDeptL."Vehicle Status"::"Demo Vehicle");
              END;
      // Start PA040070.62779
      // Stop PA034482
      // Start PA036002.26254
            IF "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" = '' THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA036002.26254
              IF VehSalesDeptL.FINDFIRST AND (VehSalesDeptL."Department Code" <> '') THEN
                "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := VehSalesDeptL."Department Code"
              ELSE
                IF LocationL."Department Code" <> '' THEN
                  "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := LocationL."Department Code"
                ELSE
                  "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := PurchHeader."Shortcut Dimension 1 Code";
      // Start PA036002.26254
            END;
      // Stop PA036002.26254
      // Start PA041187.85979
          END ELSE
            IF "Order Type" = "Order Type"::Service THEN BEGIN
              ServDeptL.SETRANGE("Location Code","Location Code");
              CASE Type OF
                Type::Item:
                  ServDeptL.SETRANGE("Line Type",ServDeptL."Line Type"::Item);
                Type::"Account (G/L)":
                  BEGIN
                    IF GLAccL.GET("No.") THEN BEGIN
                      IF GLAccL."Global Dimension 1 Code" <> '' THEN
                        "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := GLAccL."Global Dimension 1 Code";
                     END;
                    ServDeptL.SETRANGE("Line Type",ServDeptL."Line Type"::"G/L Account");
                  END;
              END;
              IF "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" = '' THEN
                IF ServDeptL.FINDFIRST AND (ServDeptL."Department Code" <> '') THEN
                  "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := ServDeptL."Department Code"
                ELSE
                  IF LocationL."Department Code" <> '' THEN
                    "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := LocationL."Department Code"
                  ELSE
                    "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := PurchHeader."Shortcut Dimension 1 Code";
            END;
      // Stop PA041187.85979
      END ELSE
        "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := PurchHeader."Shortcut Dimension 1 Code";
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE LocationCodeLookUp@5025363(VAR TextP@1109400000 : Text[250]) Change : Boolean;
    VAR
      UserLocationL@1101224019 : Record 5028664;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      // Start PA036118
      UserLocationL.FILTERGROUP(2);
      UserLocationL.SETRANGE("User ID",USERID);
      UserLocationL.FILTERGROUP(0);
      // Start PA045273
      IF NOT UserLocationL.GET("Location Code") THEN
        UserLocationL.INIT;
      // Stop PA045273
      IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(0, UserLocationL) <> ACTION::LookupOK THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      TextP := UserLocationL."Location Code";
      EXIT(TRUE);
      // Stop PA036118
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE SetAmountsToZero@5025364();
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      CLEAR(OptionVariantG);
      OptionVariantG.SETRANGE(Area, OptionVariantG.Area::Purchase);
      OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type");
      OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document No.", "Document No.");
      OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", "Line No.");
      OptionVariantG.SETRANGE(Type, OptionVariantG.Type::Vehicle, OptionVariantG.Type::"Manuf. Option");
      IF OptionVariantG.FINDSET(TRUE) THEN
