          OptionVariantG."Direct Unit Cost (LCY)" := 0;
          OptionVariantG."Unit Price (LCY)" := 0;
          OptionVariantG."Unit Price Incl. VAT (LCY)" := 0;
          OptionVariantG."Line Discount %" := 0;
          OptionVariantG."Line Discount Amount (LCY)" := 0;
          OptionVariantG."Amount (LCY)" := 0;
          OptionVariantG."Amount Incl. VAT (LCY)" := 0;
          OptionVariantG."Direct Unit Cost" := 0;
          OptionVariantG."Unit Price" := 0;
          OptionVariantG."Unit Price Incl. VAT" := 0;
          OptionVariantG."VAT Amount" := 0;
          OptionVariantG."Line Discount Amount" := 0;
          OptionVariantG.Amount := 0;
          OptionVariantG."Amount Including VAT" := 0;
          OptionVariantG."Price Calc. Valid from" := 0D;
          OptionVariantG."Price Calc. Valid to" := 0D;
          OptionVariantG."Price Calc. Price Base" := 0;
          OptionVariantG."Price Calc. Price Category" := '';
          OptionVariantG."Price Calc. Price" := 0;
          OptionVariantG."Price Calc. Surcharge %" := 0;
          OptionVariantG."Price Calc. Discount %" := 0;
          OptionVariantG."Manual Surcharge %" := 0;
          OptionVariantG."Manual Discount %" := 0;
          OptionVariantG."Discounted Unit Price" := 0;
          OptionVariantG."Customer Unit Price" := 0;
          OptionVariantG."Total Variance %" := 0;
          OptionVariantG."Unit Cost" := 0;
          OptionVariantG."Rem. Margin %" := 0;
          OptionVariantG."Changed by User ID" := '';
          OptionVariantG."Date Modified" := 0D;
          OptionVariantG."Time of Change" := 0T;
          OptionVariantG.VALIDATE(Quantity);
          OptionVariantG.MODIFY;
        UNTIL OptionVariantG.NEXT = 0;

      "Direct Unit Cost" := 0;
      "Unit Cost (LCY)" := 0;
      "Quantity Disc. %" := 0;
      "Line Discount %" := 0;
      "Line Discount Amount" := 0;
      Amount := 0;
      "Amount Including VAT" := 0;
      "Unit Price (LCY)" := 0;
      VALIDATE(Quantity);
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE PullPPG@5025365();
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      VehicleSetupG.GET;
      IF "Gen. Bus. Posting Group" = VehicleSetupG."Private Business Posting Group" THEN BEGIN
        VehicleSetupG.TESTFIELD("Prod Post Grp Differential Tax"); //Private always taxed with diferential tax
        VALIDATE("Gen. Prod. Posting Group", VehicleSetupG."Prod Post Grp Differential Tax");
      END ELSE
        IF "Vehicle Status" = "Vehicle Status"::"Used Vehicle" THEN BEGIN
          VehicleSetupG.TESTFIELD("Used Veh. Prod. Post. Group");  //Used vehicles from non-privates
          VALIDATE("Gen. Prod. Posting Group", VehicleSetupG."Used Veh. Prod. Post. Group");
        END ELSE
          IF "Vehicle Status" = "Vehicle Status"::"Demo Vehicle" THEN BEGIN
            VehicleSetupG.TESTFIELD("Demo Veh. Prod. Post. Group");  //Demo vehicles from non-private
            VALIDATE("Gen. Prod. Posting Group", VehicleSetupG."Demo Veh. Prod. Post. Group");
          END ELSE BEGIN  //New Vehicles from non-privates
            Item.GET("No.");
            VALIDATE("Gen. Prod. Posting Group", Item."Gen. Prod. Posting Group");
          END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE VINLookup@5025366(VAR TextP@1109400000 : Text) : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // Start PA044975
      EXIT(VehicleLookup(TextP,FIELDNO(VIN)));
      // Stop PA044975
    END;

    PROCEDURE VehicleLookup@1055610(VAR TextP@1109400000 : Text;FieldIDP@1055600 : Integer) : Boolean;
    VAR
      VehicleL@1109400001 : Record 5025400;
      VendL@1109400004 : Record 23;
      PurchHdrL@1109400003 : Record 38;
    BEGIN
      // Start PA044975
      IF "Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Return Order","Document Type"::"Credit Memo"] THEN
        IF "Quantity Received" = 0 THEN
          VehicleL.SETFILTER("Vehicle Status",'%1|%2|%3',
            VehicleL."Vehicle Status"::"New Vehicle",
            VehicleL."Vehicle Status"::"Used Vehicle",
            VehicleL."Vehicle Status"::"Demo Vehicle")
        ELSE
          VehicleL.SETFILTER("Vehicle Status",'%1|%2|%3|%4',
            VehicleL."Vehicle Status"::"Customer Vehicle",
            VehicleL."Vehicle Status"::"Prospect Vehicle",
            VehicleL."Vehicle Status"::"Consignment Vehicle",
            VehicleL."Vehicle Status"::"Rental Vehicle")
      ELSE BEGIN
        IF "Quantity Received" = 0 THEN
          VehicleL.SETFILTER("Vehicle Status",'%1|%2|%3|%4',
            VehicleL."Vehicle Status"::"Customer Vehicle",
            VehicleL."Vehicle Status"::"Prospect Vehicle",
            VehicleL."Vehicle Status"::"Consignment Vehicle",
            VehicleL."Vehicle Status"::"Rental Vehicle")
        ELSE
          VehicleL.SETFILTER("Vehicle Status",'%1|%2|%3',
            VehicleL."Vehicle Status"::"New Vehicle",
            VehicleL."Vehicle Status"::"Used Vehicle",
            VehicleL."Vehicle Status"::"Demo Vehicle");
      END;

      // Start PA042846
      PurchHdrL.GET("Document Type","Document No.");
      IF VendL.GET(PurchHdrL."Buy-from Vendor No.") THEN BEGIN
        IF VendL.IsTradeInVend() AND (PurchHdrL."Trade-In Customer No." > '') THEN BEGIN
          VehicleL.SETRANGE("Customer No.",PurchHdrL."Trade-In Customer No.");
        END;
      END;
      // Stop PA042846
      CASE FieldIDP OF
        FIELDNO(VIN):
          IF NOT VehicleL.GET(VIN) THEN
            VehicleL.INIT;
        FIELDNO("License No."):
          IF "License No." <> '' THEN
            VehicleL.SETRANGE("License No.","License No.");
      END;
      IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(0, VehicleL) <> ACTION::LookupOK THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      CASE FieldIDP OF
        FIELDNO(VIN):
          TextP := VehicleL.VIN;
        FIELDNO("License No."):
          TextP := VehicleL."License No.";
      END;
      EXIT(TRUE);
      // Stop PA044975
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckMaster@5025367();
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      // Start PA036118
      GetPurchHeader();
      // Stop PA036118
      CASE "Item Type" OF
        "Item Type"::Item:
      // Start PA033958
          BEGIN
      // Stop PA033958
      // Start PA043248
      // Start PA042350
      // Start PA041187.91834
            "No." := Item.ItemSearch("No.",PurchHeader."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code",1);
      // Stop PA041187.91834
      // Stop PA042350
      // Stop PA043248
      // Start PA033958
      // Start PA044817
      // Stop PA044817
          END;
      // Stop PA033958
        "Item Type"::Vehicle:
          "No." := Item.VehicleModelSearch("No.",PurchHeader."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code");
      END;
      IF (CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO(Type)) OR (CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO("No.")) THEN BEGIN
        IF Type = Type::"Account (G/L)" THEN BEGIN
          CASE "Order Type" OF
            "Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases":
              "No." := UserGLAccG.FindGLAccount("No.", UserGLAccG.Area::"Parts Purchases",USERID);
            "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases":
              "No." := UserGLAccG.FindGLAccount("No.", UserGLAccG.Area::"Vehicle Purchases",USERID);
            "Order Type"::Service:
              "No." := UserGLAccG.FindGLAccount("No.", UserGLAccG.Area::"Service Purchases",USERID);
          END;
        END;
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE InsertLineNoDistance@5025368(NoOfLinesNeededP@1109400000 : Integer;AbortOnErrorP@1109400001 : Boolean) StepValR : Integer;
    VAR
      ErrorTextL@1109400002 : Text[250];
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      PurchLine2.RESET;
      PurchLine2.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
      PurchLine2.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
      PurchLine2 := Rec;
      IF PurchLine2.FIND('>') THEN BEGIN
        StepValR := (PurchLine2."Line No." - "Line No.") DIV (1 + NoOfLinesNeededP);
        IF StepValR = 0 THEN BEGIN
          ErrorTextL := STRSUBSTNO(C_INC017,
            TABLECAPTION,
            FIELDCAPTION("Document Type"),
            "Document Type",
            FIELDCAPTION("Document No."),
            "Document No.","Line No.",
            PurchLine2."Line No.");
          IF AbortOnErrorP THEN
            ERROR(ErrorTextL)
          ELSE
            MESSAGE(ErrorTextL);
        END;
      END ELSE
        StepValR := 10000;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE TransferToSalAssignment@5025369();
    VAR
      ReservEntryL@1109400000 : Record 337;
      LinkedSalLineL@1109400001 : Record 37;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      LinkedSalLineL.SETCURRENTKEY("From Purch. Document Type","From Purch. Document No.");
      LinkedSalLineL.SETRANGE("From Purch. Document Type","Document Type");
      LinkedSalLineL.SETRANGE("From Purch. Document No.","Document No.");
      LinkedSalLineL.SETRANGE("From Purch. Line No.","Line No.");
      // Start PA043637
      LinkedSalLineL.SETRANGE("Item Type", "Item Type"::Vehicle);
      // Stop PA043637
      IF LinkedSalLineL.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          LinkedSalLineL."Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code";
      // Start PA035597
          LinkedSalLineL.ValidateShortcutDimCode(1,LinkedSalLineL."Shortcut Dimension 1 Code");
      // Stop PA035597
          LinkedSalLineL."Vehicle Status" := "Vehicle Status";
          IF LinkedSalLineL."Gen. Prod. Posting Group" <> "Gen. Prod. Posting Group" THEN BEGIN
            IF CONFIRM(C_INC064,FALSE,LinkedSalLineL."Document Type",LinkedSalLineL."Document No.") THEN
              LinkedSalLineL.VALIDATE("Gen. Prod. Posting Group","Gen. Prod. Posting Group")
            ELSE
              ERROR(C_INC065);
          END;
          LinkedSalLineL.MODIFY(TRUE);
        UNTIL LinkedSalLineL.NEXT = 0;
      END;
      CLEAR(LinkedSalLineL);
      IF "Reserved Quantity" <> 0 THEN BEGIN
        ReservEntryL.SETCURRENTKEY("Reservation Status","From Type","From Subtype","From ID",
          "From Batch Name","From Prod. Order Line","From Ref. No.","Shipment Date");
        ReservEntryL.SETRANGE("Reservation Status",ReservEntryL."Reservation Status"::Open);
        ReservEntryL.SETRANGE("From Type",ReservEntryL."From Type"::Purchase);
        ReservEntryL.SETRANGE("From Subtype","Document Type");
        ReservEntryL.SETRANGE("From ID","Document No.");
        ReservEntryL.SETRANGE("From Ref. No.", "Line No.");
        IF ReservEntryL.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
          ReservEntryL."Serial No." := VIN;
          ReservEntryL.MODIFY;
          IF LinkedSalLineL.GET(ReservEntryL."For Subtype",ReservEntryL."For ID",
             ReservEntryL."For Ref. No.")
          THEN BEGIN
            LinkedSalLineL."Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := "Shortcut Dimension 1 Code";
      // Start PA035597
            LinkedSalLineL.ValidateShortcutDimCode(1,LinkedSalLineL."Shortcut Dimension 1 Code");
      // Stop PA035597
            LinkedSalLineL."Vehicle Status" := "Vehicle Status";
            IF LinkedSalLineL."Gen. Prod. Posting Group" <> "Gen. Prod. Posting Group" THEN BEGIN
              IF CONFIRM(C_INC064,FALSE,LinkedSalLineL."Document Type",LinkedSalLineL."Document No.") THEN
                LinkedSalLineL.VALIDATE("Gen. Prod. Posting Group","Gen. Prod. Posting Group")
              ELSE
                ERROR(C_INC065);
            END;
            LinkedSalLineL.MODIFY;
          END;
        END;
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckChangePermision@5025370();
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      // Start PA040959
      IF ("Order Type" <> "Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases") AND ("Order Type" <> "Order Type"::Service) THEN
      // Stop PA040959
        EXIT;
      IF "Cockpit Entry No." <> 0 THEN BEGIN
        IF CockpitHdrG.GET("Cockpit Entry No.") THEN
      // Start PA045443
          IF (CockpitHdrG."Document Type" = CkptPurchMgmtG.CkptOrigDocTypeToDocType(CockpitHdrG."Orig. Document Type")) AND
      // Stop PA045443
             (CockpitHdrG."Processing Status" < CockpitHdrG."Processing Status"::Closed)
          THEN
            ERROR(C_INC066);
      END;
      StatusCheckFunction(FALSE);
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE IsDepositPosition@5025371();
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF ("Attached to Line No." > 0) AND ("Quantity Multiplier" <> 0) THEN BEGIN
        PurchLine2.GET("Document Type", "Document No.", "Attached to Line No.");
        ERROR(C_INC034, PurchLine2.Type, PurchLine2."No.", PurchLine2.Description);
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetNextLineNo@5025372() : Integer;
    VAR
      LastPurchLineL@1109400000 : Record 39;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      LastPurchLineL.LOCKTABLE;
      LastPurchLineL.RESET;
      LastPurchLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
      LastPurchLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
      IF NOT LastPurchLineL.FINDLAST THEN
        CLEAR(LastPurchLineL);
      EXIT(LastPurchLineL."Line No." + 10000);
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdateaAddtlItemQuantity@5025373();

      // Stop PA044975
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdateFieldInAttachedLines@1055609(UpdateFieldNoP@1055600 : Integer);
    VAR
      PurchLineL@1109400000 : Record 39;
      DepItemMakeSetupL@1101257463 : Record 5205395;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      // Start PA043248
      IF SkipUpdateAdditionalItemG THEN
        EXIT;
      // Stop PA043248
      // Start PA044975
      IF "Line No." = 0 THEN
        EXIT;
      PurchLineL.RESET;
      PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
      PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
      PurchLineL.SETFILTER(Type, '<>%1', Type::" ");
      PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Attached to Line No.", "Line No.");
      IF PurchLineL.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          CASE UpdateFieldNoP OF
            FIELDNO(Quantity), FIELDNO("Return Qty. to Ship"), FIELDNO("Qty. to Invoice"), FIELDNO("Qty. to Receive"):
              BEGIN
                IF Quantity = 0 THEN BEGIN
                  PurchLineL.VALIDATE("Qty. to Receive", 0);
                  PurchLineL.VALIDATE("Qty. to Invoice", 0);
                  PurchLineL.VALIDATE("Return Qty. to Ship", 0);
                  IF PurchLineL."Quantity Multiplier" = 0 THEN
                    PurchLineL.VALIDATE(Quantity, PurchLineL."Quantity Received")
                  ELSE
                    PurchLineL.VALIDATE(Quantity, 0);
                END ELSE
                  IF (PurchLineL."Quantity Multiplier" <> 0) OR (PurchLineL.Quantity = 0) THEN
                    PurchLineL.VALIDATE(Quantity, AddtlItemG.CalcPurchQty(Quantity, PurchLineL.Quantity, Rec, PurchLineL));
                IF PurchLineL."Quantity Multiplier" <> 0 THEN
      // Start PA033986
                  IF PurchLineL."Additional Item" <> PurchLineL."Additional Item"::" " THEN
                    IF "Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Return Order", "Document Type"::"Credit Memo"] THEN
                      PurchLineL.VALIDATE("Return Qty. to Ship", AddtlItemG.CalcPurchQty("Return Qty. to Ship", PurchLineL."Return Qty. to Ship", Rec, PurchLineL));
                IF PurchLineL."Quantity Multiplier" <> 0 THEN
                  IF PurchLineL."Additional Item" <> PurchLineL."Additional Item"::" " THEN
                    PurchLineL.VALIDATE("Qty. to Invoice", AddtlItemG.CalcPurchQty("Qty. to Invoice", PurchLineL."Qty. to Invoice", Rec, PurchLineL));
                IF PurchLineL."Quantity Multiplier" <> 0 THEN
                  IF PurchLineL."Additional Item" <> PurchLineL."Additional Item"::" " THEN
                    IF NOT ("Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::"Return Order", "Document Type"::"Credit Memo"]) THEN
                      PurchLineL.VALIDATE("Qty. to Receive", AddtlItemG.CalcPurchQty("Qty. to Receive", PurchLineL."Qty. to Receive", Rec, PurchLineL));
            END;
      // Stop PA044975
          END;
      // Stop PA033986
          PurchLineL.MODIFY;
        UNTIL PurchLineL.NEXT = 0;
      // Stop INC
      // Start PA035101
      DepItemMakeSetupL.CheckDepositPurchLine(Rec);
      // Stop PA035101
    END;

    PROCEDURE NoOnAssistEdit@5025375() : Boolean;
    VAR
      ItemMasterL@1109400000 : Record 5029101;
      VehicleModelMasterL@1109400001 : Record 5029108;
      VendMakeL@1109400002 : Record 5028684;
      CheckMasterRecsL@1109400003 : Codeunit 5029100;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      GetPurchHeader();
      CASE "Item Type" OF
        "Item Type"::Item:
          BEGIN
            VendMakeL.GetVendorMakeFilter(PurchHeader."Buy-from Vendor No.");
            VendMakeL.COPYFILTER("Make Code", ItemMasterL."Make Code");
            IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(0, ItemMasterL) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
      // Start PA032651
      // Start EU.0005642
              UpdatePurchaseLineGlobalDim(Rec, FALSE);
      // Stop EU.0005642
              VALIDATE("No.", CheckMasterRecsL.CheckMasterRecord(ItemMasterL));
      // Stop PA032651
      // Start PA042000
              EXIT(TRUE);
      // Stop PA042000
            END;
          END;
        "Item Type"::Vehicle:
          BEGIN
            VehicleModelMasterL.RESET;
            VendMakeL.GetVendorMakeFilter(PurchHeader."Buy-from Vendor No.");
      // Start PA033476
            VendMakeL.COPYFILTER("Make Code", VehicleModelMasterL."Make Code");
      // Stop PA033476
            IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(0, VehicleModelMasterL) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
              CheckMasterRecsL.CheckVehicleModel(VehicleModelMasterL);
      // Start EU.0005642
              UpdatePurchaseLineGlobalDim(Rec, FALSE);
      // Stop EU.0005642
              VALIDATE("No.", VehicleModelMasterL."No.");
      // Start PA042000
              EXIT(TRUE);
      // Stop PA042000
            END;
          END;
      END;
      // Stop INC
      // Start PA042000
      EXIT(FALSE);
      // Stop PA042000
    END;

    PROCEDURE OnDeleteDeleteSubTables@5025376();
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      OptionVariantG.SETRANGE(Area, OptionVariantG.Area::Purchase);
      OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type");
      OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document No.", "Document No.");
      OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", "Line No.");
      // Start PA036997
      IF NOT OptionVariantG.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
        OptionVariantG.DELETEALL;
        OptionVariantBOMG.DeleteRecordsFromDocument(OptionVariantG.Area::Purchase, "Document Type", "Document No.", "Line No.");
      END;
      // Stop PA036997
      DeleteVehProtectedCodes;
      VehiclePurchG.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type");
      VehiclePurchG.SETRANGE("Document No.", "Document No.");
      VehiclePurchG.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", "Line No.");
      VehiclePurchG.DELETEALL;
      IF "Trade-In for VIN" <> '' THEN BEGIN
        CASE "Document Type" OF
          "Document Type"::Invoice:
            BEGIN
              SalTradeInsG.SETCURRENTKEY("Purch. Invoice No.", "Purch. Invoice Line No.");
              SalTradeInsG.SETRANGE("Purch. Invoice No.", "Document No.");
              SalTradeInsG.SETRANGE("Purch. Invoice Line No.", "Line No.");
              IF SalTradeInsG.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                SalTradeInsG."Purch. Invoice No." := '';
                SalTradeInsG."Purch. Invoice Line No." := 0;
                SalTradeInsG.MODIFY;
              END;
            END;
          "Document Type"::"Credit Memo":
            BEGIN
              SalTradeInsG.SETCURRENTKEY("Purch. Cr. Memo No.", "Purch. Cr. Memo Line No.");
              SalTradeInsG.SETRANGE("Purch. Cr. Memo No.", "Document No.");
              SalTradeInsG.SETRANGE("Purch. Cr. Memo Line No.", "Line No.");
              IF SalTradeInsG.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                SalTradeInsG."Purch. Cr. Memo No." := '';
                SalTradeInsG."Purch. Cr. Memo Line No." := 0;
                SalTradeInsG.MODIFY;
              END;
            END;
        END;
      END;
      SalesAssistanceLineG.DeleteDocSalesAssistLine(SalesAssistanceLineG.Area::Purchase,"Document Type","Document No.","Line No.");
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetExpectedDelivDate@5025377();
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      GetPurchHeader();
      IF Type <> Type::Item THEN
        EXIT;
      IF PurchHeader."Document Type" IN [PurchHeader."Document Type"::"Return Order",PurchHeader."Document Type"::"Credit Memo"] THEN
        EXIT;

      GetItem();
      ItemVend."Vendor No." := "Buy-from Vendor No.";
      ItemVend."Unit of Measure Code" := "Unit of Measure Code";
      IF "Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::Inquiry,"Document Type"::Order] THEN
        ItemVend."Starting Date" := PurchHeader."Order Date"
      ELSE
        ItemVend."Starting Date" := PurchHeader."Posting Date";
      ItemVend."Purch. Order Type" := PurchHeader."Purch. Order Type";
      ItemVend."Ending Date" := ItemVend."Starting Date";
      Item.FindItemVend(ItemVend,"Location Code",TRUE);
      GetVendPurchOrderType();
      IF ((FORMAT(ItemVend."Lead Time Calculation") <> '') OR
         (FORMAT(VendOrderTypeG."Lead Time Calculation") <> '')) AND
         (PurchHeader."Order Date" = 0D)
      THEN
        ERROR(C_INC070,Item.TABLECAPTION,"No.",ItemVend.FIELDCAPTION("Lead Time Calculation"),PurchHeader.FIELDCAPTION("Order Date"));
      IF FORMAT(ItemVend."Lead Time Calculation") <> '' THEN
        "Expected Receipt Date" := CALCDATE(ItemVend."Lead Time Calculation",PurchHeader."Order Date")
      ELSE
        IF FORMAT(Item."Lead Time Calculation") <> '' THEN
          "Expected Receipt Date" := CALCDATE(Item."Lead Time Calculation",PurchHeader."Order Date")
        ELSE
          IF (FORMAT(VendOrderTypeG."Lead Time Calculation") <> '') AND ("Document Type" <> "Document Type"::Inquiry) THEN
            "Expected Receipt Date" := CALCDATE(VendOrderTypeG."Lead Time Calculation",PurchHeader."Order Date");
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetVendPurchOrderType@5025378();
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF (PurchHeader."Buy-from Contact No." = '') OR ("Document Type" <> "Document Type"::Inquiry) THEN
        TESTFIELD("Buy-from Vendor No.");
      IF VendOrderTypeG.GET("Buy-from Vendor No.",PurchHeader."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code",PurchHeader."Purch. Order Type") THEN
        EXIT;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE CreatedRelatedLines@5025379(PurchLineP@1109400000 : Record 39) DoFormUpdateR : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // @ Wrapper function for function CreatedRelatedLinesWithStepWidth.
      // @ It will use "0" as LineNoStepWidthP which will make the final additional line creation routine to look for a
      // @ decent step width by itself.
      // Start PA044975
      EXIT(CreatedRelatedLinesWithStepWidth(PurchLineP, 0));
      // Stop PA044975
    END;

    PROCEDURE CreatedRelatedLinesWithStepWidth@1055603(PurchLineP@1109400000 : Record 39;LineNoStepWidthP@1055600 : Integer) DoFormUpdateR : Boolean;
    VAR
      TransfExtTextL@1109400001 : Codeunit 378;
      AddItemFuncL@1109400002 : Codeunit 5028716;
    BEGIN
      // @ The function will call the appropriate function in codeunit "Additional Item - Functions"
      // @ It can consider a given Step Width for the Line number creation.
      // Start PA044975
      DoFormUpdateR := FALSE;
      IF PurchLineP.Type = PurchLineP.Type::Item THEN
        CASE "Order Type" OF
          "Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases":
            IF AddItemFuncL.TransferToPurchasing(PurchLineP, LineNoStepWidthP, AddtlItemG.FIELDCAPTION("Consider in Parts Purchases")) THEN
              DoFormUpdateR := TRUE;
          "Order Type"::Service:
            IF AddItemFuncL.TransferToPurchasing(PurchLineP, LineNoStepWidthP, AddtlItemG.FIELDCAPTION("Consider in Service Purchases")) THEN
              DoFormUpdateR := TRUE;
        END;
      IF TransfExtTextL.PurchCheckIfAnyExtText(PurchLineP, FALSE) THEN BEGIN
        TransfExtTextL.InsertPurchExtText(PurchLineP);
      END;
      IF TransfExtTextL.MakeUpdate THEN
        DoFormUpdateR := TRUE;
      // Stop PA044975
    END;

    PROCEDURE DeleteRelatedLines@5025380(WithConfirmationP@1109400000 : Boolean);
    VAR
      PurchLineL@1109400001 : Record 39;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF "Line No." <> 0 THEN BEGIN
        PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
        PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
        PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Attached to Line No.","Line No.");
        PurchLineL.SETFILTER("Line No.",'<>%1', "Line No.");
        IF WithConfirmationP THEN BEGIN
          PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Additional Item", PurchLineL."Additional Item"::"Additional Item", PurchLineL."Additional Item"::Deposit);
      // Start PA044975
          IF NOT PurchLineL.ISEMPTY THEN
      // Stop PA044975
            IF PurchLineL.COUNT = 1 THEN BEGIN
              IF CONFIRM(C_INC025, TRUE) THEN
                PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Additional Item")
              ELSE
                PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Additional Item", PurchLineL."Additional Item"::" ");
            END ELSE BEGIN
              IF CONFIRM(C_INC024, TRUE, PurchLineL.COUNT) THEN
                PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Additional Item")
              ELSE
                PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Additional Item", PurchLineL."Additional Item"::" ");
            END;
        END;
      // Start PA044975
        IF NOT PurchLineL.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
      // Start EU.0089938
          IF PurchLineL.FINDSET THEN
            REPEAT
              IF PurchLineL."Receipt No." = '' THEN
                PurchLineL.TESTFIELD("Qty. Rcd. Not Invoiced", 0);
              IF PurchLineL."Return Shipment No." = '' THEN
                PurchLineL.TESTFIELD("Return Qty. Shipped Not Invd.", 0);
            UNTIL PurchLineL.NEXT = 0;
      // Stop EU.0089938

          PurchLineL.SETFILTER("Reserved Qty. (Base)", '<>0');
          IF PurchLineL.FINDSET THEN
            REPEAT
              PurchHeader.CancelReservationOneLine(PurchLineL);
            UNTIL PurchLineL.NEXT = 0;
          PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Reserved Qty. (Base)");

          PurchLineL.SetDeleteQuietFlag(TRUE);
          PurchLineL.DELETEALL(TRUE);
          PurchLineL.SetDeleteQuietFlag(FALSE);
        END;
        PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Additional Item");
      // Start PA032441
        IF NOT PurchLineL.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA044975
          PurchLineL.MODIFYALL("Additional Item",PurchLineL."Additional Item"::" ");
          PurchLineL.MODIFYALL("Quantity Multiplier",0);
          PurchLineL.MODIFYALL("Attached to Line No.",0);
        END;
      // Stop PA032441
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE MatchPurchaseSales@5025413();
    VAR
      SalesLineL@1109400000 : Record 37;
      SalesLine2L@1109400001 : Record 37;
      SalesLineTempL@1109400002 : TEMPORARY Record 37;
      PurchOrdVehSubfPageL@1109400003 : Page 5025455;
      SalesOrdVehSufPageL@1109400004 : Page 5025449;
      PurchCrMemoVehSubfPageL@1109400005 : Page 5025451;
      PurchInvoVehSubfPageL@1109400006 : Page 5025453;
      SalesOrdVehSubPageL@1109400007 : Page 5025441;
      PurchaseRetOrdSubPageL@1000 : Page 5045501;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      SalesLineL.SETCURRENTKEY("From Purch. Document Type","From Purch. Document No.");
      SalesLineL.SETRANGE("From Purch. Document Type","Document Type");
      SalesLineL.SETRANGE("From Purch. Document No.","Document No.");
      SalesLineL.SETRANGE("From Purch. Line No.","Line No.");
      IF SalesLineL.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          SalesLine2L := SalesLineL;
          SalesLineTempL := SalesLineL;
          SalesLineTempL.INSERT;
          SalesLine2L."From Purch. Document Type" := SalesLine2L."From Purch. Document Type"::Inquiry;
          SalesLine2L."From Purch. Document No." := '';
          SalesLine2L."From Purch. Line No." := 0;
          SalesLine2L.MODIFY;
          SalesLine2L.VALIDATE("No.","No.");
          SalesLine2L.MODIFY(TRUE);
          SalesOrdVehSubPageL.Set(SalesLine2L);
          SalesOrdVehSubPageL.InsertLine();
        UNTIL SalesLineL.NEXT = 0;
      xRec.GET("Document Type","Document No.","Line No.");
      VALIDATE("No.");
      CASE "Document Type" OF
        "Document Type"::Inquiry:
          BEGIN
            CLEAR(PurchOrdVehSubfPageL);
            PurchOrdVehSubfPageL.Def(Rec);
            PurchOrdVehSubfPageL.InsertLine();
          END;
        "Document Type"::Order:
          BEGIN
            CLEAR(SalesOrdVehSufPageL);
            SalesOrdVehSufPageL.Def(Rec);
      // Start PA032542.5879513
            SalesOrdVehSufPageL.SetSkipSaveRecord(TRUE);
      // Stop PA032542.5879513
            SalesOrdVehSufPageL.InsertLine();
          END;
        "Document Type"::Invoice:
          BEGIN
            CLEAR(PurchInvoVehSubfPageL);
            PurchInvoVehSubfPageL.Def(Rec);
            PurchInvoVehSubfPageL.InsertLine();
          END;
        "Document Type"::"Return Order":
          BEGIN
            CLEAR(PurchaseRetOrdSubPageL);
            PurchaseRetOrdSubPageL.Def(Rec);
            PurchaseRetOrdSubPageL.InsertLine();
          END;
        "Document Type"::"Credit Memo":
          BEGIN
            CLEAR(PurchCrMemoVehSubfPageL);
            PurchCrMemoVehSubfPageL.Def(Rec);
            PurchCrMemoVehSubfPageL.InsertLine();
          END;
      END;
      GET("Document Type","Document No.","Line No.");
      IF SalesLineTempL.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          SalesLine2L.GET(SalesLineTempL."Document Type",SalesLineTempL."Document No.",SalesLineTempL."Line No.");
          SalesLine2L."From Purch. Document Type" := "Document Type";
          SalesLine2L."From Purch. Document No." := "Document No.";
          SalesLine2L."From Purch. Line No." := "Line No.";
          SalesLine2L.MODIFY;
        UNTIL SalesLineTempL.NEXT = 0;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE MatchPurchaseSalesOptions@5025414();
    VAR
      VarOptionL@1109400000 : Record 5025424;
      SalesLineL@1109400001 : Record 37;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF "Order Type" <> "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases" THEN
        EXIT;
      SalesLineL.RESET;
      SalesLineL.SETCURRENTKEY("From Purch. Document Type", "From Purch. Document No.", "From Purch. Line No.");
      SalesLineL.SETRANGE("From Purch. Document Type","Document Type");
      SalesLineL.SETRANGE("From Purch. Document No.","Document No.");
      SalesLineL.SETRANGE("From Purch. Line No.","Line No.");
      IF NOT SalesLineL.FINDSET THEN
        EXIT;
      REPEAT
        OptionVariantG.RESET;
        OptionVariantG.SETRANGE(Area,OptionVariantG.Area::Purchase);
        OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
        OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
        OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document Line No.","Line No.");
        IF OptionVariantG.FINDSET THEN
          REPEAT
            IF NOT VarOptionL.GET(
               VarOptionL.Area::Sale,
               SalesLineL."Document Type",
               SalesLineL."Document No.",
               SalesLineL."Line No.",
               OptionVariantG.Type,
               OptionVariantG."Make Code",
               OptionVariantG."Model Code",
               OptionVariantG."Option Code",
               OptionVariantG."Internal Code")
            THEN BEGIN
              OptionVariantG.CreateOptionForSales(OptionVariantG,SalesLineL);
            END;
          UNTIL OptionVariantG.NEXT = 0;
        OptionVariantG.RESET;
        OptionVariantG.SETRANGE(Area,OptionVariantG.Area::Sale);
        OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document Type",SalesLineL."Document Type");
        OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document No.",SalesLineL."Document No.");
        OptionVariantG.SETRANGE("Document Line No.",SalesLineL."Line No.");
        IF OptionVariantG.FINDSET THEN
          REPEAT
            IF NOT VarOptionL.GET(
               VarOptionL.Area::Purchase,
               "Document Type",
               "Document No.",
               "Line No.",
               OptionVariantG.Type,
               OptionVariantG."Make Code",
               OptionVariantG."Model Code",
               OptionVariantG."Option Code",
               OptionVariantG."Internal Code")
            THEN BEGIN
      // Start PA035634
              OptionVariantG.UpdateOptionsPrice(OptionVariantG);
      // Stop PA035634
              OptionVariantG.DELETE(TRUE);
            END;
          UNTIL OptionVariantG.NEXT = 0;
        SalesLineL.GetOptionPrice();
        SalesLineL.MODIFY;
      UNTIL SalesLineL.NEXT = 0;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE VehOptionShow@5025381();
    VAR
      OptionL@1109400000 : Record 5025424;
    BEGIN
      // Start PA036544
      IF ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function", ExitPointSetupG.Type::Pre, 'PurchVehOptionShow') THEN
        EXIT;
      // Stop PA036544
      // Start INC
      // Show Options is only possible for Item Type "Vehicle"
      IF "Item Type" <> "Item Type"::Vehicle THEN BEGIN
        MESSAGE(C_INC069,FIELDCAPTION("Item Type"));
        EXIT;
      END;
      OptionL.SETRANGE(Area, OptionL.Area::Purchase);
      OptionL.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type");
      OptionL.SETRANGE("Document No.", "Document No.");
      OptionL.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", "Line No.");

        IF "Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle THEN BEGIN
          VehicleUnitG.MakePurchOptionLines(Rec);
          COMMIT;
          OptionL.FINDFIRST;
        END;
      END;
      PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Option Variants", OptionL);
      GetOptionPrice();
      // Stop INC
      // Start PA036296.29245
      // Start PA036544
      ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function", ExitPointSetupG.Type::Post, 'PurchVehOptionShow');
      // Stop PA036544
      // Stop PA036296.29245
    END;

    PROCEDURE LocationCodeAssist@5025384();
    VAR
      ItemLocationL@1109400000 : Record 5028700;
      UserLocationL@1109400001 : Record 5028664;
      LocationFilterL@1109400002 : Text[1024];
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF Type <> Type::Item THEN
        EXIT;
      UserLocationL.SETRANGE("User ID",USERID);
      IF UserLocationL.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          LocationFilterL := LocationFilterL + '|' + UserLocationL."Location Code";
        UNTIL UserLocationL.NEXT = 0;
        LocationFilterL := COPYSTR(LocationFilterL, 2);
        ItemLocationL.FILTERGROUP(2);
        ItemLocationL.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
        ItemLocationL.SETFILTER("Location Code",LocationFilterL);
        ItemLocationL.FILTERGROUP(0);
        IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(0, ItemLocationL) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN
          VALIDATE("Location Code",ItemLocationL."Location Code");
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE FindStatus@5025383(SkipLineNoCheckP@1000 : Boolean);
    VAR
      PurchLineL@1109400000 : Record 39;
      OldStatusL@1109400001 : Integer;
      OldStatusCodeL@1109400002 : Code[20];
      NewStatusCodeL@1109400003 : Code[20];
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF StatusUpdateDeactivatedG THEN
        EXIT;
      OldStatusL := "Line Status";
      FindStatus2();
      // Start EU.0114873.115555
      IF SkipLineNoCheckP OR ("Line Status" <> OldStatusL) THEN BEGIN
      // Stop EU.0114873.115555
        IF PurchLineL.GET("Document Type","Document No.","Line No.") THEN
          MODIFY;
        IF HeadStatusUpdateDeactivatedG THEN
          EXIT;
        // Start  - performance during C90 post INC
        IF "Import Costing No." <> '' THEN
          EXIT;
      // Start PA035134
        IF NOT SkipUpdateStatusG THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA035134
      // Start EU.0041404
          CLEAR(PurchHeader);
      // Stop EU.0041404
          GetPurchHeader();
          OldStatusCodeL := PurchHeader."Status Code";
      // Start EU.0041404
      // Start EU.0114873.115555
          IF SkipLineNoCheckP THEN
            PurchHeader.UpdateDocStatus("Line No.")
          ELSE
            IF NOT NoStatusChangeG THEN
              PurchHeader.UpdateStatus;
      // Stop EU.0114873.115555
      // Stop EU.0041404
          IF OldStatusCodeL <> PurchHeader."Status Code" THEN BEGIN
            NewStatusCodeL := PurchHeader."Status Code";
            PurchHeader.GET(PurchHeader."Document Type",PurchHeader."No.");
            PurchHeader."Status Code" := NewStatusCodeL;
            PurchHeader.MODIFY;
          END;
      // Start PA035134
        END;
      // Stop PA035134
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE FindStatus2@5025386();
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      "Line Status" := "Line Status"::" ";
      IF "Quantity Invoiced" <> 0 THEN
        "Line Status" := "Line Status"::"Partly Invoiced";
      IF ("Line Status" = "Line Status"::"Partly Invoiced") AND
         ("Qty. Rcd. Not Invoiced" = 0) AND
         ("Quantity Received" = Quantity)
      THEN BEGIN
        "Line Status" := "Line Status"::"Completely Invoiced";
        EXIT;
      END;
      IF ("Line Status" = "Line Status"::"Partly Invoiced") AND
         ("Return Qty. Shipped Not Invd." = 0) AND
         ("Return Qty. Shipped" = Quantity)
      THEN BEGIN
        "Line Status" := "Line Status"::"Completely Invoiced";
        EXIT;
      END;
      IF "Qty. to Receive" > 0 THEN BEGIN
        "Line Status" := "Line Status"::"Ready for Shipment";
        IF ("Receipt No." <> '') AND ("Receipt Line No." <> 0) THEN
          "Line Status" := "Line Status"::"Completely Shipped";
      END;
      IF "Return Qty. to Ship" > 0 THEN BEGIN
        "Line Status" := "Line Status"::"Ready for Shipment";
        IF ("Return Shipment No." <> '') AND ("Return Shipment Line No." <> 0) THEN
          "Line Status" := "Line Status"::"Completely Shipped";
      END;
      IF "Line Status" > "Line Status"::"Completely Shipped" THEN
        EXIT;
      IF ("Quantity Received" <> 0) OR ("Return Qty. Shipped" <> 0) THEN
        "Line Status" := "Line Status"::"Partly Shipped";
      IF (("Line Status" = "Line Status"::"Partly Shipped") AND ("Quantity Received" = Quantity)) OR
         (("Receipt No." <> '') AND ("Receipt Line No." <> 0))
      THEN
        "Line Status" := "Line Status"::"Completely Shipped";
      IF (("Line Status" = "Line Status"::"Partly Shipped") AND ("Return Qty. Shipped" = Quantity)) OR
         (("Return Shipment No." <> '') AND ("Return Shipment Line No." <> 0))
      THEN
        "Line Status" := "Line Status"::"Completely Shipped";
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE StatusCheckFunction@5025387(CheckFieldNumberP@1109400000 : Boolean);
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF CheckFieldNumberP AND (CurrFieldNo = 0) THEN
        EXIT;
      GetPurchHeader();
      PurchHeader.ApplyStatusFunction(FALSE);
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckBelongingLines@24();
    VAR
      PurchLineL@1109400000 : Record 39;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      // Start PA039974
      IF "Currency Rounding Position" THEN
        EXIT;
      // Stop PA039974
      IF ("Order Type" = "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases") AND ("Item Type" <> "Item Type"::Vehicle) AND
         (Type <> Type::" ") AND (Type <> Type::"Charge (Item)")
      THEN BEGIN
        PurchLine2.RESET;
        PurchLine2.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
        PurchLine2.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
        PurchLine2.SETFILTER("Line No.",'<%1',"Line No.");
        PurchLine2.SETRANGE("Item Type","Item Type"::Vehicle);
        PurchLine2.SETRANGE("Import Costing No.",'');
        IF PurchLine2.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
          IF VIN <> PurchLine2.VIN THEN
            VALIDATE(VIN, PurchLine2.VIN);
          IF "Vehicle Line No." <> PurchLine2."Line No." THEN
            VALIDATE("Vehicle Line No.",PurchLine2."Line No.");
        END;
      END;
      IF ((xRec.VIN <> VIN) OR (VIN = '')) AND ("Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle) AND (Type <> Type::"Charge (Item)") THEN BEGIN
        PurchLine2.RESET;
        PurchLine2.SETCURRENTKEY("Document Type","Document No.","Line No.");
        PurchLine2.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
        PurchLine2.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
        PurchLine2.SETFILTER("Line No.",'> %1',"Line No.");
        PurchLine2.SETFILTER("No.",'<>%1','');
        PurchLine2.SETRANGE("Import Costing No.",'');
        IF PurchLine2.FINDSET THEN
          REPEAT
            IF (PurchLine2."Item Type" <> "Item Type"::Vehicle) AND (PurchLine2.Type <> PurchLine2.Type::"Charge (Item)") THEN BEGIN
              PurchLine2.VALIDATE(VIN,VIN);
              PurchLine2."Vehicle Status" := "Vehicle Status";
              IF PurchLineL.GET("Document Type","Document No.","Line No.") THEN
                PurchLine2.VALIDATE("Vehicle Line No.","Line No.")
              ELSE
                PurchLine2."Vehicle Line No." := "Line No.";
              PurchLine2.MODIFY;
            END;
          UNTIL (PurchLine2.NEXT = 0) OR (PurchLine2."Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle);
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE InsertAssociatedSalesLine@90025();
    VAR
      SalesLineL@1109400000 : Record 37;
      SalesLine2L@1109400001 : Record 37;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF "Item Type" = "Item Type"::"Veh. Transfer" THEN BEGIN
        PurchLine2.RESET;
        PurchLine2.SETCURRENTKEY("Document Type","Document No.");
        PurchLine2.SETRANGE("Document Type",Rec."Document Type");
        PurchLine2.SETRANGE("Document No.",Rec."Document No.");
        PurchLine2.SETRANGE("Line No.",Rec."Vehicle Line No.");
        IF PurchLine2.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
          SalesLineL.RESET;
          SalesLineL.SETCURRENTKEY("From Purch. Document Type","From Purch. Document No.","From Purch. Line No.");
          SalesLineL.SETRANGE("From Purch. Document Type",PurchLine2."Document Type");
          SalesLineL.SETRANGE("From Purch. Document No.",PurchLine2."Document No.");
          SalesLineL.SETRANGE("From Purch. Line No.",PurchLine2."Line No.");
          IF SalesLineL.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
            SalesLine2L.RESET;
            SalesLine2L.SETCURRENTKEY("Document Type","Document No.");
            SalesLine2L.SETRANGE("Document Type",SalesLineL."Document Type");
            SalesLine2L.SETRANGE("Document No.",SalesLineL."Document No.");
            SalesLine2L.SETFILTER("Line No.",'>%1',SalesLineL."Line No.");
            SalesLine2L.SETRANGE("Item Type","Item Type"::"Veh. Transfer");
            SalesLine2L.SETRANGE("From Purch. Document Type","Document Type");
            SalesLine2L.SETRANGE("From Purch. Document No.","Document No.");
            SalesLine2L.SETRANGE("From Purch. Line No.","Line No.");
            IF SalesLine2L.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
              SalesLineL.TESTFIELD("Quantity Invoiced",0);
      // Start PA036549.34387
              IF (SalesLine2L."Quantity Shipped" = 0) AND ("No." <> SalesLine2L."No.") THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA036549.34387
                SalesLine2L."No." := "No.";
                SalesLine2L.VALIDATE("No.");
              END;
              SalesLine2L.VIN := SalesLineL.VIN;
              IF SalesLine2L."Unit Cost (LCY)" <> Rec."Direct Unit Cost" THEN
                SalesLine2L.VALIDATE("Unit Cost (LCY)",Rec."Direct Unit Cost");
              SalesLine2L."Posting Group" := "Posting Group";
              SalesLine2L.MODIFY;
            END ELSE BEGIN
              SalesLine2L.INIT;
              SalesLine2L."Document Type" := SalesLineL."Document Type";
              SalesLine2L."Document No." := SalesLineL."Document No.";
              SalesLine2L."Line No." := SalesLineL."Line No." +
                PurchLine2.InsertLineNoDistance(1, TRUE);
              IF NOT SalesLine2L.INSERT THEN
                REPEAT
                  SalesLine2L."Line No." := SalesLine2L."Line No." - 1000;
                UNTIL SalesLine2L.INSERT;
              SalesLine2L."Item Type" := SalesLine2L."Item Type"::"Veh. Transfer";
              SalesLine2L.VALIDATE("Item Type");
              SalesLine2L.Type := SalesLineL.Type;
              SalesLine2L."Order Type" := SalesLine2L."Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases";
              SalesLine2L."No." := "No.";
              SalesLine2L.VALIDATE("No.");
              SalesLine2L.Quantity := Quantity;
              SalesLine2L.VALIDATE(Quantity);
              SalesLine2L.VIN := PurchLine2.VIN;
              SalesLine2L."From Purch. Document Type" := "Document Type";
              SalesLine2L."From Purch. Document No." := "Document No.";
              SalesLine2L."From Purch. Line No." := "Line No.";
              SalesLine2L."Posting Group" := "Posting Group";
              SalesLine2L.MODIFY;
            END;
          END;
        END;
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE TestFromService@5025625(ExternalServiceTestP@1109400000 : Boolean) : Boolean;
    VAR
      ServiceLineL@1109400001 : Record 5025625;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF ("Service Order No." = '') OR ("Service Order Line No." = 0) THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      IF NOT ServiceLineL.GET(ServiceLineL."Document Type"::Order,"Service Order No.","Service Order Line No.") THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      EXIT(NOT ExternalServiceTestP OR (ServiceLineL.Type = ServiceLineL.Type::"Ext. Service"));
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckOptionVATBaseAmount@90027(VAR OptionVariantP@1109400000 : Record 5025424;CurrFieldNoP@1109400001 : Integer) : Boolean;
    VAR
      FieldCaptionTextL@1109400002 : Text[100];
      SalesAmountL@1109400003 : Decimal;
      PurchAmountL@1109400004 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF NOT OptionVariantP."Differential Taxation" OR (CurrFieldNoP = 0) OR
         (OptionVariantP.Type = OptionVariantP.Type::Vehicle)
      THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);
      SalesAmountL := OptionVariantP.Quantity * OptionVariantP."Unit Price" - OptionVariantP."Line Discount Amount";
      PurchAmountL := OptionVariantP.Quantity * OptionVariantP."Direct Unit Cost";
      IF SalesAmountL >= PurchAmountL THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);
      CASE CurrFieldNoP OF
        FIELDNO("VAT Prod. Posting Group"):
          FieldCaptionTextL := FIELDCAPTION("VAT Prod. Posting Group");
        FIELDNO("Gen. Prod. Posting Group"):
          FieldCaptionTextL := FIELDCAPTION("Gen. Prod. Posting Group");
        ELSE
          FieldCaptionTextL := TABLECAPTION;
      END;
      ERROR(C_INC071,
        FieldCaptionTextL,
        FIELDCAPTION("VAT Base Amount"),
        OptionVariantP.FIELDCAPTION("Differential Taxation"),
        OptionVariantP.TABLECAPTION);
      // Stop INC
    END;

      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE FillDocCampLines@1109400008();
    VAR
      PurchHdrL@1109400006 : Record 38;
      CampaignMgmtL@1109400003 : Codeunit 5045777;
      AreaL@1109400004 : 'Purchase,Sale';
      DateL@1109400005 : Date;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      PurchHdrL.GET("Document Type","Document No.");
      // Start PA033733.9205326
        IF PurchHdrL."Order Type"<>PurchHdrL."Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases" THEN
          EXIT;
      // Stop PA033733.9205326
      IF "Document Type" IN ["Document Type"::Invoice,"Document Type"::"Credit Memo"] THEN
        DateL := PurchHdrL."Document Date"
      ELSE
        DateL := PurchHdrL."Order Date";
      IF ("Item Type" = "Item Type"::Item) AND ("Document Type" <> "Document Type"::"Blanket Order") THEN BEGIN
        "Campaign Code" := '';
        DocCampLineG.RESET;
        DocCampLineG.SETRANGE(Area, DocCampLineG.Area::Purchase);
        DocCampLineG.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
        DocCampLineG.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
        DocCampLineG.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", "Line No.");
        IF DocCampLineG.FINDFIRST THEN
          DocCampLineG.DELETEALL(TRUE);
        CampaignMgmtL.FillDocCampaignLine(AreaL::Purchase,Rec);
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdateDocCampLine@1109400007();
    VAR
      PurchHeaderL@1109400000 : Record 38;
      DocCampaignLineL@1109400001 : Record 5045787;
      DateL@1109400002 : Date;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      PurchHeaderL.GET("Document Type", "Document No.");
      DocCampaignLineL.RESET;
      DocCampaignLineL.SETRANGE(Area, DocCampaignLineL.Area::Purchase);
      DocCampaignLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type", "Document Type");
      DocCampaignLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.", "Document No.");
      DocCampaignLineL.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", "Line No.");
      IF DocCampaignLineL.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          IF "Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Credit Memo" THEN
            DateL := PurchHeaderL."Document Date"
          ELSE
            DateL := PurchHeaderL."Order Date";
          IF DocCampaignLineL."Allowance Type" = DocCampaignLineL."Allowance Type"::Subsequent THEN BEGIN
            DocCampaignLineL.Amount := Amount;
            DocCampaignLineL."Amount (LCY)" := CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtFCYToLCY
              (DateL, "Currency Code", Amount, PurchHeaderL."Currency Factor");
          END ELSE BEGIN
            DocCampaignLineL.Amount := DocCampaignLineL."Chain Unit Amount" * DocCampaignLineL.Quantity;
            DocCampaignLineL."Amount (LCY)" := DocCampaignLineL."Chain Unit Amount (LCY)" * DocCampaignLineL.Quantity;
          END;
          DocCampaignLineL.Post := FALSE;
          DocCampaignLineL.MODIFY;
        UNTIL DocCampaignLineL.NEXT = 0;
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE DeleteDocCampLines@1109400009();

    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      "Campaign Code" := '';
      DocCampaignLineL.RESET;

      DocCampaignLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.", "Document No.");
      DocCampaignLineL.SETRANGE("Document Line No.", "Line No.");

      // Stop INC
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE UpdateServCost@1109400010();
    VAR
      ServLineL@1109400000 : Record 5025625;
      ArchServHdrL@72000 : Record 5025636;
      ArchServLineL@1109400001 : Record 5025637;
      ServHdrL@1000000000 : Record 5025624;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF ("Order Type" <> "Order Type"::Service) OR
         ("Item Type" <> "Item Type"::"G/L Account") OR
         ("Service Order No." = '') OR
         ("Service Order Line No." = 0)
      THEN
        EXIT;
      // Start PA033152
      IF ("Document Type" <> "Document Type"::"Credit Memo") THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA033152
        IF ArchServLineL.GET(ArchServLineL."Document Type"::Order,"Service Order No.","Service Order Line No.") THEN BEGIN
          ArchServLineL."Unit Cost (LCY)" := "Unit Cost (LCY)";
      // Start EU.0087064
          IF ArchServLineL."Currency Code" <> "Currency Code" THEN BEGIN
            ArchServHdrL.GET(ServLineL."Document Type"::Order,"Service Order No.");
            ServHdrL.TRANSFERFIELDS(ArchServHdrL);
            ArchServLineL."Unit Cost" := CalcUnitCostFromLCY(ServHdrL.GetCurrencyDate(), "Unit Cost (LCY)", ArchServLineL."Currency Code", ServHdrL."Currency Factor");
          END ELSE
            ArchServLineL."Unit Cost" := "Unit Cost";
      // Stop EU.0087064
      // Start PA035597
          LOCKTABLE(TRUE,FALSE);
      // Stop PA035597
          ArchServLineL.MODIFY;
        END ELSE
          IF ServLineL.GET(ServLineL."Document Type"::Order,"Service Order No.","Service Order Line No.") THEN BEGIN
            ServLineL."Unit Cost (LCY)" := "Unit Cost (LCY)";
            ServLineL."Unit Cost" := "Unit Cost";
      // Start PA033497
      // Start EU.0087064
            IF ServLineL."Currency Code" <> "Currency Code" THEN BEGIN
              ServHdrL.GET(ServLineL."Document Type"::Order,"Service Order No.");
              ServLineL."Unit Cost" := CalcUnitCostFromLCY(ServHdrL.GetCurrencyDate(), "Unit Cost (LCY)", ServLineL."Currency Code", ServHdrL."Currency Factor");
      // Stop EU.0087064
            END ELSE
              ServLineL."Unit Cost" := "Unit Cost";
      // Stop PA033497
      // Start PA035597
            LOCKTABLE(TRUE,FALSE);
      // Stop PA035597
            ServLineL.MODIFY;
          END;
      // Start PA033152
      END;
      // Stop PA033152
      // Stop INC
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CalcUnitCostFromLCY@72000(DateP@72000 : Date;UnitCostLCYP@72001 : Decimal;CurrencyCodeP@72002 : Code[10];CurrencyFactorP@72003 : Decimal) : Decimal;
    VAR
      CurrencyL@72004 : Record 4;
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0087064
      IF CurrencyCodeP = '' THEN
        EXIT(UnitCostLCYP);
      CurrencyL.Initialize(CurrencyCodeP);
      CurrencyL.TESTFIELD("Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");
      EXIT(ROUND(CurrExchRate.ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(DateP, CurrencyCodeP, UnitCostLCYP, CurrencyFactorP), CurrencyL."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision"));
      // Stop EU.0087064
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckImportCostDelete@1101353005();
    VAR
      ImportCostLineL@1101353000 : Record 5087001;
      ImportCostL@1101353001 : Record 5087002;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF NOT ImportCostUpdateG AND ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::Order) THEN
        TESTFIELD("Import Costing No.",'');
      IF ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::Invoice) AND ("Import Costing No." > '') AND
         ("Purch. Order No." <> '') AND ("Import Costing Line No." <> 0)
      THEN BEGIN
        IF ImportCostLineL.GET("Import Costing No.","Import Costing Line No.") THEN BEGIN
          ImportCostLineL."Invoice No." := '';
          ImportCostLineL."Invoice Line No." := 0;
          ImportCostLineL.MODIFY;
        END;
      END;
      IF (("Document Type" = "Document Type"::Invoice) OR
         ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::"Credit Memo")) AND
         ("Import Cost Code" <> '')
      THEN BEGIN
        LOCKTABLE;
        ImportCostL.LOCKTABLE;
        IF ImportCostL.GET("Import Costing No.","Import Cost Code") THEN BEGIN
          ImportCostL."Document No." := '';
          ImportCostL.MODIFY;
        END;
      END;
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckSalesOrderILEReservations@1101353015(PurchLineP@1101353000 : Record 39;BinCodeP@1101353001 : Code[20]);
    VAR
      SalesLineL@1101353004 : Record 37;
      ReallocateReservationsL@1101353005 : Report 5086737;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      ReservEntry.RESET;
      ReservEngineMgt.InitFilterAndSortingLookupFrom(ReservEntry, TRUE);
      ReservEngineMgt.PurchLineFilterReservFrom(ReservEntry, PurchLineP);
      // Start PA032651
      ReservEntry.SETRANGE("For Subtype", SalesLineL."Document Type"::Order); //Sales Orders
      IF ReservEntry.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          CLEAR(ReallocateReservationsL);
          IF SalesLineL.GET(ReservEntry."For Subtype", ReservEntry."For ID", ReservEntry."For Ref. No.") THEN
            IF SalesLineL."Shipped Not Invoiced" = 0 THEN
              IF ReallocateReservationsL.SalesLineILEReservDiffBinExist(SalesLineL, BinCodeP) THEN
                ERROR(C_IMS009,
                  FIELDCAPTION("Bin Code"),
                  SalesLineL."Document Type",
                  SalesLineL."Document No.",
                  SalesLineL.FIELDCAPTION("Line No."),
                  SalesLineL."Line No.");
      // Stop PA032651
        UNTIL ReservEntry.NEXT = 0;
      // Start INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckFactoryNo@1101353008(VINoP@1101353000 : Code[20];FactoryNoP@1101353001 : Code[20]);
    VAR
      PurchLineL@1101353002 : Record 39;
    BEGIN
      // Start INC
      IF FactoryNoP = '' THEN
        EXIT;

      VehicleG.RESET;
      VehicleG.SETCURRENTKEY("Factory No.");
      VehicleG.SETRANGE("Factory No.",FactoryNoP);
      VehicleG.SETFILTER(VIN,'<>%1',VINoP);
      IF VehicleG.FINDFIRST THEN
        ERROR(C_IMS001,FIELDCAPTION("Factory No."),FactoryNoP, VehicleG.VIN);

      VehicleLedgEntryG.RESET;
      VehicleLedgEntryG.SETCURRENTKEY("Factory No.","Entry Type");
      VehicleLedgEntryG.SETRANGE("Factory No.",FactoryNoP);
      VehicleLedgEntryG.SETRANGE("Entry Type",VehicleLedgEntryG."Entry Type"::Purchase);
      VehicleLedgEntryG.SETFILTER(VIN,'<>%1',VINoP);
      IF VehicleLedgEntryG.FINDFIRST THEN
        IF VehicleG.GET(VehicleLedgEntryG.VIN) THEN
          ERROR(C_IMS001,FIELDCAPTION("Factory No."),FactoryNoP,VehicleLedgEntryG.VIN);

      PurchLineL.RESET;
      PurchLineL.SETCURRENTKEY("Document Type","Order Type","Item Type","Factory No.");
      PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type",PurchLineL."Document Type"::Order,PurchLineL."Document Type"::Invoice);
      PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Order Type",PurchLineL."Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases");
      PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Item Type",PurchLineL."Item Type"::Vehicle);
      PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Factory No.",FactoryNoP);
      PurchLineL.SETFILTER(VIN,'<>%1',VINoP);
      IF PurchLineL.FINDFIRST THEN
        IF VehicleG.GET(PurchLineL.VIN) THEN
          ERROR(C_IMS011,FIELDCAPTION("Factory No."),FactoryNoP,PurchLineL.VIN,
            PurchLineL."Document Type",PurchLineL."Document No.",PurchLineL."Line No.");
      // Stop INC
    END;

    PROCEDURE FormVINOnAfterValidate@1101342648(VAR PurchLineP@1101342643 : Record 39;VINChangedP@1101342644 : Boolean);
    VAR
      PurchHeaderL@1101314645 : Record 38;
      PurchLineL@1101342647 : Record 39;
      VehicleOptionL@1101342646 : Record 5025422;
      VINUpdateRequiredL@1101342645 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // Start PA032651
      IF PurchLineP.VIN = '' THEN
        EXIT;
      IF PurchLineP."Item Type" <> PurchLineP."Item Type"::Vehicle THEN
        EXIT;
      // Start PA033985.18808
      IF ("Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle) AND VINChangedP THEN BEGIN
        PurchHeaderL.GET(PurchLineP."Document Type",PurchLineP."Document No.");
        SalesIncentiveMgmtG.UpdateSalesIncentivesPurch(PurchHeaderL,PurchLineP);
      END;
      // Stop PA033985.18808
      IF NOT VehicleG.GET(PurchLineP.VIN) THEN
        EXIT;
      VINUpdateRequiredL := VINChangedP;
      IF NOT VINUpdateRequiredL THEN
        IF PurchLineP."Document Type" = PurchLineP."Document Type"::Order THEN BEGIN
          VehicleOptionL.SETCURRENTKEY(VIN,"Copy-to Setting",Type);
          VehicleOptionL.SETFILTER(VIN, PurchLineP.VIN);
          VehicleOptionL.SETRANGE("Copy-to Setting", VehicleOptionL."Copy-to Setting"::"To Own Doc. Line");
          VehicleOptionL.SETRANGE(Type, VehicleOptionL.Type::"Other Item");
          IF NOT VehicleOptionL.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
            PurchLineL.SETCURRENTKEY("Document Type","Document No.","Item Type",VIN);
            PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type", PurchLineP."Document Type");
            PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.", PurchLineP."Document No.");
            PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Item Type", PurchLineL."Item Type"::"Veh. Transfer");
            PurchLineL.SETRANGE(VIN, PurchLineP.VIN);
            IF PurchLineL.ISEMPTY THEN
              VINUpdateRequiredL := TRUE;
          END;
        END;
      IF VINUpdateRequiredL THEN BEGIN
        VehicleUnitG.MakePurchOptionLines(PurchLineP);
        VehicleUnitG.MakePurchVehicleLines(PurchLineP);
        VehicleUnitG.MakePurchLinesFromOption(PurchLineP);
        PurchLineP.GetOptionPrice();
      END;
      // Stop PA032651
      // Start PA041187.68831
      PurchLineL.RESET;
      PurchLineL.SETCURRENTKEY("Document Type","Document No.","Item Type",VIN);
      PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type", PurchLineP."Document Type");
      PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.", PurchLineP."Document No.");
      PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Item Type", PurchLineL."Item Type"::"Veh. Transfer");
      PurchLineL.SETRANGE(VIN, PurchLineP.VIN);
      IF PurchLineL.ISEMPTY THEN
        IF ("Item Type" = "Item Type"::Vehicle) AND VINChangedP THEN
          VehicleUnitG.InsertPurchaseDefaultTransFees(PurchLineP,FALSE);
      // Stop PA041187.68831
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckReplacement1toN@1100409000() : Boolean;
    VAR
      CurrentItemReplacementsL@1100409000 : Record 5028701;
    BEGIN
      // @ checks if for this added Item No. an 1 to N Replacement was stored into Current Item Replacements Table.
      // Start PA033958
      CurrentItemReplacementsL.RESET;
      CurrentItemReplacementsL.SETRANGE("Old Item No.","No.");
      CurrentItemReplacementsL.SETRANGE("1:N Replacement",TRUE);
      IF NOT CurrentItemReplacementsL.ISEMPTY THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);
      EXIT(FALSE);
      // Stop PA033958
    END;

    PROCEDURE Fill1toNReplIntoPurchLines@1100409002() : Code[20];
    VAR
      CurrentItemReplacementsL@1100409000 : Record 5028701;
      PurchLineL@1100409001 : Record 39;
      ReplacedItemNoL@1100409003 : Code[20];
      RetItemNoL@1100409004 : Code[20];
    BEGIN
      // @ Fill 1 to N Repl Into Purch Lines
      // Start PA033958
      CurrentItemReplacementsL.RESET;
      CurrentItemReplacementsL.SETRANGE("Old Item No.","No.");
      CurrentItemReplacementsL.SETRANGE("1:N Replacement",TRUE);
      IF CurrentItemReplacementsL.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
        ReplacedItemNoL := "No.";
        "No." := CurrentItemReplacementsL."New Item No.";
        RetItemNoL := "No.";
        CurrentItemReplacementsL.NEXT;
        REPEAT
          PurchLineL.INIT;
          PurchLineL := Rec;
          PurchLineL."Line No." := PurchLineL.GetNextLineNo();
          PurchLineL.VALIDATE("No.",CurrentItemReplacementsL."New Item No.");
          PurchLineL.VALIDATE(Quantity,1);
          PurchLineL.INSERT;
        UNTIL CurrentItemReplacementsL.NEXT = 0;
        CurrentItemReplacementsL.RESET;
        CurrentItemReplacementsL.SETRANGE("Old Item No.",ReplacedItemNoL);
        CurrentItemReplacementsL.SETRANGE("1:N Replacement",TRUE);
        IF NOT CurrentItemReplacementsL.ISEMPTY THEN
          CurrentItemReplacementsL.DELETEALL;
      END ELSE
        RetItemNoL := "No.";
      EXIT(RetItemNoL);
      // Stop PA033958
    END;

    PROCEDURE AdditionalItemQtyConfirmation@1101368191() : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // Asks the User to Cofirm modification of Quantity of Additional Item
      // @ retval : Boolean
      // Start PA033986
      // Start EU.0045397.45399
      IF "Quantity Multiplier" = 0 THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);

      IF "Attached to Line No." > 0 THEN BEGIN
      // Stop EU.0045397.45399
        PurchLine2.GET("Document Type", "Document No.", "Attached to Line No.");
        EXIT(CONFIRM(C_INC079,FALSE,PurchLine2.Type, PurchLine2."No.", PurchLine2.Description));
      END;
      // Stop PA033986
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckNegativeStock@1119432002() : Text[1024];
    VAR
      ReservationEntryL@1119432003 : Record 337;
      ReturnShipL@1000000002 : Record 6651;
      ItemJnlCheckLineL@1119432000 : Codeunit 21;
      ReservedQtyOnInvL@1119432001 : Decimal;
      CheckQtyL@1101422630 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      // @ The function has to prepare some data to call the real function in codeunit 21.
      // Start PA033978
      IF Type <> Type::Item THEN
        EXIT('');
      CASE "Document Type" OF
        "Document Type"::"Credit Memo":
      // Start PA041987
          BEGIN
            IF ReturnShipL.GET("Return Shipment No.", "Return Shipment Line No.") THEN
              IF ReturnShipL."Return Qty. Shipped Not Invd." >= "Qty. to Invoice" THEN
                EXIT('');
            CheckQtyL := "Qty. to Invoice";
          END;
      // Stop PA041987
        "Document Type"::"Return Order":
          CheckQtyL := "Return Qty. to Ship (Base)";
      END;
      IF CheckQtyL = 0 THEN
        EXIT('');

      IF "Reserved Qty. (Base)" <> 0 THEN
      // Start EU.0005636
        ReservedQtyOnInvL := ReservMgtG.CalcReservQtyOnInventory(
      // Stop EU.0005636
          ReservationEntryL."For Type"::Purchase,
          "Document Type",
          "Document No.",
          "Line No.",
          '',
          "No.",
          "Location Code",
          "Bin Code");
      EXIT(ItemJnlCheckLineL.PerformNegItemStockCheck(
        "No.",
        "Location Code",
        "Bin Code",
        USERID,
        CheckQtyL,
        ReservedQtyOnInvL,
        GETPOSITION(TRUE)))
      // Stop PA033978
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetVehicleStatusForChargeItem@1101267193();
    VAR
      PurchLineL@1101267195 : Record 39;
      VehSalesDeptL@1101267194 : Record 5028667;
    BEGIN
      // @ This function gets the Vehicle Status for "Charge (Item)"
      // Start PA034482
      IF "Item Type" = "Item Type"::"Charge (Item)" THEN BEGIN
        IF ("Order Type" = "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases") AND
           ("Document Type" = "Document Type"::Order)
        THEN BEGIN
          VehSalesDeptL.SETRANGE("Location Code","Location Code");
          VehSalesDeptL.SETRANGE("Line Type",VehSalesDeptL."Line Type"::"Charge (Item)");

          PurchLineL.RESET;
          PurchLineL.SETRANGE(PurchLineL."Document Type","Document Type");
          PurchLineL.SETRANGE(PurchLineL."Document No.","Document No.");
          IF "Line No." <> 0 THEN BEGIN
            PurchLineL.SETFILTER(PurchLineL."Line No.",'<%1',"Line No.");
          END;
          PurchLineL.SETRANGE(PurchLineL."Item Type", "Item Type"::Vehicle);
          IF PurchLineL.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
            VehStatusG := PurchLineL."Vehicle Status"
          END ELSE BEGIN
            VehStatusG := "Vehicle Status"::"New Vehicle";
          END;

        END;
      END;
      // Stop PA034482
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckForLineDuplicates@1109400019();
    VAR
      PurchLineL@1109400000 : Record 39;
      AdditionalItemL@1109400005 : Record 5028716;
      AddItemDuplicateWarningBufferL@1055602 : Text;
      CounterL@1055600 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      // @ Function checks for duplicated lines on documents with type Order.
      // Start PA037942
      UserSetupGet;
      CASE UserSetupG."Check For Lines Duplicate No." OF
        UserSetupG."Check For Lines Duplicate No."::" ":
          EXIT;
        UserSetupG."Check For Lines Duplicate No."::Warning,
        UserSetupG."Check For Lines Duplicate No."::Error:
          BEGIN
            PurchLineL.RESET;
            PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type","Document Type");
            PurchLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.","Document No.");
            PurchLineL.SETFILTER("Line No.",'<>%1',"Line No.");
            PurchLineL.SETRANGE(Type,Type);
            PurchLineL.SETRANGE("No.","No.");
            IF NOT PurchLineL.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
      // Start PA044975
              IF UserSetupG."Check For Lines Duplicate No." = UserSetupG."Check For Lines Duplicate No."::Error THEN
                ERROR(C_INC_DuplicateError,"Item Type","No.");
              IF NOT CONFIRM(C_INC_DuplicateWarning, FALSE, "Item Type", "No.") THEN
                ERROR('');
            END;
      // Start PA037942.48468
            AdditionalItemL.RESET;
            AdditionalItemL.SETRANGE("Additional Item No.","No.");
            CASE "Order Type" OF
              "Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases":
                AdditionalItemL.SETRANGE("Consider in Parts Purchases", TRUE);
              "Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases":
                AdditionalItemL.SETRANGE("Consider in Vehicle Purchases", TRUE);
              "Order Type"::Service:
                AdditionalItemL.SETRANGE("Consider in Service Purchases", TRUE);
            END;
      // Start EU.0053218
            IF AdditionalItemL.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
              IF UserSetupG."Check For Lines Duplicate No." = UserSetupG."Check For Lines Duplicate No."::Error THEN
                ERROR(C_INC_DuplicateErrorAddItem, Type, "No.");
              REPEAT
                CounterL += 1;
                AdditionalItemL.CALCFIELDS("Item Description");
                AddItemDuplicateWarningBufferL := AddItemDuplicateWarningBufferL + '\' +
                  STRSUBSTNO('%1. %2 %3', CounterL, AdditionalItemL."Item No.", AdditionalItemL."Item Description");
              UNTIL AdditionalItemL.NEXT = 0;
              IF NOT CONFIRM(STRSUBSTNO(C_INC_DuplicateWarningAddItem, Type, "No.", AddItemDuplicateWarningBufferL, '\\'),FALSE) THEN
                ERROR('');
            END;
      // Stop EU.0053218
      // Stop PA044975
          END;
      // Stop PA037942.48468
      END;
      // Stop PA037942
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckCodedPart@1109400023();

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CheckQuantityChangeWithReservationEntries@563602();
    VAR
      ReservEntryL@563602 : Record 337;
      ReservedQuantityReductionL@563600 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      // @ This function will check if a quantity change needs to correct in the related reservation entries the reserved quantities.
      // Start EU.0005636
      ReservMgtG.InitFilterAndSortingLookupFrom(ReservEntryL, TRUE);
      ReservMgtG.PurchLineFilterReservFrom(ReservEntryL, Rec);
      IF ReservEntryL.ISEMPTY THEN
        VALIDATE("Reserved Qty. (Base)", 0)
      ELSE BEGIN
        ReservEntryL.CALCSUMS(Quantity);
        ReservedQuantityReductionL := ReservEntryL.Quantity - "Outstanding Qty. (Base)";
        IF ReservedQuantityReductionL <= 0 THEN
          EXIT;
        IF ReservEntryL.Quantity = 1 THEN BEGIN
          IF NOT CONFIRM(C_Quest_NewQuantityIsBelowExistingReservation, FALSE, ReservedQuantityReductionL) THEN
            ERROR('');
        END ELSE
          IF NOT CONFIRM(C_Quest_NewQuantityIsBelowExistingReservations, FALSE, ReservEntryL.Quantity, ReservedQuantityReductionL) THEN
            ERROR('');
        MODIFY;
        ReservMgtG.ReduceQuantityInReservFor(ReservEntryL, ReservedQuantityReductionL);
        GET("Document Type", "Document No.", "Line No.");
      END;
      // Stop EU.0005636
    END;

    PROCEDURE MarkRecordsFromRetShipment@1109400012(VAR ItemLedgEntryP@1109400000 : Record 32) : Boolean;
    VAR
      ItemLedgEntryL@1109400001 : Record 32;
      RecordsFromRetShipFoundL@1109400002 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // @ Marks records from Return Shipment Lines.
      // @ param ItemLedgEntryP - Record Item Ledger Entry ByVAR
      // @ retval - Boolean

      // Start PA041662.73195
      IF NOT ItemLedgEntryP.FINDSET THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      REPEAT
        ItemLedgEntryP.MARK(TRUE);
      UNTIL ItemLedgEntry.NEXT = 0;

      ItemLedgEntryL.COPY(ItemLedgEntryP);
      ItemLedgEntryL.SETRANGE(Open, FALSE);
      ItemLedgEntryL.SETRANGE(Positive, FALSE);
      ItemLedgEntryL.SETFILTER("Applies-to Entry", '<>%1', 0);
      IF ItemLedgEntryL.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          IF ABS(ItemLedgEntryL.Quantity) > ABS(ItemLedgEntryL."Invoiced Quantity") THEN
            IF ItemLedgEntryP.GET(ItemLedgEntryL."Applies-to Entry") THEN BEGIN
              RecordsFromRetShipFoundL := TRUE;
              ItemLedgEntryP.MARK(TRUE);
            END;
        UNTIL ItemLedgEntryL.NEXT = 0;
      EXIT(RecordsFromRetShipFoundL);
      // Stop PA041662.73195
    END;

    PROCEDURE CopyEmissiontoSalesLine@1109400014(FieldIdP@1109400000 : Integer);
    VAR
      SalesLineL@1109400001 : Record 37;
    BEGIN

              SalesLineL."Emission Test Procedure" := "Emission Test Procedure";

              SalesLineL."Cruising Range" := "Cruising Range";
      // Stop PA042665.860848
            FIELDNO("Combined Consumption"):
              SalesLineL."Combined Consumption" := "Combined Consumption";
          END;
          SalesLineL.MODIFY;
        UNTIL SalesLineL.NEXT = 0;
      // Stop PA042665
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckVehTradeIn@1109400016() : Boolean;
    VAR
      SalesTradeInL@1109400000 : Record 5025442;
      PostedSalesTradeInL@1109400001 : Record 5025443;
    BEGIN
      // @ This function is used to check if the Vehicle is Trade-In
      // @ retval - Boolean

      // Start PA041187.90233
      SalesTradeInL.RESET;

      IF PostedSalesTradeInL.COUNT MOD 2 <> 0 THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);
      EXIT(FALSE);
      // Stop PA041187.90233
    END;

    PROCEDURE CreateTempReplChain@1055604(ItemNoP@1055600 : Code[20];ChainNoP@1055601 : Integer);

        ;
      // Stop PA044817
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckItemReplcmnt@1055608();
    VAR
      CurrItemReplL@1055600 : Record 5028701;
      CurrItemRepl2L@1055603 : Record 5028701;
      ReplChainL@1055601 : Record 5028707;
      ReplChain2L@1055602 : Record 5028707;
    BEGIN
      // @ This function searches, according to Item Replacement Status, for uncomplete replacements in
      // @ Current Item Replacement table.

      // Start PA044817
      IF Item."Replacement Status" = Item."Replacement Status"::"Will be replaced" THEN BEGIN
        CurrItemReplL.RESET;
        CurrItemReplL.SETRANGE("Old Item No.", "No.");
        IF CurrItemReplL.FINDSET THEN
          // Handle N to 1 future replacements
          IF CurrItemReplL."N:1 Replacement" THEN BEGIN
            // Found the first of the line
            IF CurrItemReplL."Attached to Replacement No." = 0 THEN BEGIN
              CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemReplL."Old Item No.",1);
              CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemReplL."New Item No.",1);
              // Search for the attached
              CurrItemRepl2L.RESET;
              CurrItemRepl2L.SETCURRENTKEY("Attached to Replacement No.");
              CurrItemRepl2L.SETRANGE("Attached to Replacement No.", CurrItemReplL."Replacement No.");
              IF CurrItemRepl2L.FINDSET THEN
                REPEAT
                  CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemRepl2L."Old Item No.",1);
                UNTIL CurrItemRepl2L.NEXT = 0;
            END ELSE BEGIN
              // Found an attached replacement, so find the first in line
              CurrItemRepl2L.RESET;
              CurrItemRepl2L.SETRANGE("Replacement No.", CurrItemReplL."Attached to Replacement No.");
              IF CurrItemRepl2L.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemRepl2L."Old Item No.",1);
                CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemRepl2L."New Item No.",1);
              END;
              // Search for the attached
              CurrItemRepl2L.RESET;
              CurrItemRepl2L.SETRANGE("Attached to Replacement No.", CurrItemReplL."Attached to Replacement No.");
              IF CurrItemRepl2L.FINDSET THEN
                REPEAT
                  CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemRepl2L."Old Item No.",1);
                UNTIL CurrItemRepl2L.NEXT = 0;
            END;

          END ELSE BEGIN
            // This may handle both 1:1 or 1:N current replacements
            REPEAT
              CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemReplL."Old Item No.",1);
              CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemReplL."New Item No.",1);
            UNTIL CurrItemReplL.NEXT = 0;
          END;
      END ELSE
        IF Item."Replacement Status" = Item."Replacement Status"::"Replacement Item" THEN BEGIN
          CurrItemReplL.RESET;
          CurrItemReplL.SETRANGE("New Item No.", "No.");
          IF CurrItemReplL.FINDSET THEN
            // Handle 1 to N future replacements
            IF CurrItemReplL."1:N Replacement" THEN BEGIN
              // Found the first of the line
              IF CurrItemReplL."Attached to Replacement No." = 0 THEN BEGIN
                CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemReplL."Old Item No.",1);
                CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemReplL."New Item No.",1);
                // Search for the attached
                CurrItemRepl2L.RESET;
                CurrItemRepl2L.SETCURRENTKEY("Attached to Replacement No.");
                CurrItemRepl2L.SETRANGE("Attached to Replacement No.", CurrItemReplL."Replacement No.");
                IF CurrItemRepl2L.FINDSET THEN
                  REPEAT
                    CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemRepl2L."New Item No.",1);
                  UNTIL CurrItemRepl2L.NEXT = 0;
              END ELSE BEGIN
                // Found an attached replacement, so find the first in line
                CurrItemRepl2L.RESET;
                CurrItemRepl2L.SETRANGE("Replacement No.", CurrItemReplL."Attached to Replacement No.");
                IF CurrItemRepl2L.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                  CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemRepl2L."Old Item No.",1);
                  CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemRepl2L."New Item No.",1);
                END;
                // Search for the attached
                CurrItemRepl2L.RESET;
                CurrItemRepl2L.SETRANGE("Attached to Replacement No.", CurrItemReplL."Attached to Replacement No.");
                IF CurrItemRepl2L.FINDSET THEN
                  REPEAT
                    CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemRepl2L."New Item No.",1);
                  UNTIL CurrItemRepl2L.NEXT = 0;
              END;
            END ELSE BEGIN
              // This may handle both 1:1 or N:1 current replacements
              REPEAT
                CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemReplL."Old Item No.",1);
                CreateTempReplChain(CurrItemReplL."New Item No.",1);
              UNTIL CurrItemReplL.NEXT = 0;
            END;
        END;
      // Stop PA044817
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE ConfirmItemReplacement@4729400();
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0047294
      CASE Item."Replacement Status" OF
        Item."Replacement Status"::"Has been replaced":
          ShowReplcmtG := CONFIRM(C_INC039, TRUE, "No.");
        Item."Replacement Status"::"Replacement Item":
          ShowReplcmtG := CONFIRM(C_INC037, TRUE, "No.");
        Item."Replacement Status"::"Will be replaced":
          ShowReplcmtG := CONFIRM(C_INC038, TRUE, "No.");
      END;
      // Stop EU.0047294
    END;

    PROCEDURE NoStatusUpdate@1000000000(NoStatusChangeP@1000000000 : Boolean);
    BEGIN
      // @ Function Not to update the status
      // @ if it comes from CopyDocument
      // @ param NoStatusChangeP : Boolean
      // Start EU.0041404
      NoStatusChangeG := NoStatusChangeP;
      // Stop EU.0041404
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE ReValidateItemNoField@2542300(NewItemNoP@2542301 : Code[20]) : Boolean;
    VAR
      OldItemL@2542300 : Record 27;
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0025423
      IF "No." = NewItemNoP THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      OldItemL.GET("No.");
      WithoutReplcmtWindowG := TRUE;
      VALIDATE("No.", NewItemNoP);
      WithoutReplcmtWindowG := FALSE;
      EXIT(TRUE);
      // Stop EU.0025423
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdatePurchaseLineGlobalDim@564202(VAR PurchLineP@564200 : Record 39;ValidateP@564201 : Boolean);
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0005642
      GlobalDimMgtG.ValidateDocLineDimensions(PurchLineP, GlobalDimCodeG);
      IF ValidateP THEN BEGIN
        PurchLineP.VALIDATE("Shortcut Dimension 1 Code", GlobalDimCodeG[1]);
        PurchLineP.VALIDATE("Shortcut Dimension 2 Code", GlobalDimCodeG[2]);
      END ELSE BEGIN
        PurchLineP."Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" := GlobalDimCodeG[1];
        PurchLineP."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code" := GlobalDimCodeG[2];
      END;
      // Stop EU.0005642
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE AllowManualGlobalDimChange@564200() : Boolean;
    VAR
      AllowChangeL@564200 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // @ This function checks if manual change of Global Dimensions (Make Code or Department Code) is allowed based on Type and Item Type in 'Purchase Line'
      // Start EU.0005642
      CASE TRUE OF
        (CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO("Shortcut Dimension 1 Code")) AND ("Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" <> xRec."Shortcut Dimension 1 Code"):
          CASE Type OF
            Type::"Charge (Item)":
              AllowChangeL := FALSE;
            Type::Item,
            Type::"Fixed Asset":
              AllowChangeL := TRUE;
            Type::"Account (G/L)":
              IF GlobalDimMgtG.AllowDimChange(Rec) THEN
                AllowChangeL := TRUE;
          END;
        (CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO("Shortcut Dimension 2 Code")) AND ("Shortcut Dimension 2 Code" <> xRec."Shortcut Dimension 2 Code"):
          CASE Type OF
            Type::Item:
              CASE "Item Type" OF
                "Item Type"::Item,
                "Item Type"::Vehicle:
                  AllowChangeL := FALSE;
                "Item Type"::"Veh. Transfer":
                  AllowChangeL := TRUE;
              END;
            Type::"Charge (Item)":
              AllowChangeL := FALSE;
            Type::"Fixed Asset":
              AllowChangeL := TRUE;
            Type::"Account (G/L)":
              IF GlobalDimMgtG.AllowDimChange(Rec) THEN
                AllowChangeL := TRUE;
          END;
        ELSE
          AllowChangeL := TRUE;
      END;
      EXIT(AllowChangeL);
      // Stop EU.0005642
    END;
